 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa 
  
   Buddhābadānaṃ 
  
     Tathāgataṃ jetavane vasantaṃ apucchi vedehamuni nataṅgo 
  Sabbaññabuddhā kira nāma honti bhavanti te hetuhi kehi vira     
  
   Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī ānanandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena 
 Ye pubba   buddhesu katādhikārā aladdhamokkha jinasāsanesu 
  
   Teneva   sambodhimukhena dhīrā ajjhāsayenāpi mahābalena 
 Paññāya teje sutikkhapaññā sabaññubhavaṃ anupāpuṇanti 
  
   Ahampi pubbabuddhesu buddhattamabhipatthayiṃ 
 Manasāyeva hutvāna dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā 
  
   Atha buddhāpadānāni suṇātha suddhamānasā   
 Tiṃsapāramisampuṇṇā dhammarājā asaṅkhiyā 
  
   Sambodhiṃ buddhaseṭṭhānaṃ sasaṅghe lokatāyake 
 Dasaṅguli namassitvā sirasā abivādayiṃ   
  
   Yāvatā buddhakhettesu ratanā vijjantasaṅkhiyā 
 Ākāsaṭṭhā ca bhummaṭṭhā manasā sabbamāhariṃ   
  
   Ādito paṭhāya imā canasso gāthāyo     potthakesu santi   Catutthagāthāya dutiyadedhā 
 ce pañcamagāthāya paṭhamandho ca syāmapotthake na santi   Dhīrā se   Sabba se   
 Tenidha se   Abhivādaye se   Māhare     se 
  
                 
  
   Tattha rūpiyabhumiyaṃ pāsādaṃ māpayiṃ   ahaṃ 
 Nekabhummaṃ   ratanamayaṃ ubbiddhaṃ nabhamuggataṃ 
  
   Vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ suvibhatta ṃmahārahaṃ 
 Kanakāmayasaṅghāṭaṃ   toraṇacchattamaṇḍitaṃ   
  
    Paṭhamā veḷuriyā bhumi vimalābbhasamā subhā 
 Nalīni   jalajākiṇaṇavarakañcanabhumiyā 
  
    Pavāḷaṃsā   pavāḷavaṇaṇā kāci lohitakā subhā 
 Indagopakavaṇṇāhā bhumi obhāsati disā 
  
    Suvibhattā gharamukhā niyyuhā sīhapañajarā 
 Caturo vedikā jālagandhāvela   manoramā 
  
    Nīlā pītā lobhitā odātā suddhakāḷakā 
 Kūṭāgāravarūpetā satatratanabhusitā   
  
                 
  
    Olokamayā  padumā vāḷa   vihagasobhitā 
 Nakkhattatārakākiṇṇā candasuriyehi    maṇḍitā 
  
    Hemajālena sañachannā soṇṇa   kiṅkiṇikāyutā 
 Vātavegena kujanti soṇṇamālā manoramā 
  
    Mañjeṭṭhakaṃ lohitakaṃ pitakaṃ haripiñjaraṃ 
 Nānāraṅgehi suppitaṃ ussitaddhajamāliniṃ 
  
    Nānā bahu nekasatā phaḷikā rajatāmayā 
 Maṇimayā lohitaṅkā masāragallamayā tathā 
 Kākādavakaniñcittā saṇhakāsikasatthatā 
  
    Kambalā dukulā cinā patatuṇṇā paṇḍupāvurā 
 Vividhattharaṇaṃ    sabbaṃ manasā paññapesahaṃ    
  
    Tāsu tāsveva bhumisu ratanakuṭalaṅkatā 
 Maṇiverācanā ukkā dhārayantā sutiṭṭhare 
  
    Sobhanti esikāthambhā subhā kañcanatoraṇā 
 Jamebānadā sāramayā atho rajatamayāpi ca 
  
    Kenā sandhi    suvibhattā kavāṭaggaḷacittitā 
 Ubhato puṇṇaghaṭānekā padumuppalaṃyutā 
  
    Atite sababbuddhe ca sasaṃghe lokanāyake 
 Pakativaṇaṇarūpena nimminitvā sasāvake 
  
   Māpaye     se   Kekabhumiṃ       Saṅghātaṃ ma   Kontacchattehi maṇḍitaṃ ma 
   Nalina ma   Pavāḷaṃsa       Gandhavelā       Vibhusitā       Olokayamayā se 
    Candasurehi ma se    Vivittattharaṇaṃ    Paññapemahaṃ se        Nekāsanti a mu 
 se 
  
                 
  
    Tena dvārena pavisitvā sabbe buddhā sasāvakā 
 Sabbasovaṇṇaye  pīṭhe nisinnā ariyamaṇḍalā 
  
    Ye ca etarahi atthi buddhā loke anuttarā 
 Atitā   vatatamānā ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāruhuṃ   
  
    Paccekakhuddhe nekasate sayambhu aparājite 
 Atite vattamāne   ca bhavanaṃ sabbe samāruhuṃ  
  
    Kapparukkhā bahu atthi ye dibbā ye ca mānusā 
 Sabbaṃ dussaṃ samāhatvā acchādemi   ticivarā 
  
    Khajjaṃ bhojjaṃ sāyaniyaṃ sampannaṃ   pānabhojanaṃ 
 Maṇimaye pubhe patte sampuretvā adāsasahaṃ 
  
    Dibbacakkhusamā hutvā maṭṭhacivarasaṃyutā    
 Madhunā sakkharā ceva telena madhuphāṇitā 
  
    Tappitā paramannena sabbe te ariyamaṇḍalā 
                 
 Ratanāgabbhaṃ pavisitvā kesariva guhāsayā 
  
    Mahārahamhi sayane sīhaseyyamakappayuṃ 
 Sampajānā samuḍhāya sayane pallaṅkamābhujuṃ 
 Gocaraṃ sabbabuddhānaṃ jhānaratisamappitā 
  
    Aññe dhammāni desenti aññe kiḷanti indhiyā 
 Aññe abhiññā appenti abhiññāvasibhāvitā 
 Vikubbanā vikubbanti aññe nekasahassiyo   
  
    Buddhāpi buddhe pucchanti visayaṃ sabbaññumālayaṃ 
 Gambhiraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ paññāya vinikhujjhare 
  
    Sāvakā buddhe pucchanti buddhā pucchanti sāvake 
 Aññamaññaṃ ca pucchanti   aññoññaṃ    byākaronti te 
  
    Buddhā paccekabuddhā ca sāvakā paricārakā 
 Evaṃ sakāya ratiyā    pāsāde bhiramanti te 
  
    Chattā tiṭṭhantu ratanā kañcanāvelapantikā   
 Muttājālaparikkhittā sabbe    dhārentu    matthake 
  
    Bhavantu ceḷavitānā soṇṇatārakacitatinā 
 Vicittamālyavitānā    sabbe dhārentu matthake 
  
    Vitatā mālyadāmehi gandhadāmehi sobhitā 
 Dussadāmehi parikiṇṇā ratanadāmavibhusitā 
  
   Atite ma   Samāhariṃ mu a   Cattamānā ma   Samāhariṃ mu a   Acchādesiṃ       
 Sabbanta se ma   Maṭhā se ma a   Anekasatasahassiyo se aññeneka sahassiyo     se    
 Evaṃ ratisurammānā     se    Suvaṇṇajālābhi saṃyuttaṃ rajatajālamaṇihi ca        
 Muttajālaparikkhittaṃ chattaṃ        Dhārenti se    Vicittā malya         soṇṇamaye 
  aṭṭhakathā  
  
                 
  
    Pupphābhikiṇṇā sucittā surabhigandhudhupitā    
 Gandhapañcaṅgulikatā   hemacchadanachāditā   
  
    Catuddisā pokkharañño padumuppalasanthatā 
 Sovaṇṇarūpā khāyantu padumareṇurajaggatā 
  
    Pupphanatu pādapā sabbe pāsādasasa samantato 
 Sayaṃ ca pupphā ñcitvā gantvā   bhavanamokiruṃ   
  
    Sikhino tattha naccantu dibbahaṃsā pakujare 
 Karavikā ca gāyantu dijasaṃghā samantato 
  
    Bheriyo sabbā vajjantu viṇā sabbā ravantu   tā 
 Sabbā saṃgini vattantu pāsādassa samantato 
  
                 
  
    Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi cakkavāḷe tato pare 
 Mahantā jotisampannā acchiddā ratanāmāya 
  
    Niṭṭhantu soṇṇapalalaṅkā diparukkhā jalantu te 
 Bhavantu ekapajjotā dasasahassiparamparā 
  
    Gaṇikā lāsikā ceva naccantu accharāgaṇā 
 Nānāraṅgā padissantu pāsādassa samantato 
  
    Dumagge pabbatagge vā sinerugirimuddhani 
 Ussāpemi dhajaṃ sabbaṃ vicittaṃ pañcavaṇṇikaṃ 
  
    Narā nāgā ca gandhabbā sabbe devā apentu te 
 Namassantā pañajalikā pāsādaṃ parivārayuṃ 
  
    Yaṃ kiñci kusalaṃ kammaṃ kattabbaṃ kiriyaṃ mama 
 Kāyena vācā manasā tidase sukataṃ kataṃ 
  
    Ye sattā saññino atthi ye ca sattā asaññino 
 Kataṃ puññaphalaṃ mayhaṃ sabbe bhāgi bhavantu te 
  
    Yesaṃ kataṃ suviditaṃ dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayā 
 Ye ca tasmiṃ na jānanti devā gananvā nivedayuṃ 
  
    Sababalokambhi   ye sattā jivantāhārahetukā 
 Manuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ labhantu mama tejasā   
  
    Manasā dānaṃ māya dinnaṃ manasā pāsādamāvahiṃ    
 Pujitā sabbasambuddhā paccekā jinasāvakā 
  
    Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagañachahaṃ 
  
    Ave bhave pajānāmi devatte atha mānuse 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi manasā patthanāphalaṃ 
  
   Bhusitā se   Gulaṅkitā se   Chadanamālikā se   Gandhā       Motaruṃ se   Rasantu 
 ma   Sabbe         Cetasā     se   Māpayiṃ se 
  
                  
  
    Devānaṃ adhiko homi bhavāmi manujādhipo 
 Rūpalakkhaṇasampanno paññāya asamo bhave 
  
    Bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭhaṃ ratanañca anappakaṃ 
 Nānāvidhāni   vatthāni nabhā khippaṃ upenti maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā   pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi dibbā bhakkhā upenati maṃ   
  
    Pathavyā  pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi ratanā sabba upenati maṃ 
  
                 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba gandhā upenati maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba yānā upenati maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbā mālā upenati maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi alaṅkārā upenati maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabbā kaññāupenati maṃ 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi upenati madhusakkharā 
  
    Pathavyā pabbate ceva ākāse udake vane 
 Yaṃ yaṃ hatthaṃ pasāremi sabba khajjā upenati maṃ 
  
    Adhane addhikajane yācake ca pathāvino 
 Dadāmahaṃ   dānavaraṃ sambodhivarapattiyā 
  
    Nādento pabbataṃ selaṃ gajjento   bahalaṃ giriṃ 
 Sadevalokaṃ hāsento   buddho loke bhavāmahaṃ 
  
    Disā dasavidhā loke yāyato natthi antakaṃ 
 Tasmiñca disābhāgambhi buddhakkhettā   asaṅkhiyā 
  
    Pabhā pakittinā mayhaṃ yamakā raṃsivāhanā 
 Etthantare raṃsijālaṃ āloko vipulo bhave 
  
    Etatake lokadhātumbhi sabbe passantu maṃ janā 
 Sabbe ca sumanā hontu sabbe maṃ anuvattare   
  Sabbe maṃ anuvattanti yāva brahmanivesanaṃ    
  
    Vissaṭṭha   madhunādena amataṃ bherimāhaniṃ   
 Ethentare janā sabbe suṇantu madhuraṃ giraṃ 
  
    Dhammameghe pavassanne sabbe hontu anāsavā 
 Yettha pacchimakā sattā sotāpannā bhavantu te 
  
    Datvā dātabbakaṃ dānaṃ sīlaṃ puretvasesato 
 Nekkhamme pāramiṃ gantvā    patto sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
                 
  
    Paṇḍite paripucchitvā katvā viriyamuttamaṃ 
 Khantiyā pāramiṃ gantvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
    Katvā daḷhamadhiṭṭhānaṃ    puretvā saccapāramiṃ    
 Mettāya pāramiṃ gantvā patetā sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
    Lābhālābhe sukhe sukkhe sammāne cāvamānane   
 Sabbattha samako hutvā patto sambodhimuttamaṃ 
  
   Vividhāni ca ma se   Puthavyā       Me       Yammekataṃ       Gacchento ma 
   Sadevakaṃ hāsayanto ma se   Khette ma   Visiṭṭha       Māhane     se    Patvā 
        Saccamadhiṭana        Saccapārami puriya ma se    Ca vimānane ma       
     potthekesu dissati   Addhacandakatihi anakariko bhāgo marammapotthakesu ceva 
 seluttarārāmapotthake ca dissati 
  
                  
  
    Kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā viriyañcāpi   khemato 
 Āraddhaviriyā hotha esā buddhānusāsanī 
  
    Vivādaṃ bhayato disvā avivādañca khemato 
 Samaggā sakhilā hotha esā buddhānusāsani 
  
    Pamādaṃ bhayato disvā appamādaṃ ca khemato 
 Bhavethaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ esā buddhānusāsani 
  
    Samāgatā bahu buddhā arahantā ca sabbaso 
 Sambuddhe arahante ca vandamānā namassatha 
  
    Evaṃ acintiyā buddhā buddhadhammā acintiyā 
 Acintiyesu pasannānaṃ vipāko hoti acintiyo 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano buddacariyaṃ   sambhāvayamāna beddhāpadāniyaṃ nāma 
 dhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthāni 
  
   Buddhāpadānaṃ samantaṃ   
  
  
                 
  
   Pacceka buddhāpadānaṃ 
  
 Atha paccekkhuddhāpadānaṃ suṇātha 
  
    Tathāgataṃ jevane vasantaṃ apucchi vedehamuni nataṅgo 
  Paccekabuddhā kira nāma honti bhavanti te hetuhi kehi vīra  
  
    Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesī ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena 
 Ye pubbabuddhesu   katādhikārā aladdhamokkhā jinasāsanesu 
    Teneva saṃvegamukhena dhīrā vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññā 
 Ārammaṇenāpi paritatakena pacekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti 
  
    Sabbamhi lokamhi mamaṃ ṭhapetvā paccekabuddhehi samova natthi 
 Tesaṃ imaṃ vaṇaṇapadesamattaṃ vakkhāmahaṃ sādhu mahāmuninaṃ 
  
    Sayameva buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ   sādhuni vākyāni madhuṃva   khuddaṃ 
 Anuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayanatā suṇātha sabbesu pasannacittā 
  
    Paccekabuddhānaṃ samāgatānaṃ   paramparavyākaraṇāni yāni 
 Ādīnavo yañca virāgavatthu yathā ca bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu 
  
   Akosajjaṃ ca se   Buddhacaritaṃ ma   Sabbabuddhesu     mase 
   Mahesinaṃ ma   Madhuñca     madhuva ma   Sahagatānaṃ ma 
  
                 
                  
  
    Saṃrāgavatthusu   virāgasaññi rattambhi lokambhi virattacittā 
 Hitvā papañce   vijiya endināni   tatheva   bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu 
  
    Sabbesu bhutesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ 
 Mettena cittena hitānukampi eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo  
  
    Sabbesu bhutesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññatarampi tesaṃ 
 Namettena cittena hitānukampi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Saṃsaggajātassa bhavanti senahā senahanvayaṃ dukkhamidaṃ pahoti 
 Ādinaṃ senahajaṃ pekkhamāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Mitte subhajje anukampamāno hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibaddhacitto 
 Etaṃ bhayaṃ panthave pakkhemāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Vaṃso visālova yathā visanettā puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā 
 Vaṃsakaḷirova asajjamāno eko care khagagavisāṇakappo 
  
    Migo araññambhi yathā abaddho ye nicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāya 
 Viññu naro seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko vare khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Āmantanā hoti sabāyamajjhe va ca   ṭhāne gamane cārikāya 
 Anabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Khiḍḍhā rati hoti sahāyamajjhe puttesu pemaṃ vipulañca hoti 
                 
 Piyavippayogaṃ   vijigucchamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Cātuddiso appaṭigho ca hoti santussamāno itaritarena 
 Parissayānaṃ sabhitā achambhi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
   Sarāgavatthūsu   ma se   Papañcaṃ       Jita endanāni       
   Tattheva      ayaṃ gāthā marammapotthake ca suttanipāte ca na vajjati 
   Vāse mu a   Piyababiyogaṃ ma 
  
                  
  
    Dussaṅgahā pabbajitāpi eke atho gahaṭṭhā gharamāvasantā 
 Apposukko paraputtesu hutvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
    Oropayitvā gibhibyañajanāni saṃsinapatto   yatā koviḷāro 
 Chenvāna viro   gigibandhanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃvaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhiraṃ 
 Abhibhuyya sabbāni parisasyāni careyya tenattamano satimā 
  
     No ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃvaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhiraṃ 
 Rājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya eko care mātaṅga raññeva nāgo   
  
     Addhā pasaṃsāma sabhāyasampadaṃ seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sabhāyā 
 Ete aladdhā anavajjabhoja eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Disvā suvaṇaṇasasa pabhassarāni kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāni 
 Saṃghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Evaṃ dutiyena sabhā mamassa vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā ca 
 Etaṃ bhayaṃ āyatiṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
                  
  
     Kāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā virūparūpena mathetti cittaṃ 
 Ādinavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Īti ca gaṇḍo ca upadadavo ca rogo ca sallañca bhañcametaṃ 
 Etaṃ bhayaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Sitañca aṇhañca khudaṃ pipāsaṃ vātātape ḍaṃsasiriṃsape ca 
 Sabbāni petāni abhibbhavitvā   eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
   Saṃchinnapatto mu a   Dhīro se   Khaggavisāṇakappo su ni 
   Abhisambhavitva su ni 
  
                  
  
     Nāgova yuthāni vivajjayitvā saṃjātakhandho padumi uḷāro 
 Yathābhirantaṃ  viharaṃ   araññe eko care khaggavisāṇakapepā 
  
     Aṭṭhāna taṃ saṅgaṇikāratassa yaṃ phassaye sāmayikaṃ vimutatiṃ 
 Ādiccabandhussa vaco tisamma eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Diṭṭhivisukāni upātivatetā patto niyāmaṃ paṭiladdhamaggo 
 Uppannañāṇemhi anaññanyo eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Tillolupo nikkuho nippipāso nimmakkha niddhantakasāvamoho 
 Nirāsayo   sabbaloke bhavitvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Pāpaṃ sahāyaṃ pirivajjayetha anatthadassiṃ visame niviṭṭaṃ 
 Sayaṃ   na seve pasutaṃ pamattaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Bahussutaṃ dhammadharaṃ bhajetha mittaṃ uḷāraṃ paṭibhāṇavantaṃ 
                  
 Aññāya atthāni vineyya kaṃkhaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Khiḍḍhaṃ ratiṃ kāmasukhañca loke analaṅkaritvā anapekkhamano 
 Vibhusanaṭṭhānā cirito saccavādi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Puttañca dāraṃ pitarañca mātaraṃ dhanāni dhaññāni ca khandhavāni 
 Hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni   eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Saṅgo eso parittaṃ ettha sobyaṃ appassādo dukkhamevettha bhiyyo 
 Gaho   eso iti ñatvā matimā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni jālaṃ va bhotvā salilambhucārī 
 Aggiva daḍḍhaṃ anivattamāno eko care khagagavisāṇakappo 
  
     Okkhittacakkhu na ca pādalolo guttindiyo rakkhitamānasāno 
 Anavassuto apariḍayhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
   Yathābhirataṃ    Vihare su ni   Nimmakkho se     su ni   Nirāsaṃso ma se   Passaṃ 
 se   Yatoṭṭhitāni se   Gāḷho ma kaṇḍo     kaḍḍho se gaḷo su ni   Hitvā ma se jālaṃ 
 pahitvā     
  
                  
  
     Ohārayitvā   giyibyañajanāni saṃchinnapatto yathā pārichatto 
 Kāsāyavattho abhinikkhamitvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Rasesu gedhaṃ akaraṃ alolo anaññaposi sapadānacārī 
 Kule kule appaṭibaddhacitto eko care khagagavisāṇakappo 
     Pahāya pañcāvaraṇāni cetaso upakkilese byapanujja sabbe 
 Anisasito chejja sinehadosaṃ   eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
                  
  
     Vipiṭṭhi katvāna sukhaṃ ca dukkhaṃ   pubebava ca somana   domanassaṃ   
 Laddhānupekkhaṃ samathaṃ visuddhaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Āraddhavirayo   paramatthapattiyā alinacitto akusitavutti 
 Daḷhanikkamo thāmabaluppanno eko care khagagavisāṇakappo 
  
     Paṭisallānaṃ   jhānamariñcamāno   dhammesu niccaṃ anudhammacāri 
 Ādinavaṃ sammasitā bhavesu eko care khagagavisāṇakappo 
  
     Taṇhakkhayaṃ patthayaṃ appamatto aneḷamugo sutavā satimā 
 Saṅkhātadhammo niyato padhānavā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Sīhova saddesu asantasanto vātova jālambhi asajjamāno 
 Padumaṃva toyena alippamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Sīho yathā dāṭhabali pasayha rājā migānaṃ abhibhuyyacāri 
 Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Metaṃ upekkhaṃ karuṇaṃ vimuttiṃ āsevamāno muditañca kāle 
 Sabbena lokena virujjhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃ sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni 
 Asantasaṃ jāvitasaṅkhayambhi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
   Ohāpayitvā ma   Chetvā snehapadosaṃ       Dukkhaṃ ca       Somanassa       
 se su ni   Āraddhaviro ma   Paṭisallina ma paṭisallāna       Jhānapariccamāno ma 
  
                  
                  
  
     Bhajanti sevanti ca kāraṇatthā nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā 
 Anattatthapaññā asuci manussā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Visuddhasīlā suvisuddhapaññā samābhitā jāgariyānuyuttā 
 Vipassakā dhammavisesadassi maggaṅgabojjhaṅgagate vijaññā 
  
     Suññatappaṇihinañcānimittaṃ   āsevayitvā jinasāsanambhi 
 Ye sāvakatataṃ na vajanti dhīrā bhavanti paccekajinā sayambhu 
  
     Mahantadhammā bahudhammakāyā cittissarā sabbadukkhoghatiṇṇā 
 Udaggacittā paramatthadassi sīhopamā khaggavisāṇakappo 
  
     Santindriyā santamanā samādhi paccattagambhiramatappacārā   
 Dipā paratthaṃ idha vijjalantā paccekabuddhā sattaccitāme   
  
     Pahīṇasabbāvaraṇā janindā lokappadīpā ghanakañcanābhā 
 Nissaṃsayaṃ lokasudakkhiṇeyyā paccekabuddhā sattaccitāme   
  
     Paccekabuddhānaṃ subhāsitāni caranti lokamhi sadevakambhi 
 Sutvā tathā ye na karonti bālā caranti dukkhesu punappunaṃ te 
  
     Paccekabuddhānaṃ subhāsitāni madhuṃ yathā buddamavassavanataṃ   
 Sutvā tathā ye paṭipattiyuttā bhavanti te saccadasā sapañña 
  
                  
  
     Paccekabudehi jinehi vuttā   gāthā   uḷārā abhinikkhamitvā 
 Tā sakyasihena naruttamena pakāsitā dhammavijānanatthaṃ 
  
     Lokānukampāya imāni tesaṃ paccekabuddhāna vikubbitāni 
 Saṃvegā saṅgamati   mativaḍḍhanatthaṃ sayambhusihena pakāsitāni 
   Pacecaka buddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ   
  
   Paññappaṇidhiñca tathānimittaṃ     suññappanidhiṃ   ma   Paccantasattesu 
 satippacārā     se   Satataṃ hitā me Ma     se   Satataṃ hitā me mase   Khuddamiva 
       Bhāsitā ma   Kathā ma se   Saṃvegasaṅgaṃmati mu a 
  
                  
                  
  
   Atha therāpadānaṃ suṇātha 
  
    Sāriputtattherāpadānaṃ  
  
     Himavattasasa avidūre lambako nāma pabbato 
 Assamo sukato mayahaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā 
  
     Uttānakulā nadikā supatitthā manoramā 
 Susuddha   pulinākiṇṇā avidūre mamassamā 
  
     Asakkharā apabbhārā sādu appaṭigandhikā 
 Sandati nadikā tattha sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
     Kumbhilā makarā cettha suṃsumārā ca kacchapā 
 Caranti nadiyā   tattha sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
     Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā   mucaṃrohitā 
 Maggurā   papatāyantā   sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
     Ubhokulesu nadiyā pupphino phalino dumā 
 Ubhato abhilambantā sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
     Ambā sālā ca   tilakā pāṭali sinduvārakā   
 Dibbagandhaṃ   sampavantipphitā mama asasame 
  
     Campakā salalā nīpā   nāgapunnāgaketakā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ   sampavantipphitā mama asasame 
  
     Atimuttā asokā ca bhaginimālā ca pupphitā 
 Aṅkolā bimbijālā    ca pupphitā mama asasame 
  
                  
  
     Keṭakā    kandali ceva godhukā    tiṇasulikā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ   sampavanti sobhayantā    mamasasmaṃ 
  
     Kaṇikārā kaṇṇikā    ca asanā ajjunā    bahu 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavanti sobhayantā    mamassamaṃ 
  
     Punnāgā giripunnāgā koviḷārā ca pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavanti sobhayantā    mamassamaṃ 
  
     Uddālakā ca kuṭajā kadambā vakulā    bahu 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavanti sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
     Āḷakā isimuggā ca kadali mātuluṅgiyo 
 Gandhodakena saṃvaddhā phalāni dhārayanti te 
  
     Aññe pupphanti padumā aññe jāyanti kesarī 
 Aññe opupphā padumā pupphitā taḷāke    sadā 
  
   Saṃsuddha       Sandati nadikā     se a   Balajā ma the jalajā       Maṅgurā    
   Ca patāyanti       Ambā kolakā       Sindhucārikā     a sindhacārikā ma se   
 Dibbāgandhā     a Se   Nimbā the    Bimbajālā ma    Ketakā        Kekhukā     
 se    Sampavannā sobhayanti ma se    Kaṇikā        Aṃjani     se ajjanā ma the 
 aṃjanā a    Sobhamānā        Bahulā ma    Tadā ma     se 
  
                  
  
     Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā niddhāvanti mulāliyo 
 Siṅghāṭakapattamākiṇṇā   sobhanti   taḷāke sadā 
  
     Nayitā ambagandhi ca uttālā   bandhujīvakā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavanti taghāke pupphitā   dasā   
  
     Piṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā muñaja   rohitā 
 Saṅgulā   maṅgurā   ceva vasanti taḷāke sadā 
  
     Kumbhilā suṃsumārā ca tantigāhā ca rakkhasā 
 Oguhā   ajaharaṃ   ca vasanti taḷāke sadā 
  
     Pārevatā ravihaṃsā cakkavākā nadivarā 
 Kokilā sukasāḷikā   upajivantitaṃ saraṃ 
  
     Kukutthakā kulirakā vane pokkharasātakā 
 Dindibhā suvapotā ca upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
                  
  
     Haṃsā kokañcā mayurā ca kokilā tamba cuḷākā 
 Pampakā    jīvaṃjivā ca upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Kosikā poṭṭhasisā ca kurarā    senakā bahu 
 Mahākālā ca sakuṇā upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Pasadā ca varāgā ca cākā    bheraṇḍakā    bahu 
 Rohiccā suggapotā    ca upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Sīha vyagghā ca dipi ca acchakokataracchakā 
 Tidhāpabhinnā mātaṅgā    upajivantitaṃ saraṃ 
  
     Kinnarā vānarā ceva atho pi vanakammikā 
 Cetā ca ludadakā ceva upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Tindukāni piyālāni madhukā kāsumārayo    
 Dhuvapphalāni    dhārenti avidūre mamassamā 
  
     Kosumbhā    salalā nīpā    sāduphalasamāyutā    
 Dhuvapphalāni dhārenti avidūre mamassamā 
  
     Haritakā āmalakā ambā jambuvibhīṭakā    
 Kolā bhallātakā billā    phalāni dhārayanti te 
  
     Āluvā ca kalambā ca biḷālitakkaḷāni    ca 
 Jivakā sutakā    ceva bahukā mama assame 
  
   Siṅghāṭi     se ma saṅghāṭi the a sipāṭi mu a   Sobhenti mu a sobhayanti       
 Utuḷahi     uttali mu a   Pupphitā taḷāke ma the   Saṅkulā     se   Maggurā ma the 
 a   Ogahā       Ajakārā mu a   Sāḷi ca     se sāḷikā ma the    Sampakā        
 Kururā the    Camarā ma the okā se    Gaṇḍakā ma the    Sukapotā ma the puggasa    
 Tidhappahinnā ma the    Madhukekā sumāriyo     the a    Dhuvaṃ mathe a    
 Kosambā ma the    Nimbā ma the    Sāraphala     se a    Vibhedakā ma the se    
 Belā ma the se bellā     a    Bilāni     takkolāni the    Sabhakā     saraṇā the 
  
                  
  
     Assamassāvidurambhi taḷākāsuṃ   sunimmitā 
 Acchodakā sitajalā supatitthā manoramā 
  
     Padumuppalasaṃcchannā puṇḍarikasamāyutā 
 Mandālakehi   saṃchannā dibbagandho pavāyati   
  
     Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampanne pupphite phalite vane 
 Sukate assame ramme viharāmi ahaṃ tadā   
  
     Sīlavā vatasampanno jhāyī jhānarato sadā 
 Pañcābhiññābalappatto   suruci nāma tāpaso 
  
     Catubbisasahassāni sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ 
 Sabbeva brāhmaṇā ete jātimanto yasassino 
  
     Lakkhaṇe itihase ca sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe 
 Padakā veyyākaraṇā sadamme   pāramiṃ gatā 
  
                  
  
     Uppātesu   nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā 
 Pathavyā bhumyantalikkhe   mama sisasā susikkhitā 
  
     Appicchā nipakā ete appāhārā alolupā 
 Lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
     Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samābhitā 
 Ākiñcaññaṃ patthayantā parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
     Abhiññāpāramippattā pettike gocare ratā 
 Antalikkhacarā dhīrā parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
     Saṃvutā chasu dvaresu anejā rakkhitindriyā 
 Asaṃsaṭa ca te dhīrā mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Pallaṅkena nisajjāya ṭhāna   vaṅkamanena ca 
 Vitināmenti te rattiṃ mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Rajaniye na rajjanti dusasniye na dussare 
 Mohaniye na muyhanti mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Iddhiṃ vimaṃsamānā te vattanti niccakālikaṃ 
 Paṭhaviṃ te pakampenti sārambena durāsadā 
  
   Taḷākāpi the taḷākāsu       Mandārakehi the   Dibbagandhā pavāyare the   Tadā 
 ahaṃ the   Phalappatto     se   Saddhamme     se   Uppadesu     se   
 Bhummantalikkhe the       hānā     se 
  
                  
  
     Kiḷamānā ca te sissā kīḷanti jhāyakīḷitaṃ 
 Jambuto phalamānenti mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Aññe gacchanti goyānaṃ aññe pubbavidehakaṃ   
 Aññe ca uttarakuruṃ esanāya durāsadā 
  
     Purato khāriṃ pesenti pacchatova vajanti te 
 Catubbisasahassehi chāditaṃ hoti ambaraṃ 
  
     Aggipāki anaggica danto dukkhalikā pi ca 
 Asamena koṭṭakā   keci pavattaphalabhojane 
  
     Udakorohanā   keci sāyaṃ pāto sucitā 
 Toyābhisecanakarā   mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā paṅkadantā rajassirā 
 Gandhitā silagandhena mama sissā durāsadā 
  
                  
  
     Pātova sannipatitvā   jaṭilā uggatāpanā 
 Lābhālābhaṃ pakittetvā gacchanti ambare tadā 
  
     Etesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ mahāsaddo pavattiti 
 Ajinacammasaddena moditā   honti devatā 
  
     Diso disaṃ pakkamanti antalikkhacarā isī 
 Sake balenupatthaddhā   te gacchanti yadicchakaṃ 
  
     Paṭhavikampakā ete sabbeva tabhacārino 
 Uggatejā duppasahā sāgarova akhobhiyā 
  
     hānavaṅkamino   keci keci nesajjikā isī 
 Pavattabhojanā keci mama sissā durāsadā 
  
     Ttovihārino ete hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Anattukkaṃsakā sabbe na te vambhenti kassaci 
  
     Siharājāva sambhitā   gajarājāva thamavā 
 Durāsadā vyagghāriva āgacchanti mamantike 
  
   Pubbavidehanaṃ ma     se   Koṭṭhakā     koṭṭikā mu a   Rohakā     se   
 Sekacaraṇi     se secakaraṇā ma   Sannipātetvā ma se a   Muditā ma se a   Sakabale 
       hānavaṅkamiyā       Ca chambhitā the 
  
                  
  
     Vijjādharā devatā ca nāgāgandhabbarakkhasā 
 Kumbhaṇḍā dānavā garuḷā upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Te jaṭākhāribharitā   ajinuttaravāsanā  
 Antalikkhacarā sabbe upajivanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
     Sadānucchavikā ete aññamaññaṃ sagāravā 
 Catubbisasahassānaṃ khipitasaddo   na vijjati 
  
     Pāde pādaṃ nikkhipantā appasaddā susaṃvutā 
 Upasaṅkamma sabbeva sirasā vandare mamaṃ 
  
     Tehi sissehi parivuto santehi ca tapassibhi 
 Vasāmi assame tattha jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ 
  
     Isinaṃ silagandhena pupphagandhena cubhayaṃ 
 Phalīnaṃ phalagandheṇa gandhito hoti assamo 
  
     Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi arati me na vijjati 
 Sake sisse ovadanto bhayyo hāsaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
  
     Pupphānaṃ pupphamānānaṃ phaḷānañca vipaccataṃ 
 Dibbā gandhā pavāyanti sobhayantā mamasasamaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Samādhimbhā vuṭṭhahitvā ātāpi nipako ahaṃ 
 Khāribhāraṃ gahetvā vanaṃ ajjhogahiṃ tadā 
     Uppāte supine cāpi lakkhaṇesu susikkhito 
 Pavattamānaṃ   mantapadaṃ dhārayāmi ahaṃ tadā   
  
     Anomadassi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Vivekakāmo sambuddho bhimavantamupāgami 
  
     Ajjhogahetvā himavantaṃ aggo kāruṇiko muti 
 Pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
     Tatthaddasāsiṃ   sambuddhaṃ sappabhāsaṃ manoramaṃ 
 Indivaraṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ 
  
     Palantaṃ diparukkhaṃva vijjuṃ gagane   yathā 
 Suphullaṃ sālarājā va addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Ayaṃ nago mahāvīro dukkhassantakaro muni 
 Imaṃ dassanamāgamma sabbadukkhā   pamuccare 
  
     Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ lakkhaṇaṃ upadhārayiṃ 
 Buddho nu kho na vā buddho handa passāmi   cakkhumaṃ 
  
   Bhārikā     the   Vāsino ma     se   Khitta saddo     
   Vattamānaṃ ma se   Sadā ma se   Tamaddasāhaṃ the ma se 
   Vijjutaṃgagane the vijjuṃvabbhaghane       Sabbe dukkhā       Taṃ namassāmi the 
  
                  
  
     Sahassārāni cakkāni dissanti caraṇuttame 
 Lakkhaṇānisasa disvāna niṭṭhaṃ gacchiṃ tathāgate 
  
     Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna sammajjitvānahaṃ kadā 
 Atha   pupphe samānetvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ apūjayiṃ 
  
     Pujayitvāna sambuddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
 Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā namassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Yena ñāṇena sambuddho viharittha   anāsavo 
 Taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
     Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ sayambhu amitodaya 
 Tava dasasnamāgamma kaṅkhāsotaṃ taranti te 
  
     Tuvaṃ sattathā ca ketu ca dhajo yupo ca pāṇinaṃ 
 Parāyaṇo pātiṭa ca dipo ca dipaduttamo 
  
     Sakkā samudde udakaṃ   pametuṃ āḷhakena vā 
 Na tveva tava sabbaññu ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave 
  
     Dharetuṃ paṭhaviṃ sakkā ṭhapetvā tulamaṇḍale 
 Na tveva tava sabbañuñāṇaṃ sakkā dharetave 
  
                  
  
     Ākāsaṃ manituṃ sakkā rajjuyā aṅgulena vā 
 Na tveva tava sabbañuñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave 
  
     Mahāsamudde udakaṃ paṭhaviṃ cākhilaṃ jahe    
 Buddhañāṇaṃ upādāya upamāto   na yujjare 
  
     Sadevakassa lokassa cittaṃ yesaṃ   pavattati 
 Antojālikatā   ete tava ñāṇambhi cakkhuma 
  
     Yena ñāṇena pattosi kecalaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
 Tena ñāṇena sabbaññu maddasi paratittiye 
  
     Imā gāthā thavitvāna   suruci nāma tāpaso 
 Ajinaṃ pattharitvāna paṭhaviyaṃ nisīdi so 
  
     Cullāsitisahassāni ajjhogāḷho mahaṇṇave 
 Accuggato tāvadeva girirāja pavuccati 
  
   Aṭṭhā     se   Vihareti ma viharati       Samudde udakaṃ sakkā the   Paṭhavi 
 cākhilā jahe     paṭhavi akhilā jaṭe ma   Upamā te       Sesaṃ se   Antojālagatā 
     a   Payitvāna     
  
                  
  
     Tāva accuggato nerū āyato vitthato ca so 
 Cuṇṇito aṇubhedena koṭisatasahassaso   
  
     Lakkhe ṭhapiyamānambhi parikkhayamagacchatha 
 Na ttheva tava sababaññu ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   
  
     Sukhumacchikena jālena udakaṃ yo parikkhipe 
 Ye keci udake pāṇā antejālikatā siyuṃ 
  
     Tatheva hi mahāvīra ye keci puthu titthiyā 
 Diṭṭhigahanapakkhantā   paramāsena mohitā 
  
     Tava suddhena ñāṇena anāvaraṇadassinā 
 Antojālagatā   ete ñāṇaṃ te nātivattare 
  
     Bhagavā tamhi samaye anomadassi mahāyaso 
 Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā disaṃ olokayi jino 
  
     Anomadassi munino nisabho nāma sāvako 
 Parivuto satasahassehi santacittehi tādihi 
  
     Khiṇāsavehi suddhehi chaḷabhiññehi jhāyibhi    
 Cittamaññāya buddhassa upesi   lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Antalikkhe ṭhitā tattha padakkhiṇamakaṃsu te 
 Namassantā pañajalikā otaruṃ buddhasantike 
  
     Anomadasasi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe   nisīditvā sītaṃ pātukari jino 
  
     Varuṇo nāmupaṭṭhāko sabbaññussa mahesino    
 Ekaṃsaṃ civaraṃ katvā apucchi lokanāyakaṃ 
  
                  
  
      Ko nu kho bhagavā hetu sitakammassa satthuno  
 Na hi buddhā ahetu hi sītaṃ pātukaronti te  
  
     Anomadassi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Saṅghamajjhe   tisiditvā imaṃ gāthamabhāsatha 
  
     Yo maṃ pupphena pujesi ñāṇañcāpi anutthavi 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mamabhāsato 
  
     Buddhassa giramaññāya sabbe devā samāgatā 
 Saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamuṃ 
  
   Sahassiyo ma       Khayeta ce the   Pakkhandā ma the     
   Jālikā ma   Tādihi       Upeti the   Bhikkhumajjhete   Anomadasasissa satthuno ma 
 the se   Bhikkhumajjhe the se 
  
                  
  
     Dasasu   lokadhātusu devatā yā   mahiddhikā 
 Saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamuṃ 
  
      Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅgini parivāressanti maṃ   niccaṃ 
 buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Upaṭṭhissantimaṃ    niccaṃ buddhapujāyidaṃ 
  
     Soḷasitthisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇaḍalā 
  
     Aḷārapambhā hasulā   susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ buddhapurāyidaṃ 
  
     Kappasatasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhantuṃ cakakvatti rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati 
  
     Sahassakkhantuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
     Pacchimbhave sampatte   manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Brāhmaṇi sāriyā nāma dhārayissati kucchinā 
  
     Mātuyā nāmagottena paññāyissatayaṃ naro 
 Sāriputtoti nāmena tikkhapañño bhavissati 
  
     Asitikoṭi   chaḍḍetvā pabbajissatakiñcano 
 Gavesanto santipadaṃ carissati mabhiṃ imaṃ 
  
     Aparimeyye   ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sāriputto ti nāmena hessati aggasāvako 
  
                  
  
     Ayaṃ bhāgirathi  gaṅgā himavantā pabhāvitā 
 Mahāsamuddamappeti tappayanti mahodadhiṃ 
  
     Tathevā yaṃ sāriputetā sake tisu    visārado 
 Paññāya pāramiṃ gananvā tappayissati pāṇino 
  
     Himavantaṃ upādāya sāgarañca mahosadadhiṃ 
 Etthantare yaṃ pulinaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
     Tampi sakkā asesena saṅkhātuṃ gaṇanā yathā 
 Na tveva sāriputtassa paññāya nto bhavissati 
  
   Sabbesu the   Devakāyā mu a   Parivārenti taṃ       Taṃ       Phasulā       
 Pacchime bhavasampatte ma the   Koṭiṃ ma the 
   Appameyya ma   Bhāgirasi ma        Sāke tisu ma the a 
  
                  
  
     Lakkhe ṭhapiyamānambhi khiye gaṅgāya vālukā 
 Na tveva sāriputtassa paññāya nto bhavissati 
  
     Mahāsamudde ūmiyo gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyā 
 Tatheva sāriputtasasa paññāyanto na hessati 
  
     Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā hessati agagasāvako 
  
     Pavattinaṃ dhammacakkaṃ sakyaputtena tādinā 
 Anuvantessani sammā   vassento   dhamamavuṭṭhiyota 
  
     Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati 
  
     Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ anomadassissa satthuno 
 Yassāhaṃ kāraṃ katvāna sabbattha pāramiṃ gato 
  
     Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbāṇaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ 
 Vicinaṃ titthiye sabbe tadāhaṃ saṃsariṃ bhave 
  
     Yathāpi vyādhito poso pariyeseyya osadhaṃ 
 Vicineyya vanaṃ   sabbaṃ vyādhito parimuttiyā 
  
     Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbāṇaṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
 Abbokiṇṇaṃ   pañcasataṃ pabbajiṃ isipabbajaṃ 
  
     Jaṭibhārena bharito ajinuttaranivāsano   
 Abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā brahmalokaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Natthi bāhirake   suddhi ṭhapetvā jinasāsanaṃ 
 Ve keci buddhimā sattā sujjhanti jinasāsane 
  
     Attakāramayaṃ   etaṃ nayidaṃ itihitihaṃ    
 Adaṅkhataṃ gavesanto kutitthaṃ sañcariṃ ahaṃ 
  
   Anuvattisasti sadadhammaṃ ma the   Vassanto ma the     se 
   Dhanaṃ ma the   Avyakiṇṇaṃ       Nivāsaha ma     se 
   Bāhiyake the   Atthakāmaṃ mamaṃ     se   Itihaṃ tadā     se 
  
                  
  
     Yathā sāratthiko poso kadaliṃ chetvāna phālaye 
 Na tattha sāraṃ vindeyya sārena ritatako hi so 
  
     Tatheva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhi bahujjanā 
 Asaṅkhatena rittāse   sārena kadali yathā 
  
     Pacchīmabhave sampatte   brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ 
 Mahābhogaṃ   chaḍḍhayitvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
   Paṭhamabhāṇavāraṃ   
  
     Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragu 
 Brāhmaṇo sañajayo nāma tassa mule vasāmahaṃ 
  
     Sāvako te mahāvīra assaji nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Durāsado uggatejo piṇḍāya carati tadā   
  
     Tamaddasāsiṃ   sappaññaṃ muniṃ mone samāhitaṃ 
 Santacittaṃ mahānāgaṃ suphullaṃ padumaṃ yathā 
  
     Disvā me cittamuppajji   sudannaṃ suddhamānasaṃ 
 Usabhaṃ pavaraṃ viraṃ arahā yaṃ bhavissati 
     Pāsādiko iriyati abhirūpo susaṃvuto 
 Uttame damathe danto amatadassi   bhavissati 
  
     Yannunāhaṃ uttamatthaṃ puccheyyaṃ tuṭṭhamānasaṃ 
 So me puṭṭhā kathessati paṭipucchāma haṃ tadā 
  
     Piṇḍapātaṃ   carantassa pacchato agamāsahaṃ 
 Okāsaṃ paṭimānetto pucchituṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
  
     Vithantare   anuppatataṃ upagantvāna pucchahaṃ 
 Kathaṃ gottosi tvaṃ vīra kassa sissosi mārisa  
  
     So me puṭṭhā viyākāsi asambhitova    kesarī 
 Buddho loke samuppanto tasasa sissombhi āvuso 
  
                  
  
     Kidisaṃ te mahāvīra anujāta mahāyasa     
 Buddhassa sāsanaṃ dhammaṃ  Sādhu me kathayassu bho 
  
   Rittāva       Pacchime bhava ma the   Koṭiyo sataṃ     
   Sadā       Tamaddasāhaṃ ma the tamaddasāmi se   Vitatimuppajji ma the 
   Anomadassi ma   Piṇḍacāraṃ       Vithintare ma the    Ajambhitova the    
 Mahāyaso     
  
                  
  
     So me puṭṭhā kathi   sabbaṃ gambhiraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ 
 Taṇhāsallassa bhantāraṃ sabbadukkhāpanudanaṃ   
  
      Ye dhammā hetuppabhavā tesaṃ hetuṃ tathāgato āha 
 Tesañca yo nirodho evaṃvādi mahāsamaṇo  
  
     Sohaṃ vissajjite pañeha paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃ 
 Virajo vimalo āsiṃ sutvāna jinasāsanaṃ 
  
     Sutvāna munino vākyaṃ passitvā dhammamuttamaṃ 
 Pariyogāḷhasaddhammo ima gāthaṃ abhāsahaṃ 
  
      Eso va dhammo yadi tāvadeva paccabyathā padamasokaṃ 
 Adiṭṭhaṃ abbhathītaṃ bahukehi   kappanahutehi 
  
     Svāhaṃ dhammaṃ gavesanto kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto kālo me nappamajjituṃ  
  
     Tosikohaṃ assajinā patvāna acalaṃ padaṃ 
 Sahāyakaṃ gavesanto assamaṃ agamāsabhaṃ 
  
     Duratova mamaṃ disvā sahāyo me susikkhito 
 Iriyāpathasampanno   idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
     Pasannamukhanettosi munibhāvova dissati 
 Amatādhigato kacci nibbāṇaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ  
  
     Subhānurūpo āyāsi āneñajakārito viya 
 Dantova dantadamathe   upasantosi brāhmaṇa 
  
     Amataṃ mayā adhigataṃ sokasallapanudanaṃ    
 Tvampi taṃ adhigacchāhi   gacchāma buddhasantikaṃ 
  
     Sādhuti so paṭissutvā   sahāyo me susikkhito 
 Hatthena hatthaṃ gaṇhitvā upāgami   tava ntikaṃ    
  
   Kathaṃ ma   Dukkha   ma the   Bahuhi ma   Ariyāpathaṃ mama disvā ma the 
   Dannovuttamadamathe mu a   Salla visodhanaṃ the sallavinodāṃ     se 
   Adhigacchasi ma     se   Sādhuni paṭisuṇitvā ma the se   Upagamma ma 
    Santhusantikaṃ     
  
                  
  
     Ubhopi pabbajissāma sakyaputta tavantike    
 Tava sāsanamāgamama viharāma anāsavā 
  
     Kolito iddhiyā seṭṭho ahaṃ paññāya pārago 
 Ubhova ekato hutvā sāsanaṃ sobhayāmase 
  
                  
  
     Apariyositasaṅkappo kutitthe sañcariṃ ahaṃ 
 Tava dassanamāgamma saṅkappo purito mama 
  
     Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya pupphanti samaye dumā 
 Dibbagandhā sampavanti nosenti sabbapāṇinaṃ   
     Tathevāhaṃ mahāvīra sakyaputta mahāyasa 
 Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya samayesāmi pupphituṃ 
  
     Vimuttipupphaṃ esanto bhavasaṃsāramocanaṃ 
 Vimuttipupphalābhena tosemi sabbapāṇinaṃ 
  
     Yāvatā buddhakhettambhi ṭhapetvāna mahāmuniṃ 
 Paññāya sadiso natthi tava puttassa cakkhuma 
  
     Suvinitā ca te sissā parisā ca susikkhitā 
 Uttame damathe dantā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samāhitā 
 Munī moneyyasampannā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Appicchā nipakā dhīrā appāhārā ālolupā 
 Vivekābhiratā dhīrā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Āraññakā dhutadharā jhāyino lukhacīvarā 
 Vivekābhirātā dhīrā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Paṭipannā phalaṭṭhā ca sekhā phalasamaṅgino 
 Āsiṃsakā   uttamatthaṃ parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Sotāpannā ca vimalā sakadāgāmino ca ye 
 Anāgāmi ca arahā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Satipaṭṭhanakusalā bojjhaṅgabhāvanāratā 
 Sāvakā te bahu sabbe parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
   Sakya puttassa santike the    Evaṃ sabbattha    Āsisakā ma the 
  
                  
  
     Iddhipādesu   kusalā samādhibhāvanāratā 
 Sammappadhānamanuyuttā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā 
 Paññāya pāramiṃ pattā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Edisā te mahāvira tava sissā susikkhitā 
 Durāsadā uggatejā parivārenti taṃ sadā 
  
     Tehi sissehi parivuto saññatehi tapassihi 
 Migarājāvasambhito   uḷurājava sobhasi 
  
     Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya ruhanti dharaṇirūhā 
 Vepullataṃ pāpuṇanti phalañca adadyanti te 
  
                  
  
     Paṭhavisadiso tvaṃsi sakyaputta mahāyasa 
 Sāsane te patiṭaya labhanti amataṃ phalaṃ 
     Sindhu sarasasati ceva tadiyo candabhāgikā    
 Gaṅgā ca yamunā ceva sarakhu ca atho mahi 
  
     Etāsaṃ sandamānānaṃ sāgaro sampaṭicchati 
 Jahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ sāgarotveva ñāyati 
  
     Tathevime catubbaṇṇā   pabbajitvā tavantike 
 Jahanti purimaṃ nāma buddhaputtāni ñāyare 
  
     Yathāpi cando vimalo gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyā 
 Sabbe tāragaṇe loke ābhāya atirocati 
  
     Tathe tvaṃ mahāvīra parivuto devamānuse 
 Ete sabbe atikkamma jalasī sabbadā tuvaṃ 
  
     Gambhire uṭṭhitā ūmi na velaṃ ativattare    
 Sabbāva velaṃ   phusanti saṃvuṇṇā vikiranti tā 
  
     Tatheva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhi bahujjanā 
 Dhammaṃ vaditukāmā   te nātivattanti taṃ muniṃ 
  
     Sace ca taṃ pāpuṇanti paṭivādehi   cakkhuma 
 Tavantikaṃ upāgantvā sañcuṇṇāva bhavanti te 
  
     Yathāpi udake jātā kumudā mandālakā   bahu 
 Upalimpanti toyena kadadama    kalalena ca 
  
     Tatheva bahukā sattā loke jātā virūhare 
 Aṭṭitā rāgadosena kadadame kumudaṃ yathā 
  
     Yathāpi padumaṃ jalajaṃ jalamajjhe virūhati 
 Na so    limpati toyena pariyuddho    hi kesarī 
  
   Iddhipāde ca ma   Cambhito the   Bhāgiyo       Catuvaṇṇā ma       Ativattani 
 ma     se   Sabbā velaṃ ma     the   Vāditukāmā ma the dhāritukāma     se   
 Parivārehi se   Maddālikā     
    Kassamaṃ ma the    Taṃ the    Parisuddhaṃ the 
  
                  
  
     Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra goke jato mahāmuni 
 No palimpasi   lokena toyena padumaṃ yathā 
  
     Yathāpi ramamake mase bahu pupphanti vārijā 
 Nātikkamanti taṃ māsaṃ samayo pupphanāya so 
  
                  
  
     Tatheva tvaṃ sakyaputta pupphito te vimutatiyā 
 Sāsanaṃ nātivattanti   padumaṃ vārijaṃ yathā 
  
     Supupphito sālarājā dibbaṃ gandhaṃ pavāyati 
 Aññasālehi parivuto sālarājāva sobhani 
     Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra buddhañāṇena pupphito 
 Bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto sālarājāva sobhasi 
  
     Yathāpi solo himavā osadho sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Nāgānaṃ asurānañca devatānañca ālayo 
  
     Tatheva tvaṃ vahāvīra osadho viya pāninaṃ 
 Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā 
  
     Anusiṭṭhā mahāvīra tayā kāruṇikena te 
 Ramanti dhammaratiyā vasanti tava sāsane 
  
     Vigarājā yathā sīho abhinikkhamma āsayā 
 Catuddisā viloketvā   tikkhantuṃ abhinādati   
  
     Sabbe migā uttasanti migarājassa gajjato 
 Tathā hi jātimā eso pasu   tāseti sabbadā 
  
     Gajjato te mahāvīra vasudhā sampakampati    
 Bodhaneyyaṃ cakkhujjhanta tasanti mārakāyikā 
  
     Tasanti titthiyā sabbe nadato te mahāmune    
 Kākasenāva vibabhantā   migaraññā yathā migā 
  
     Ye keci gaṇino loke satthāroti pavuccare 
 Paramparāgataṃ dhammaṃ desenti parisāya te 
  
     Na he vaṃ   tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃ 
 Sāmaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā kevalaṃ bodhipakkhiyaṃ 
  
   Limpati ma the    Evaṃ sabbattha    Disānuloketvā ma catuddisaṃ the 
   Abhinādayi ma the se   Pasuṃ ma   Vasudhāyaṃ pakampani the ma   Mahāmunima the 
   Kākā senāva vibbhanti ma the   Naheva     natvevaṃ ma the 
  
                  
  
     Āsayānusayaṃ ñatvā indriyānaṃ balābalaṃ 
 Bhabbābhabbe viditvāna mahāmeghova gajjasi 
  
     Cakkavāḷapariyantaṃ   nisinnā parisā bhave 
 Nānādiṭṭhā vicintentā   vimaticchedanāya taṃ 
  
                  
  
     Sabbesaṃ cittamaññāya opammakusalo muni 
 Ekaṃ pañahaṃ kathentova vimatiṃ chindasi   pāṇinaṃ 
  
     Upatissasadiseheva   vasudhā puritā bhave 
 Sabbeva te pañajalikā kittayuṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Apatissasadiseheva   vasudhā puritā bhave 
 Parimetuṃ na sakkeyyuṃ   appameyyā tathāgatā 
  
     Yathā sakena thāmena kittito hi mayā   jino 
 Kappakoṭimpi kittentā evameva pakittayuṃ 
  
     Sace hi koci devo vā manusso vā susikkhito 
 Pametuṃ parikappeyya   vighātaṃ va labheyya so 
  
     Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya sakyaputta mahāyasa 
 Paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Titthiye sampamaddāmi vattemi jinasāsanaṃ 
 Dhammasenāpati ajja sakyaputassa sāsane 
  
     Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sukhitto saravegova kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ   
  
     Yo koci manujo bhāṃ dhāreyya matthake sadā 
 Bhārena dukkhito asasa bhārehi bharito tathā 
  
     Ḍayhamāno tihagagihi bhavesu saṃsariṃ ahaṃ 
 Bharito bhavabhārena neruṃ uccārito   yathā 
  
     Oropito ca me bhāro bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā 
 Karaṇiyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ sakyaputtassa sāsane 
  
     Yāvatā buddhakhettambhi ṭhapetvā sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Ayaṃ aggomhi paññāya sadiso me na vijjati 
  
   Pariyantā ma the se   Vicintenti     vicinattā the   Chindi   sabbattha    
 Apadisasadiseheva     a   Na pappeyyuṃ Te     napabbeyyuṃ ma   Mahā     se 
   Puritaṃ parikaḍiḍhesya     se a   Jhāpayi mama a mu   Giriṃ uccārito mu a giriṃ 
 udadharito the se 
  
                  
  
     Samādhimhi sukusalo iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato 
 Icchāmāno cahaṃ ajja sahassaṃ abhinimminena 
  
                  
  
     Anupubbavihārassa visabhuto mahāmuni 
 Kathesi sāsanaṃ mayhaṃ nirodo sayanaṃ mama 
  
     Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ me samādhikusalo ahaṃ 
 Sammappadhānānuyutto bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato 
  
     Sāvakena hi pattabbaṃ sabbameva kataṃ mayā    
 Lokatāthaṃ ṭhapetvāna sadiso me na vijjati 
  
     Samāpattinayakusalo   jhānavimokkhānaṃ khippalābhi  
 Bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato sāvakaguṇapāramiṃ gatosmi   
  
     Sāvakaguṇenāpi phussena   buddhiyā purisuttamagāravā    
 Saddhāya saṅgahitaṃ   cittaṃ sadā sabrahmacārisu 
     Uddhaṭaviso va    sappo chinnavasāṇova usabho 
 Nikkhittamānadappo   upemi garugāravena gaṇaṃ 
  
     Yadi rūpani bhatvayya paññā me vasumati na sameyya 
 Anomadassissa bhagavato phalametaṃ ñāṇathavanāya    
  
     Pavattinaṃ dhammacakkaṃ sakyaputtena tādinā 
 Anuvattemahaṃ sammā    ñāṇathavanāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Mā me kadāci pāpicechā kusito hinavīriyo 
 Appassuto anācāro sameto ahu katthaci 
  
     Bahussuto ca medhāvi sīlesu susamābhito 
 Cetosamathānuyutetā api muddhati tiṭṭhatu 
  
     Taṃ vo vadāmi bhadhadante yāvantettha samāgatā 
 Appicchā hotha santuṭṭhā jhāyī jhānaratā sadā 
  
                  
  
     Yamahaṃ paṭhamaṃ disvā virajo vimalo ahuṃ 
 So me ācariyo dhīro assaji nāma sāvako 
  
     Tassāhaṃ vāhasā ajja dhammasenāpati ahuṃ 
 Sabbattha pāramiṃ patvā    viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Yo me ācariyo āsi assaji nāma sāvako 
 Yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasati usasisamhi karomahaṃ 
  
   Kataṃ mama     se   Samāpattinaṃ kusalo ma the samāpattivinaya se 
   Jhānavimokkhapaṭilābhi the vimokkhakhippalābhi ma   Sāvakapāramiṃ gato the 
 sāvakapāramiṃ ma   Phusena se       Parisuttamabhāravā     se gāravaṃ the   
 Sabbesaṃ sahinaṃ the yaṃ saddhāsaṅgahitaṃ ma   Udadhata ma     the 
   Dappova ma the    Ñāṇathomanāya se    Anuvattesahaṃ sabbaṃ ma the    Patto se 
  
                  
  
     Mama kammaṃ saritvāna gotamo sakyapuṅgavo  
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāriputto thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sāriputtattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Mahāmoggallānattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Vihāsi himavantamhi devasaṅghapurakkhato 
  
     Varuṇo nāma nāmena nāgarājā ahaṃ tadā 
 Kāmarūpī vikubbāmi   mahodadhinivāsahaṃ   
  
     Saṅgaṇiyaṃ   gaṇaṃ hitvā turiyaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃ 
 Sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vādesuṃ accharā tadā 
  
     Vajjamānesu turiyesu   devā turiyāni   vajjayuṃ    
 Ubhinnaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna budedhāpi   sampabujjhatha 
  
     Nimantiyitvā sambuddhaṃ sakaṃ bhavanamupāgamiṃ 
 Āsanaṃ paññapetvāna kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Khiṇāsavasahassehi parivuto lokanāyako 
 Ohāsento disā sabbā bhavanaṃ me upāgami 
  
                  
  
     Upaviṭṭhaṃ vahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Sabhikkhusaṅghaṃ tappesiṃ   annapānenahaṃ tadā 
  
     Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
   Vikuppāmi the   Nivāsayaṃ ma the   Aṅgiṇiyaṃ se abiniyaṃ a 
   Turesu ma the   Turāni ma the   Vajjiṃsu     se a 
   Sambuddho the   Tappemi the ma         imā devā gāthāyo   se     potthakesu na 
 vijjanti 
  
                  
  
      Yo   so saṅghaṃ apūjesi   buddhañca lokanāyakaṃ 
 Tena cittappasādena devalokaṃ gamissati 
  
     Santasattatikkhantuṃ ca devarajjaṃ karisasti 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ   aṭṭhasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
  
     Pañca paññāsakkhantuñca cakakvatti bhavissati 
 Bhogā asaṅkhiyā tassa uppajjissanti tāvade 
  
     Aparimeyye ito kappo okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Nirayā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Kolito nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati 
  
     So pacchā pabbajitvāna kusalamulena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato dutiyo hessati sāvako 
  
     Āraddhavirayo pahitatto iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibabāyissatanāsavo  
     Pāpamittopanissāya kāmarāgavasaṃ gato 
 Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi ghatayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso 
  
     Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi nirayaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Pāpakammasamaṅgittā   bhinanasīso marāmahaṃ    
  
     Idaṃ pacchāmakaṃ mayahaṃ carimo cattate bhavo 
 Idhāpi edisaṃ   mayhaṃ maraṇakāle bhavissati 
  
     Pavivekamanuyutto samādhibhāvanārato 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Dharaṇimpi sugambhiraṃ bahalaṃ duppadhaṃsiyaṃ 
 Vāmaṅguṭṭhena khobheyyaṃ   iddhiyā pāramiṃ gato 
  
     Asmimānaṃ na passāmi māno mayhaṃ na vijjati 
 Sāmaṇere upādāya garucittaṃ karomahaṃ 
  
     Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ kammamabhinihariṃ 
 Tāhaṃ bhūmimanuppatto pattomahi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
              Gāthā             gāthāhi samā  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā moggallāno thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Moggallānattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Yaṃ ma te   Ahojesi the   Pathavya rajjaṃ mu a   Gottena se   Samaṅgito the 
 samaṅginaṃ       Bhavāmahaṃ     se   Tādiso the ediso ma   Caleyyaṃ the 
  
                  
  
   Mahākassapattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Nibbute lokanāthambhi pujaṃ kubbanti satthuno 
  
     Udaggacittā   janatā āmoditapamoditā 
 Tesu saṃvegajātesu piti me upapajjatha   
  
     Ñātimitte samānetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  Parinibbuto mahāvīro handa pujaṃ karomaye  
  
     Sādhuni te paṭissutvā bhiyo hāsaṃ janiṃsu me 
  Buddhasmiṃ lokanāthasmiṃ kāhāma puññasañcayaṃ  
  
     Agghiyaṃ sukataṃ katvā satahatthasamugagataṃ 
 Diyaḍḍhatthapatthaṭaṃ   vimānaṃ nabhamuggataṃ 
  
     Katvāna hammiyaṃ   tattha tālapattihi citatitaṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā cetiyaṃ pujayuttamaṃ 
  
     Aggikkhandheva jalito sālarājāva   phullito 
 Indalaṭṭhiva ākāse obhāseti catudadisā 
  
     Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā katvana kusalaṃ bahuṃ 
 Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna nidasaṃ upapajjahaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Sahassayuttabhayavābhiṃ dibbayānamadhiṭṭhito 
 Ubbiddhaṃ   bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ sattabhumaṃ   samuggataṃ 
  
     Kuṭāgārasahassāni sabbasoṇṇamayā   ahu 
 Jalanni sakatejena disā sabbā pabhāsayaṃ 
  
     Santi aññepi niyyuhā lohitaṅkamayā tadā 
 Tepi jotenti ābhāya samantā caturo disā 
  
     Puññakamāmabhinibbattā kuṭāgārā sunimmitā 
 Maṇimayāpi jotenti disā dasa samantato 
  
     Tesaṃ ujjotamānānaṃ obhāso vipulo ahu 
 Sabbe deve atibhomi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi ubbiddho   nāma khattiyo 
 Cāturanto vijitāvi paṭhaviṃ    āvasiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Tatheva    bhaddake kapepa tiṃsakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ 
 Sakakammābhīraddhomhi cakakavatti mahabbalo 
 Satatratanasampanno catudipamhi isasaro 
  
     Tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayahaṃ indalaṭṭhiva uggataṃ 
 Āyāmato catubbisaṃ    vitthārena ca dvādasaṃ    
  
    Aggiṃ minannatā janatā ti samuho aggiṃ ādāhanatthāya minantā   rāsi karontā    
 aṭṭhakathā   Udapajjatha ma       Diyaḍḍhahatthasatampi       Agaghiyaṃ     
 se   Kiṃsuko viya se   Ubabhidaṃ the   Sattabhumi     se   Sabbe sovaṇṇayā     
 sabbe the   Catubbisa ma the se    Pathacayyaṃ the    Tattheva the    Catubbisa ma the 
 se    Davādasa se ma the dvādasā     
  
                  
  
     Ramakaṃ nāma nagaraṃ daḷahapākāratoraṇaṃ 
 Āyāmato pañcacasataṃ vitthārena tadaḍḍhakaṃ 
 Ākinnaṃ janakāyehi tidasānaṃ puraṃ viya 
  
     Yathā sucighare suci pakkhittā paṇṇavisati 
 Aññamaññaṃ paghaṭṭenati ākiṇṇaṃ hoti taṃ tadā   
  
     Evampi nagaraṃ mayhaṃ hatthassarathasaṅkulaṃ 
 Manussehi sadākiṇṇaṃ   rammakaṃ nagaruttamaṃ 
  
     Tattha bhutvā pivitvā   ca puna devattanaṃ   gato 
 Bhave pacchimake mayhaṃ ahosi kulasampadā 
  
                  
  
     Brahmaññakulasambhuto mahāratanasañcayo 
 Asitikoṭiyo hitvā hiraññassāpi pabbajiṃ   
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākassapo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mahākassapattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
   Anuruddhattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Sumedhaṃ bhagavantāhaṃ lokajeṭṭhā narāsabhaṃ 
 Vupakaṭṭhaṃ viharantaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Upagantvā sambuddhaṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Añajalimpaggahetvāna buddhaseṭṭhamayāva haṃ 
  
      Anukampa   mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha narāsabha 
 Padīpaṃ te padassami rukkhamulambhi jhāyato  
  
     Adhivāsesi so dhīro sayambhu vadataṃ varo 
 Dumesu vinivijjhitvā yantaṃ yojetva haṃ   tadā 
  
     Sahassavaṭṭiṃ pādāsiṃ buddhassa lokabandhuno 
 Sattāhaṃ pajjalitvāna dīpā vupasamiṃsu me   
  
     Tena cittappasādena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ vimānamupapajjahaṃ 
  
     Uppannassa devattaṃ vyamhaṃ āsi sunimmitaṃ    
 Samantato pajjalati dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Samantā yojanasataṃ virocesiṃ    ahaṃ tadā 
 Sabbe deve atibhomi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Hoti laṅkataṃ ma the laṅkato se   Tadākiṇṇaṃ     se   Bhuttāca pītvā     bhutvā 
 vasitvā ca se   Punapi devataṃ ma the   Paribbajiṃ     se   Anukampi       
 Yojiyahaṃ ma the   Padipa vupasammisu       Thambho āsi sunimamito ma     se 
    Virocemi     
  
                  
  
     Tiṃsa kappāni devindo devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Na maṃ kevatimaññanti   dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Aṭṭhavisatikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
 Divārattiñca passāmi samantā yojanaṃ tadā 
  
     Sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena passāmi santhusāsane 
 Dibbacakkhuṃ anuppatto dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Sumedho nāma sambuddho tiṃsakappasahassino 
 Tassa dīpo mayā dinno vippasanne cetasā 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anuruddho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Anuruddhattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Puṇṇattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Ajjhayako mattadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu 
 Purakkhatomahi sissehi upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mama kammaṃ pakittesi saṅkhittena mahāmuni 
  
     Tāhaṃ dhammaṃ suṇitvāna abhivādetvāna satthuno 
 Añajalimpaggahetvāna pakkāmiṃ dakkhiṇamukho 
  
     Saṅkhittena suṇitvāna vitthārena adesayiṃ    
 Sabbe sissā   attamanā sutvāna mama bhāsato 
  
     Sakadiṭṭhiṃ vinodetvā buddhe cittaṃ pasādayuṃ 
 Saṅkhittenapi desemi   vitthārena tatheva haṃ   
  
                  
  
     Abhidhammanayaññuhaṃ   kathāvatthuvisuddhiyo 
 Sabbesaṃ viññapetvāna viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Ito pañcasate kappe caturo suppakāsakā 
 Sattaratanasampannā catudipambhi issarā 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasso ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇeṇā mattāniputto thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Puṇṇamattāniputtattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
   Kevitimaññanti the ma   Abhāsayiṃ ma   Piyā the   Desesiṃ ma 
   Pibhāsayiṃ ma   Nayaññehaṃ ma     
  
                  
  
   Upālittherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nagare haṃsavatiyā sujāto nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Asitikoṭinicayo pahutadhanadhaññacā 
  
     Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu 
 Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca sadhamme   pāramiṃ gato 
  
     Paribbājā ekasikhā   gotamā   buddhasāvakā 
 Carakā   nāpasā ceva caranti mabhiyā tadā 
  
     Tepi maṃ parivārenti brāhmaṇo vissuto iti 
 Bahujjano maṃ pujeti nāhaṃ pujemi kañcanaṃ 
  
     Pujārahaṃ na passāmi mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadā 
 Buddhoti vacanaṃ   natthi tāva nupapajjate jano 
  
     Accayena ahorattā padumuttaranāyako    
 Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā loke uppajji cakkhumā 
  
     Vitthārino   bāhujaññe puthubhute ca sāsane 
 Upāgami tadā buddho nagaraṃ haṃsasavhayaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Pitu atthāya so buddho dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā 
 Tena kālena parisā samantā yojanaṃ tadā 
  
     Sammato manujānaṃ so   sunando nāma tāpaso 
 Yāvatā buddhaparisā pupphehacchādayi tadā 
  
     Catusaccaṃ pakāsente seṭṭhe ca    pupphamaṇḍape 
 Koṭisatasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu 
  
     Sattarattindivaṃ buddho vassetvā    dhammavuṭṭhiyo     
 Aṭṭhame divase patte sunandaṃ kittayī jino 
  
      Devaloke manusse vā saṃsaranto ayaṃ bhave 
 Sabbesaṃ pavaro hutvā bhavesu saṃsarissati 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Mattāniputto puṇeṇāti hessati santhusāmako  
  
     Evaṃ kittayi sambuddho    sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā 
 Bhāsayanto janaṃ sabbaṃ dassayanto sakaṃ balaṃ 
  
   Saddhamme     the   Ekabhikkhā ma   Gotama       Varaṇā the 
   Kiñcanaṃ a mu   Savanaṃ ma   Nāmako ma   Vitthārike ma     
   Yo ma se    Heṭṭhā ca ma heṭṭhato the    Vasasitvā ma     
    Vuṭṭhiyā     the    So buddho Ma 
  
                  
  
     Katañajali namassanti sunandaṃ tapasaṃ janā   
 Buddhe kāraṃ karitvāna sodhesi   gatimattano 
  
     Tattha me ahu saṅkappo sutvāna munito vacaṃ 
 Ahampi kāraṃ kassāmi yathā pasasāmi gotamaṃ 
  
     Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kiriyaṃ cintayiṃ   mamaṃ 
 Kyāhaṃ kammaṃ ācarāmi puññakkhette anuttare  
  
     Ayañca pāṭhiko   bhikkhu sabbapāṭhina   sāsane 
 Vinaye ca agganikkhitetā taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ   ahaṃ 
  
     Idaṃ me amitaṃ bhogaṃ akkhobhaṃ sāgarūpamaṃ 
 Tena bhogena buddhassa ārāmaṃ māpayiṃ   ahaṃ 
  
     Sobhanaṃ nāma ārāmaṃ nagarassa puratthato 
 Kitvā   satasahassena saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ 
  
                  
  
     Kūṭāgāre ca pāsāde maṇḍape hammiye guhā 
 Caṅkame sukate katvā saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ 
  
     Jantāgharaṃ aggisālaṃ atho udakamāḷakaṃ 
 Nahānagharaṃ māpayitvā bhikkhusaṅghassadāsabhaṃ 
  
     Āsandiyo piṭhake ca paribhoge ca bhājane 
 Ārāmikañca bhesajjaṃ sabbametaṃ adāsabhaṃ 
  
     Ārakkhaṃ paṭṭhapetvāna pākāraṃ kārayiṃ daḷhaṃ 
 Mā naṃ koci viheṭhesi santacittāna tādinaṃ 
  
     Āvāsaṃ satasahassena   saṅghārāme    amāpayiṃ 
 Vepullataṃ pāpayitvā    sambuddhaṃ upanāmayiṃ 
  
      Niṭṭhāpito mayā rāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni 
 Niyyādesasāmi    te    vīra adhivāsehi cakkhuma  
     Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya adivāsesi nāyako 
  
     Adhivāsanamaññāya sabbaññussa mahesino 
 Bhojanaṃ paṭiyādetvā kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Ārocitambhi kālambhi pudumuttaranāyako 
 Khiṇāsamasahassehi ārāmaṃ me upāgami 
  
     Nisinnaṃ kālamaññāya annapānena tappayiṃ 
 Bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya idaṃ vacanamabuviṃ 
  
   Tadā     se   Sodheti the   Citatayi the   Pāṭhito ma pāṭiko the   Sabbapāṭhissa ma 
 sabbapāṭhiva the sabbapāṭhika a mu   Patthaye a mu   Māpaye a mu   Katvā     the 
   Satasahassenāvāsaṃ ma āvāsasatasahasse se āvāsasatasabhassena the    Saṅghārāmaṃ 
        Vepullaṃ taṃ māpayitvā ma the    Niye jessami the    Taṃ ma se the 
  
                  
  
      Kito satasahassena tattakeneva kārito 
 Sobhano nāma ārāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni   
  
     Iminārāmadānena vetanāpaṇidhibhi ca 
 Bhave nibbattamānohaṃ labhāmi mama patthitaṃ  
  
     Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Yo so buddhassa pādāsi saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi puṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
                  
  
     Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅgini 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Chaḷāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā 
  
     Āḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajajaṃ karissati 
  
     Devarājena pattabbaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilabhissati 
 Anunabhogo hutvāna idavarajjaṃ karissati 
  
     Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo  
 Gotamo nama gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Upāli nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
     Vinaye pāramiṃ patthā   ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido 
 Jinasāsanaṃ dhārayanto   viharissanāsavo 
  
     Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesasti  
  
     Aparimeyyupādāya patthemi tava sāsanaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo 
  
   Mune the   Patto     the   Jotayanto the dhārento     se 
  
                  
  
     Yathā sulāvuto poso rājadaṇḍena tajjito 
 Sule sātaṃ avindanto   parimuttiṃva icchati 
  
     Tathehāhaṃ mahāvīra bhavadaṇḍena tajjito 
 Kammasulāvuto santo pipāsāvedanaṭṭito   
  
     Bhave sātaṃ na vindāmi ḍayahanto tihi aggihi 
 Parimuttiṃ gavesāmi yathāpi rājadaṇḍito 
  
                  
  
     Yathā visādo   puriso visena paripiḷito 
 Agadaṃ so gaveseyya visaghātāyupānaṃ   
  
     Gavesamāno passeyya agadaṃ visaghātakaṃ 
 Taṃ pivitvā   sukhī assa visamhā parimuttiyā 
  
     Tathehāhaṃ mahāvīra yatā visahato   naro 
 Samapiḷito avijjāya saddhammādamesayiṃ   
  
     Dhammāgadaṃ   gavesanto adadakkhiṃ sakyasāsanaṃ 
 Aggaṃ sabbosadhānaṃ taṃ sabbasallavinodanaṃ 
     Dhammosadhaṃ pipitvāna visaṃ sabbaṃ samuhaniṃ   
 Ajarāmaraṃ sitibhāvaṃ nibbāṇaṃ phassayiṃ    ahaṃ 
  
     Yathā bhūtaṭṭito    poso bhūtagāhena piḷito 
 Bhūtavejjaṃ gaveseyya bhūtasmā parimuttiyā 
  
     Gavesamāno passeyya bhūtavijjāsu kovidaṃ     
 Tassa so vihane    bhūtaṃ samulañca vināsaye 
  
     Tathevāhaṃ mahāvīra tamaggāhena piḷito 
 Ñāṇālokaṃ gavesāmi tamato parimuttiyā 
  
     Athaddasaṃ sakyamuniṃ kilesatamasodhanaṃ 
 So me tamaṃ vinodesi bhūtavejjova bhūtakaṃ    
  
     Saṃsārasotaṃ saṃchindiṃ tuṇhāsotaṃ nivārayiṃ 
 Bhavaṃ ugghāṭayiṃ sabbaṃ bhūtavejjova mulato 
  
     Garuḷo yathā opatati    pannagaṃ bhakkhamattano 
 Samantā yojanasataṃ vikkhobheti mahāsaraṃ 
  
     Pannagaṃ so gahetvāna adhosisaṃ viheṭhayaṃ    
 Ādāya so pakkamati yena kāmaṃ vihaṅgamo 
  
     Tathevāhaṃ    mahāvīra yathāpi garuḷo khalī    
 Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto dose vikkhālayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Diṭṭho ahaṃ dhammavaraṃ santipadamanuttaraṃ 
 Ādāya viharāmetaṃ garuḷo pannagaṃ yathā 
  
   Na vindanto     the   Vedanaddito the   Visārado the 
   Yupāyanaṃ ma se a yupāyaso       Pivitvāna the   Visato ma   Mesahaṃ     the 
   Dhammosadha the   Samuhataṃ the    Passayiṃ ma       Bhūtaddito the    
 Bhūtavejjaṃ sukovidaṃ the    Vihite the    Bhūtikaṃ  sabbesu     Yathopatti ma opatti 
     opatitaṃ the    Vipoṭhayaṃ the    Tatheva tvaṃ ma        Balaṃ the 
  
                  
  
     Āsāvati nāma latā jātā cittalatāvane 
 Tassā vassasahassena ekaṃ nibbattate phalaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Taṃ devā paṭirūpāsanti tāva dūre phale sati    
 Devānaṃ sā piyā   evaṃ āsāvatilatuttamā 
  
     Satasahassupādāya tāhaṃ   paricare muniṃ 
 Sāyaṃ pātaṃ namassāmi devā āsāvatiṃ yathā 
  
     Avañajhā pāricariyā amoghā ca namassanā 
 Durāgatampi maṃ mantaṃ khaṇo maṃ   na virādhayī 
  
     Paṭisandhiṃ na pasasāmi vicinanto bhave ahaṃ 
 Nirūpadhi vippamutto upasanno carāmahaṃ 
  
     Yathāpi padumaṃ nāma suriyaraṃsena pupphati 
 Tathevāhaṃ mahāvīra buddharaṃsena pupphito 
  
     Yathā balākāyonimbhi na vijjati pumā   sadā 
 Meghesu gajjamānesu gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti tā sadā 
  
     Cirampi gabbhaṃ dhārenti yāva megho na vassati    
 Bhārato parimuccanti yadā megho pavassati 
  
     Padumuttarabuddhassa dhammameghena gajjato 
 Saddena dhammameghassa dhammagabbhaṃ agaṇhihaṃ 
  
     Satasahassupādāya   puññagabbhaṃ dhatramahaṃ 
 Nappamuñcāmi bhārato dhammameghe   na gajjati   
  
     Yadā tuvaṃ sakyamune ramme kāpilavatthave 
 Gajjasi    dhammameghena bhārato parimuttahaṃ     
  
     Suññataṃ animitataññaca tathāppaṇihitampi    ca 
 Caturo ca phale sabbe dhamme vijanayiṃ ahaṃ    
   Dutiyabhāraṇavāraṃ   
  
   Tāva duraphalaṃ pati the   Devānaṃ bhāsiyā the   Nāhaṃ the   Yaṃ ma   Pumo ma   
 Na vacchati ma gajjati     se the a   Satasahassaṃ upādāya     the   Megho the   
 Vacchati ma    Vaccasi ma gajajito the    Parimuccahaṃ se parimuñcihaṃ the    Athappa 
 se the    Dhammagabbhe vijayāhaṃ the dhamme ca vijaṭāyahaṃ     a 
  
                  
  
     Aparimeyyupādāya patthemi tava sāsanaṃ 
 So me attho anuppatto sannipadamanuttaraṃ 
  
                  
  
     Vinaye pāramiṃ patto yathāpi pāṭhiko   isi 
 Na me samasamo atthi   dhāremi sāsanaṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Vinaye khandhake cāpi tikacchede ca pañcame 
 Ettha me   vimati natthi akkhare vyañajanepi vā 
  
     Niggahe paṭikamme ca ṭhānāṭhāna ca kovido 
 Osāraṇe vuṭṭhāpane sabbattha pāramiṃ gato 
  
     Vinaye khandhake cāpi nikkhipitvā padaṃ ahaṃ 
 Ubhato viniveṭhetvā rasato osareyyahaṃ 
  
     Niruttiyā sukusalo atthānatthe ca kovido 
 Anaññātaṃ mayā natthi ekaggo satthusāsane 
  
     Rūpadakkho ahaṃ ajja sakyaputtasasa sāsane 
 Kaṅkhaṃ sabbaṃ vinodemi chindāmi sabbasaṃsayaṃ 
  
     Padaṃ anupadañcāpi akkharañcāpi vyañajanaṃ   
 Nidāne pariyosāne sabbattha kovido ahaṃ 
  
     Yathāpi rājā balavā niggaṇhitvā parantape    
 Vijinitvāna saṅgāmaṃ nagaraṃ tattha māpaye 
  
     Pākāraṃ parikhañcāpi esikaṃ dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ 
 Aṭṭālake ca vividhe kāraye nagare bahu 
  
     Siṅghāṭakaṃ vaccarañca   suvibhattantarāpaṇaṃ 
 Kārayeyya   sabhaṃ tattha atthānatthavinicchayaṃ 
     Nigghātatthaṃ amittānaṃ chiddāchiddañca jānituṃ 
 Balakāyassarakkhāya   senāpaccaṃ ṭhapeti   so 
  
     Ārakkhatthāya bhaṇḍassa nidhānakusalaṃ naraṃ 
 Mā me bhaṇḍaṃ vinasasiti bhaṇḍarakkhaṃ ṭhapeti    so 
  
   Paṭiko se the pāṭako ma   Na mogho idānatthi the   Ettake the 
    Evaṃ sabbesu    Nihanatvā parakhattiye the   Ovaraṃ ca the   Kāraye so ma   
 Sametuṃ balakāyassa the rakkhāya balakāyassa     se      ṭhapesi ma se the 
  
                  
  
     Māmako   hoti yo rañño vuddhiṃ yasa ca icchati 
 Tassādhikaraṇaṃ deti mittassa paṭipajjituṃ 
  
     Uppātesu nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidaṃ 
 Ajjhāyakaṃ mantadharaṃ porohicce ṭhapeti   so 
  
                  
  
     Etebhaṅgehi sampanno khattiyoti pavuccati 
 Sadā rakkhanti rājānaṃ cakkavākova dukkhitaṃ   
  
     Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra hatāmittova   khattiyo 
 Sadevakassa lokassa dhammarājāti vuccati 
  
     Titthiye nihanitvāna   mārañcāpi sasenakaṃ 
 Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamitvā dhammanagaraṃ amāpayī 
  
     Sīlaṃ pākārakaṃ   tattha ñāṇaṃ te dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ 
 Saddhā te esikā dhira dvārapālo ca saṃvaro 
  
     Satipaṭṭhānamaṭṭālaṃ paññā te vaccaraṃ mute 
 Iddhipādañca siṅghāṭaṃ dhammavithi sumāpitā   
  
     Suttantaṃ abhidhammo   ca vinayo   cā pi kevalaṃ 
 Navaṅgaṃ buddhavacanaṃ esā    dhammasabha tava 
  
     Suññataṃ animittañca appaṇibhitavihārakaṃ    
 Anejaṃ    ca nirodho ca esā dhammakuṭi tava 
  
     Paññāya agganikkhitto    paṭibhāne ca kovido 
 Sāriputtoti nāmena dhammasenāpiti tava 
  
     Cutupapātakusalo iddhiyā pāramiṅgato 
 Kolito nāma nāmona mune tava purobhito    
  
     Porāṇakavaṃsadharo uggatejo durāsado 
 Dhutavādiguṇenaggo    akkhadhasso tavaṃ mune 
  
   Mamattho ma se mamato a samattho te   hapesi ma se the   Dukkhinaṃ ma pakkhinaṃ 
 the   Mahāmittova the   Niharitvāna se a   Pākārikaṃ ma     se   Sumāpitaṃ ma     
   Abhidhammaṃ     ma se 
   Vinayaṃ     ma se    Ettha        Vihārañcappaṇihitaṃ  sabbesu  
    Anejjaṃ the    Aggo ma        Porohicco tavaṃ mune ma     se the    Guṇe aggo 
 ma dhutaṅgādi   the 
  
                  
  
     Bahussuto dhammadharo sabbapāṭhi ca sāsane 
 Ānando nāma nāmena dhammārakkho tavaṃ mune 
  
     Ete sabbe atikkamma pamesi   bhagavā mamaṃ 
 Vinicchayamme pādāsi vinaye   viññudesitaṃ   
  
     Yo koci vinaye pañahaṃ pucchati buddhasāvako 
 Tattha me cittanā natthi taññevatthaṃ kathemahaṃ 
  
     Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvā taṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Vinaye mādiso   natthi kuto bhīyyo bhavissati 
  
                  
  
     Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā evaṃ gajjati gotamo 
 Upālissa samo natthi vinaye khandhakesu ca   
  
     Yāvatā buddhabhanitaṃ navaṅgaṃ satthusāsanaṃ 
 Vinayogadhitaṃ   sabbaṃ vinayamulaṃti passato   
  
     Mama kammaṃ saritvāna gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
     Satasahassupādāya imaṃ ṭhānamapatthayiṃ 
 So me atthā anuppatto vinaye pāramiṅgato 
  
     Sakyānaṃ nandijanano kappako āsahaṃ pure 
 Vijahitvāna   taṃ jātiṃ putto jāto mahesino 
  
     Ito dutiyake kappe añajaso nāma khattiyo 
 Anantatejo amitayaso bhumipālo mahaddhano 
  
     Tassa rañño ahaṃ putto candano   nāma khattiyo 
 Jātimadenupatthaddho yasabhogamadena ca 
  
     Nāgasatasahassāni sababālaṅkārabhusitā 
 Tidhā pabhinnamātaṅgā parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
     Sabalehi parītohaṃ    uyyānaṃ gantukāmako 
 Ārūyha sirikaṃ nāgaṃ nagarā nikkhamiṃ tadā 
  
     Caraṇena ca sampanno guttadvāro susaṃvuto 
 Dovalo nāma sambuddho āgacchi purato mama 
  
     Pesetvā sirikaṃ nāgaṃ budadhaṃ āsādayiṃ tadā 
 Tato sañajātakopo so nago nuddharate    padaṃ 
  
     Nāgaṃ duṭṭhamanaṃ    disvā buddhe kopaṃ akāsahaṃ 
 Vihesayitvā    sambuddhaṃ uyyānaṃ agamāsahaṃ 
  
   Mahesi ma the pihesi       Vinayaṃ ma   Vinayaññunadesitaṃ the 
   Sadiso ma   Vā the   Vinaye kathitaṃ the   Vinaya mulapassino ma    mulakapassino 
 se   Vijayitvāna the   Sunando the    Paretohaṃ     a    Muddharate the    
 Ruṇṇamanaṃ ma se the a 
    Viheṭhayitvā  katthivi  
  
                  
  
     Sātaṃ tattha vindāma siro   pajjalito yathā 
 Pariḷāhena ḍayhāmi macchova baḷisādako 
  
                  
  
     Sasāgarantā paṭhavi ādittā viya hoti me 
 Pitusantikupāgamma idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Āsīvisaṃ va kupitaṃ aggikkhandhaṃva āgataṃ 
 Matataṃva kuñajaraṃ dantiṃ yaṃ sayambhumasādadhiṃ 
  
     Āsādito mayā buddho ghoro ugagatapo jino 
 Purā sabbe vinassāma khamāpessāma taṃ muniṃ 
  
     No ce taṃ nijjhapessāma   attadantaṃ samābhitaṃ 
 Orena sattadivasā   raṭṭhaṃ me vidhamissati 
  
     Sumekhalo kosiyo ca siggavo cāpi sattuko    
 Āsādayitvā isayo duggatā te saraṭṭhakā   
  
     Yadā kuppanti isayo saññatā brahmacārino  
 Sadevakaṃ vināsenti sasāgaraṃ sapabbataṃ  
  
     Tiyojanasahassambhi purise sannipātayiṃ 
 Accayaṃ desanatthāya sayambhuṃ upasaṅkamiṃ 
  
     Alalavatthā allasirā sabbeva pañajali katā 
 Buddhassa pāde nipatitvā idaṃ vacanamabravuṃ    
  
      Khamassu tvaṃ mahāvīra abhiyācati taṃ jano 
 Pariḷāhaṃ vanodehi mā no raṭṭhaṃ vināsaya 
  
     Sadevamānusā sabbe sadānavasarakkhasā 
 Ayomayena kuṭena siraṃ bhindeyyu me sadā   
  
     Udake   aggi na saṇṭhāni khijaṃ selena rūhati 
 Agade kimi na saṇṭhāni kopo buddhe na jāyati 
  
     Yathāpi bhumi acalā appameyyo ca sāgaro 
 Anannako ca ākāso evaṃ buddhā akhobhiyā   
  
     Sadā khantā mahāvīrā khamitā ca tapassino 
 Khantānaṃ khamitānañca gamanaṃ taṃ    na vijjati    
  
   Sire a mu   Nikkhamessāmi the   Sattame divase     the   Sattako ma   Sasenakā 
     the   Brahmacārayo se     the   Mabuviṃ ma     the   Dake ma   Buddho 
 akhobhiyo a ma        Khamanaṃ vo the 
  
                  
  
     Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho pariḷāhaṃ vinodayaṃ   
 Mahājanassa purato nabhaṃ abbhuggami tadā 
  
                  
  
     Tena kammenahaṃ dhira bhinattataṃ ajjhupāgato 
 Samatikkamma taṃ jātiṃ pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ 
  
     Tadāpi maṃ mahāvīra ḍayahamānaṃ susaṇṭhitaṃ   
 Pariḷāhaṃ vinodesi sayambhuñca khamāpayi 
  
     Ajjāpi maṃ mahāvīra ḍayahmānaṃ tihaggihi 
 Nibbāpesi tayo aggi sitibhāvañca pāpiyī 
  
     Yesaṃ sotāvadhānatthi   suṇātha mama bhāsato 
 Atthaṃ tumhaṃ pavakkhāmi yathā diṭṭhaṃ padaṃ mama 
  
     Sayambhuṃ taṃ vimānetvā   santacittaṃ samāhitaṃ 
 Tena kammenahaṃ ajja jātomhi nicayotiyaṃ 
  
     Mā vo khaṇaṃ virādhetha khaṇātītā hi socare 
 Sadatthe vāyameyyātha khaṇo vo paṭipādito 
  
     Ekaccānañca vamanaṃ ekaccānaṃ virecanaṃ 
 Visaṃ halāhalaṃ eke   ekaccānaṃ va osadhaṃ 
  
     Vamanaṃ paṭipapannānaṃ phalaṭṭhānaṃ virecanaṃ 
 Osadhaṃ phalalābhinaṃ puññakkhettaṃ gavesitaṃ 
  
     Sāsanena viruddhānaṃ visaṃ hālāhalaṃ yathā 
 Āsiviso diṭṭhiviso evaṃ jhāpeti taṃ naraṃ 
  
     Sakiṃ pitaṃ   halāhalaṃ uparundhati jīvitaṃ 
 Sāsanena virujjhitvā kappakoṭimbhi ḍayhati 
  
     Khantiyā avihiṃsāya mettacittavatāya ca 
 Sadevakaṃ so tāreti   tasmā vo avirodhiyo   
  
     Lābhālābhe na sajjanti sammanana   vimānane 
 Paṭhavisadisā buddhā tasmā te na virodhiyā   
  
   Vinodayī se     the    Evaṃ sabbattha    Sotapathā atthi the 
   Khamāpetvā the   Ete       Sakiṃ bhuttaṃ the   Tarati ma     se   Avirādhiyā ma 
   Virādhiyā     ma 
  
                  
  
     Devadatte ca vadhake vore aṅgulimālake 
 Dhanapāle rāhule ca sabbesaṃ samako muni 
  
                  
  
     Etesaṃ paṭigho   natthi rāgoseṃ na vijjati 
 Sabbesaṃ samako buddho vadhakassorasassa ca 
  
     Panthe disvāna kāsāvaṃ chaḍḍhinaṃ miḷhamakkhitaṃ 
 Sirasmiṃ   añjaliṃ katvā vanditabbaṃ iḍasiddhajaṃ  
     Abbhatitā ca ye buddhā vattamānā anāgatā 
 Dhajenānena sujjhanti tasmā ete namassiyā 
  
     Satthukappaṃ suvinayaṃ dhāremi hadayenahaṃ 
 Namasasmāno vinayaṃ viharissāmi sabbadā 
  
     Vinayo āsayo   mayhaṃ vinayo ṭhānacaṅkamaṃ 
 Kappami vinaye vāsaṃ vinayo mayha gocaro 
  
     Vinaye pāramippatto samathe   cāpi kovido 
 Upāli taṃ mahāvīra pade vandati satthuno 
  
     So ahaṃ vicarissāmi gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ 
 Namasasmāno sambuddheṃ dhammassa ca sudhammataṃ 
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā   natthi dāni punabbhavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upālithero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Upālittherāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
   Aññākoṇḍaññattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumutatrasambuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ vināyakaṃ 
 Buddhabhumimanuppattaṃ paṭhamaṃ addasaṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Yāvatā bodhiyā yakkhā sabbe samāgatā 
 Sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vandanti pañajalikatā 
  
                  
  
     Sabbe devā tuṭṭhamanā ākāse sañcaranti te 
  Buddho ayaṃ anuppatto andhakāratamonudo  
  
   Paṭighaṃ ma     se a   Sirasā se the   Canditabbo isiddhajo the   Āsayaṃ     the   
 Samaye the   Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo ma 
  
                  
  
     Tesaṃ hāsaparetānaṃ mahānādo pavattatha 
  Kilese jhāpayissāmi sammāsambuddhasāsane  
  
     Devānaṃ giramaññāya vācāsabhimudiritaṃ 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ādibhikkhamadāsahaṃ 
  
     Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro 
 Devasaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Sattāhaṃ abhinikkhamma bodhiṃ ajjhagamaṃ ahaṃ 
 Idaṃ me paṭhamaṃ bhattaṃ brahmacariyassa   yāpanaṃ 
  
     Tusitā hi idhāgantvā yo me bhikkhaṃ upānayī 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
     Tiṃsakappasahassāni   devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Sabbe deve abhibhotvā tidivaṃ āvasissati 
  
     Devalokā civitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Sahassadhā cakkavatti tattha rajjaṃ karissati 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tidasā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Agārā pabbajitvāna chabbassāni vasisasti 
  
     Tato sattamake vasse buddho saccaṃ kathessati 
 Koṇḍaññā nāma nāmena paṭhamaṃ sacchikābhiti  
  
     Nikkhantenānupabbajiṃ   padhānaṃ sukataṃ mayā 
 Kilese jhāpanatthāya pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
     Abhigantvāna sabbaññu buddho loke sadevake 
 Isināme   migāraññe amataṃ bherimāhahani 
  
     Sodāni patto amataṃ santaṃ padamanuttaraṃ 
 Sababāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
                  
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aññā  koṇḍaññā thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Añña koṇḍaññattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
   Brahmacārissa ma the     brahmacariya se   Sahassena     tiṃsamatte kappasahasse 
 ma se   Pabbajjaṃ       Imināme ma     se   Aññāta a mu aññā si mu 
  
                  
  
   Piṇḍolabhāradvājattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Purato himavantassa cittakuṭe vasi tadā 
  
     Abhitarūpo tatthāsiṃ migarājā catukkamo 
 Yassa saddaṃ suṇitvāna vikkhambhanti bahujjanā 
  
     Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha upagañajiṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Vuṭṭhitassa samādhimhā buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
     Catuddisā namassitvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ naruttamaṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā sihanādaṃ nadiṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Padamuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Sakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
     Buddhassa giramaññāya sabbe devā samāgatā 
 Āgato vadataṃ seṭṭho dhammaṃ sossāma 
  
     Tesaṃ hāsaparetānaṃ purato lokanāyako 
 Mama saddhaṃ pakittesi dighadassi mahāmuni 
  
      Yenidaṃ padumaṃ dinnaṃ sihanādo ca nādito 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
     Ito aṭṭhamake kappe cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Sattaratanasampanno catudipambhi issaro 
  
     Kārayissati issariyaṃ   mahiyā catusaṭṭhiyā   
 Padumo nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
                  
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamonāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Pakāsite pāvacane brahmabandhu bhavissati 
 Brahmaññā abhinikkhamma pabbajissati tāvade 
  
     Padhānapabhitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
     Vipane pannaseyyambhi vāḷamigasamākule 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo  
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ  
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piṇḍolabhāradvā thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Piṇḍolabharadvājattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Issaraṃ ma     se   Catusattiyā a mu  theragāthaṭṭhakathāya na sametidaṃ apadānaṃ 
  
                  
  
   Khidiravaniyarevatattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Gaṅgā bhagirathi   nāma himavantā pabhāvitā    
 Kutitthe   nāviko āsiṃ orime ca tariṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Pubbe mayhaṃ sutaṃ āsi padumuttaranāyako   
 Vasīsatasahassehi gaṅgāsotaṃ tarissati   
  
     Bahu nāvā samānetvā vaḍḍhakihi susuṅkhataṃ 
 Nāvāya chadanaṃ katvā patimāniṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
     Āgantvāna ca sambuddho āruhi tañca nāvukaṃ   
 Vārimajjhe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
      Yo so tāresi sambuddhaṃ saṅghañcāpi anāvaṃ 
 Tena cittappasādena devaloke ramissati 
  
     Nibbattissati te vyambhaṃ sukataṃ nāvasaṇṭhitaṃ 
 Ākāse pupphachadanaṃ dhārayissati sabbadā 
  
     Aṭṭhapaññāsakappambhi tārako   nāma khattiyo 
 Cāturanto vijitāvi cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
                  
  
     Sattapaññāsakappambhi campako nāma khattiyo 
 Uggacchantova suriyo jotissati mahabbalo 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tidasā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Revato nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati 
  
     Agārā nikkhamitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhaghavato sāsāne pabbajissati 
  
     So pacchā pabbajitvāna yuttayogo vipasasako   
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo  
  
     Ciriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
     Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayī mama  
  
     Tato maṃ vananirataṃ  disvā lokantagu muni 
 Vanavāsibhikkhunaggaṃ    paññapesi mahāmati   
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khadiravaniyo revato thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Khadiravaniyarevatattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
   Bhāgirasi ma     se   Pabhūtā bhimavantato the   Titthassa the   Padumuttaranāyako 
 sambuddho dipaduttemo ma     a   Gaṅgātiramupāgato ma the   Nāvālañachakaṃ
