 Nerū nagānaṃ pavaro siluccayo 
 Tatheva ye cittavasena vattare 
 Na buddhañāṇassa kalaṃ upenti te 
  
      Dhamme vidhiṃ   ṭhapevona buddho kāruṇiko isi 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo so ñāṇaṃ pakittesi buddhambhi lokanāyako 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ na gamissati   
  
      Kilese jhāpayitvāna ekaggo susamābhito 
 Sobhito nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako  
  
   Te sisse simu   Pāyasogandha machasaṃ   Vācāsabhimudiritaṃ simu machasaṃ   
 Dhammavidhiṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Paññase kappasahasse sattevāsuṃ yasuggatā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbesamuhatā    
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sobhito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sobhitattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Sudassanattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vitatthānadiyā   tīre pilakkho   phalito ahu 
 Tāhaṃ rukkhaṃ gavesanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Kenakaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā vaṇṭe chetvanāhaṃ tadā 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno 
  
      Yena ñāṇena pattosi accutaṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
 Taṃ ñāṇaṃ abhipujemi buddhaseṭṭha mahāmuni 
  
      Ñāṇambhi pujaṃ katvāna pilakkhaṃ   addasaṃ ahaṃ 
 Paṭiladdhombhi taṃ paññaṃ   ñāṇapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ñāṇapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito terasakappambhi dvādasāsuṃ phaluggatā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sudassano thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sudassanattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Candanapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kinnaro tadā 
 Pupphabhakkho cahaṃ āsiṃ pupphanivasano tathā   
  
      Atthadassi tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭhā narāsabho 
 Vipanaggena   niyyāsi haṃsarājāva ambare 
  
       Namo te purisājañña cittaṃ te suvisodhitaṃ 
 Pasannamukhanettosi   vippasannamukhindriyo 
  
   Samuggatā     se   Vitthatāyanadi     cintā machasaṃ simu vitthatāya syā   
 Pilakkhu machasaṃ   Pilakkhuṃ machasaṃ   Saññaṃ     se syā   Cahaṃ     se   
 Pācanaggena     se   Mukhavaṇṇesi     se 
  
                   
  
      Orohatvāna ākāsā bhuripañño sumedhaso 
 Saṅghāṭiṃ pattharitvāna pallaṅkena upāvisi 
  
      Valinaṃ candanādāya agamāsiṃ jinantikaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Abhivādetvāna sambuddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Pāmojjaṃ janayitavona sakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate candanaṃ yaṃ apūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Catuddase kappasate ito āsiṃsu te tayo 
 Rohitā   nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā candanapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Candanapujakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
   Aṭṭhamabhāṇavāraṃ   
  
                   
  
     Pupphachadaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sunando nāma nāmena buhmaṇo mantapāragu 
 Ajjhāyako yājayogo   vājapeyyaṃ ayājayī 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu aggo kāruṇiko isi 
 Janataṃ anukampanetā ambare caṅkami tadā 
  
      Caṅkamitvāna sambuddho sabbaññu lokanāyako 
 Metatāya aphari satte appamāṇaṃ nirūpadhi 
  
      Vaṇṭe chetvāna pupphini brāhmaṇo mantapāragu 
 Sabbe sisse samanetvā ākase ukkhipāpayi 
  
      Yāvatā nagaraṃ āsi pupphānaṃ chadanaṃ tadā 
 Buddhassa ānubhāvena sattāhaṃ na vigacchatha 
  
      Teneva sukkamūlena anubhotvāna sampadā 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya tiṇṇo loke visattikaṃ 
  
      Ekādase kappasate pañcatiṃsāsu khattiyā 
 Ambaraṃsa sanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pupphajadaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pupphachadaniyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Rohaṇi machasaṃ     so   Yācayogo machasaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappeyaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pāyāsassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekatāḷisito kappe buddho nāmāsi khattiyo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāyāsadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pasāyadāyakottherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
     Rahosaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassāvidure vasabho nāma pabbato 
 Tasmiṃ pabbatapādamhi assamo āsi māpito 
  
      Tīṇi sissasahassāni vācesiṃ brāhmaṇo   tadā 
 Saṃharitavona   te sisse ekamantaṃ upāvisiṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekamantaṃ nisīditvā brāhmaṇo mantapāragu 
 Buddhavedaṃ   gavesanto ñāṇe cittaṃ pasādayīṃ 
  
      Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā nisīdiṃ paṇṇasatthare 
 Pallaṅkamābhujitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ñāṇasaññayidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattavisatikappambhi   rājā siridharo ahuṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rahosaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Rahosaññakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Campakapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
 Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā osadhiṃ viya tārakaṃ 
  
      Tayo māṇavakā āsuṃ sake sippe susikkhitā 
 Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna anventi mama pacchato 
  
      Puṭake satta pupphāni nikkittāni tapassinā 
 Gahetvā tāni ñāṇambhi vessabhussā hiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ñāṇapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekunataṃse kappambhi vipulābha sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā campakapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Campakapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
   Brāhmaṇe   Saṃsāvevona     se sāsāvitvāna syā   Buddhavesaṃ     se   
 Sattavisamahi kappamahi     se 
                   
  
     Atthasandassakettharāpadānaṃ 
  
      Visālamāle āsino addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Khiṇāsavaṃ khalappattaṃ bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ 
  
      Satasahassā tevijjā chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā 
 Parivārenti sambuddhaṃ ko disvā nappasidati 
  
      Ñāṇe upanidhā yassa na vijjati sadevake 
 Anantañāṇaṃ sambuddaṃ ko disvā nappasidati 
  
      Dhammakāyañca dipentaṃ kevalaṃ ratanākaraṃ 
 Vikopetuṃ   na sakkonti ko disvā nappasidati 
  
      Imāhi tihi gāthāhi nārado saragacchiyo    
 Padumuttaraṃ thavitvāna sambuddhaṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Tena cittappasādena buddhasanthavanena ca 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ   
  
      Ito tiṃse kappasate sumitto nāma khattiyo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā atthasandassako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Atthasandassakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Ekapasādaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nārado iti me nāmaṃ kesavo iti maṃ vidu 
 Kusalāsalaṃ esaṃ agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃ 
  
      Mettacitto kāruṇiko atthadassi mahāmuni 
 Assāsayanto satte so dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā 
  
      Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Satthāraṃ abhivādetvā pakkāmiṃ pācināmukho 
  
      Sattarase kappasate rājā āsiṃ mahipati 
 Amittatāpano nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapasādaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Hakapasādaniyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Vikappetuṃ machasaṃ   Nāradavahaya vacachalo machasaṃ   Nupapajjatha simu 
  
                   
  
      Migarājā tadā āsiṃ abhijāto sukesari 
 Giriduggaṃ gavesanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Ayaṃ nukho mahāvīro nibbāpeti mahājanaṃ 
 Yannunāhaṃ upāseyyeṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
      Sākhaṃ sālassa bhañajitvā sakosaṃ   pupphamāhariṃ 
 Upāgantvāna sambuddhaṃ adāsiṃ pupphamuttamaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiroyiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca navame kappe virācana sanāmakā 
 Tayo āsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sālapupphadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sālapupphadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Piyālaphadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Pārādhako   tadā āsiṃ parapāṇuparodhako    
 Pabbhāre seyyaṃ kappemi avidūre sikhisatthuno 
  
      Sāyaṃ pātañca passāmi buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ 
 Deyyadhammo ca me nathi dipadindassa tādino 
  
                   
  
      Piyāpaphalamādāya agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃ 
 Paṭiggahesi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
  
      Tato paraṃ upādāya parivāraṃ   vināyakaṃ 
 Tena cittappasādena tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ ahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito paṇṇarase kappe tayo āsuṃ piyālito 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piyālaphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Piyālaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
   Sobhitavaggo cuddasamo   
  
   Sakoṭaṃ       Pārāvato simu parādhako       Paramānuparodhako     se   
 Paricāriṃ simu 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Sobhitota sudassato ca candano pupphachadano 
 Rabho campakapupphi ca atthasandassakena ca 
 Ekapasādi   sāladado dasamo phaladāyako 
 Gāthāyo sattati dve ca gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi 
   Sobhitavaggo cuddasamo   
  
     Atichattiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Parinibbute bhagavati atthadassanaruttame 
 Chattānichattaṃ   kāretvā thupambhi abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Kālena kālaṃ āgantvā namassiṃ satthu cetiyaṃ   
 Pupphacchadanaṃ katvāna chattamhi abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Sattarase kappasate devarajjaṃ akārayiṃ 
 Manussattaṃ na gacchāmi thupapujāyi daṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā atichattiyo   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Atichattiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Thambhāropakattherāpadanaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi dhammadassinarāsabhe 
 Āropesiṃ dhajatthamhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa cetiye 
  
      Nisseṇiṃ māpayitvāna thupaseṭṭhaṃ samāruhiṃ 
 Jātipupphaṃ gahetvāna thupamahi abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Aho buddho dhammo aho no satthusampadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thupapujāyi daṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe thupasikharanāmakā 
 Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā thambhāropako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Thambhāropakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Ekadussi     se syā   Chattādhichattaṃ simu   Lokanāyakaṃ     se machasaṃ   
 Adhichattiyo simu 
  
                   
  
     Vedikārakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi piyadassi naruttame 
 Pasannacitto sumano muttāvedimakāsahaṃ 
  
      Maṇihi paravāretvā akāsiṃ vedimuttamaṃ 
 Vedikāya mahaṃ katvā tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Maṇi dhārenti ākāse puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Soḷaseto kappasate maṇippabhāsanāmakā 
 Khattiṃsāsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vedikārako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Vedikārakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Saparivāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Jalitvā aggikkhandhova sambuddho parinibbuto 
  
      Nibbute ca mahāvire thupo vitthāriko ahu 
 Ahorattaṃ   upaṭṭhenti dhātugehe varuttame 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano akaṃ candanavedikaṃ 
 Diyati dhumakkhandho ca   thupānucchavikotadā 
  
      Bhave nibbattamānambhi devatte atha mānuse 
 Omattaṃ me na passāmi pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pañcadase kappasate ito aṭṭhajanā ahu 
 Sabbe samattanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saparivāriyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saparivāriyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Ummāpupphiyatherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi  ahutinaṃ paṭiggahe 
 Siddhatthambhi bhagavati mahāthupamaho ahu 
  
      Mahe pavattamānambhi siddhatthassa mahesino 
 Ummāpupphaṃ gahetvāna thupamhi abhiropayiṃ 
  
   Duratova machasaṃ thapadattaṃ se syā   Dissati thupakkhandho katthaci  lokambhite 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi thupapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca navame kappe somadevasanāmakā 
 Pañcāsitisu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ummāpupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ummāpupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Anulopadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Anomadassimunino bodhivedimakāsahaṃ 
 Sudhāya piṇḍaṃ datvāna pātikammamakāya haṃ   
  
      Disvā taṃ sukataṃ kammaṃ anomadassi naruttamo 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Iminā sudhākammena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna dukkhassantaṃ karissati   
  
      Pasanna mukhavaṇṇomhi ekaggo susamāhito 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Ito kappasate āsiṃ paripuṇṇe anunake 
 Rājā sabbaghano nāma cakakvatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā anulepadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Anulepadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Maggadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Uttaritvāna nadikaṃ vanaṃ gacchati cakkhumā 
 Tamaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ siddhatthaṃ varalakkhaṇaṃ 
  
      Kudadāpaliṭakamādāya samaṃ katvānataṃ pathaṃ 
 Satthāraṃ abhivādevo sakaṃ cittaṃ padādayiṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakāriṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi maggadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattapaññāsakappamhi eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Nāmena suppabuddhoti nāyako so narissaro 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maggadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Maggadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Pāṇikammaṃ machasaṃ phātikammaṃ aṭṭhakathā 
  
                   
                   
  
     Phalakakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Yānakāro pure dārukamme susikkhito 
 Candanaṃ palakaṃ kavo adāsiṃ lokabandhuno 
  
      Pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ suvaṇṇassa sunimmitaṃ 
 Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ dibbayānaṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ 
  
      Pāsādā sivikā ceva nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ 
 Akkhohaṃ atanaṃ mayhaṃ phalakassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekatanavute ito kappe phalakaṃ yamahaṃ dadiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phalakassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattapaññāsakappambhi caturo nimamitacahayā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phalakadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Phalakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Vaṭaṃsakiyattherāpadanaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma nāmena sayambhu aparājito 
 Vivekamanubrūhanto ajjhogāhi mahāvanaṃ 
  
      Sallaṃ puppitaṃ disvā ganthitvāna   vaṭaṃsakaṃ 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sammukhā lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassambhi yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ūnavise kappasate soḷasāsiṃsu nimamitā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vaṭaṃsakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Vaṭaṃsakiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Pallaṅkadāyakattherāpadanaṃ 
  
      Sumedhassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Pallaṅko hi mayā dinno sauttara sapacchado 
  
      Sattaratanasampanno pallaṅko āsi so tadā 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya nibbattati sadā mama 
  
   Bandhitvāna simu 
  
                   
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassambhi pallaṅkamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pallaṅkassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Visakappasahassambhi suvaṇṇābhā tayo janā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pallaṅkadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pallaṅkadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Chattaṃ thambho ca vedi ca parivārummapupphiyo 
 Anulepo maggadāyī phalakadāyi vaṭaṃsako 
 Pallaṅkadāyī gāthāyo chapaññāsa pakittititā 
   Chattavaggo paṇṇarasamo   
  
     Bandhujīvakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candaṃva vimalaṃ sudadhaṃ vippasannamanāvilaṃ 
 Nandibhavaparikkhiṇaṃ tiṇṇaṃ loke visattikaṃ 
  
      Nibbāpayantaṃ janataṃ tiṇṇaṃ tārayataṃ varaṃ   
 Vanasmiṃ jhāyamānaṃ taṃ ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ 
  
      Bandhujīvakapupphāni laggetvā suttakenahaṃ  
 Budadhassa abhiropesiṃ sibino lokabandhuno 
  
                   
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammakāriṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito sattamake kappe manujindo brabhāyaso 
 Samattacakkhu nāmāsiṃ cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bandhujīvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bandhujīvakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Muniṃ     se syā   Suttake agaṃ simu 
  
                   
  
     Tambapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Parakammāyane yutto aparādhaṃ akāsahaṃ 
 Vanannaṃ atidhāvissaṃ bhayabheravasamappito 
  
      Pupphitaṃ pādapaṃ disvā piṇḍibaddhaṃ sunimmitaṃ 
 Tambapupphaṃ gahetvāna bodhiyaṃ okiriṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Gatamaggaṃ gavesanto āgacchuṃ mama santikaṃ 
 Te ca disvānahaṃ tathe ācajjaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
  
      Canditvā ca ahaṃ bodhiṃ vippasannena cetasā 
 Anekatāle papatiṃ giridugge bhayānake 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayi 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhijujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca tatiye kappe rājā susaññato   ahaṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tambapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tambapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Vithisammajjakattherāpādanaṃ 
  
      Udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva pitaraṃsiṃva   bhānumaṃ 
 Paṇṇarase yathā candaṃ niyyantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhasaṭṭhisahassāni sabbe khiṇāsavā ahu 
 Parivāriṃsu sambuddhaṃ dipadindaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
      Sammajjitvāna taṃ vithiṃ niyante lokanāyake 
 Ussāpesiṃ dhajaṃ tathe vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Ekatavute ito kappe yaṃ dhajaṃ abhiroyiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito catutthake kappe rājābhosiṃ mahabbalo 
 Sabbākārena sambanno sudhajo iti vissuto 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vithisammajjako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Vithisammajjakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
   Samphusito ahuṃ simu   Sitaraṃsiṃva simu 
  
                   
  
     Kakkārupujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Devaputto aśaṃ santo pujayiṃ sikhināyakaṃ 
 Kakkārupupphaṃ saggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphambhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca namame kappe rājā sattuntamo ahuṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kakkārupujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kakkārupujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Mandāravapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Devaputto ahaṃ santo pujesiṃ sikhināyakaṃ 
 Mandāravena pupphena buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Sattāhaṃ chadanaṃ āsi dibbaṃ mālyaṃ tathāgate 
 Sabbe janā samāgantvā namassiṃsu tathāgataṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca dasame kappe rājāhosiṃ punindharo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mandāravapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mandāravapujakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Kadambapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre kukkuṭo nāma pabbato 
 Tamhi pabbatapādamhi sattabuddhā vasanti te 
  
      Kadambaṃ pupaphitaṃ disvā diparājāṃva uggataṃ 
 Ubhohatthebhi paggayha sattabuddhe samokiriṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ   
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhajāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dve navute ito kappe sattāsuṃ pupphanāmakā  
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kadambapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kadambapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
   Mahipujayiṃ     se   Thullanāyakā     
  
                   
                   
  
     Tiṇasulakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre bhūtagaṇo nāma pabbato 
 Vasateko jino tattha sayambhu lokanissaṭo 
  
      Tiṇasule gahetvāna buddhasa abhiropayiṃ 
 Ekunasatasabhassaṃ kappaṃ   na vinipātiko 
  
      Ito ekādase kappe ekosiṃ dharaṇiruho 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇasulako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiṇasulakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Nāgapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sacaccho nāma nāmena brāhmaṇo mantapāragu 
 Purakkhato sasissehi vasati pabbatantare 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma ji āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
      Vehāsambhi caṅkamati dhupeti   jalate tathā 
 Hāsaṃ mama viditvāna   pakkāmi pācināmukho 
  
      Tañca acchariyaṃ disvā abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ 
 Nāgapupphaṃ gahetvāna gatamaggamhi okiriṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ pupphaṃ ekiriṃ ahaṃ  
 Tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse kappasate   rājā āsiṃ mahāratho 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāgapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nāgapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sahassaṃ kappānaṃ     se sahassakappaṃ simu   Dhupāya machasaṃ   Disvāna 
       Pupphamabhiropayiṃ       Ekaniṃse ito kappe syā 
  
                   
                   
  
     Punnāgapupphiyatthorāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kānanaṃ vanamogayha vasāmi luddako ahaṃ 
 Punnāgaṃ pupaphitaṃ disvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ 
  
      Taṃ pupphaṃ vicinitvāna sugandhaṃ gandhitaṃ subhaṃ 
 Thupaṃ karitvāna puline buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Dve navute ato kappe yaṃ pupphamaśipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekamhi navute kappe eko āsiṃ tamonudo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā punnāgapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Punānāgapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Kumudadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre mahājātassaro ahu 
 Padumupapalasañachanno puṇḍarikasamotthaṭo   
  
      Kukuttho   nāma nāmena tatthāsiṃ sakuṇo tadā 
 Silavā buddhisampanno puññāpuññesu kovido 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Jātassarassāvidure sañcarittha mahāmuni 
  
      Jalajaṃ kumudaṃ chetvā   upanesiṃ mahesino 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya paṭiggahi mahāmuni 
  
      Tañca dānaṃ daditvāhaṃ sukkamūlena codito 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Soḷaseto kappasate āsuṃ varuṇanāmakā 
 Aṭṭha ete janādhipā cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kumudadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kumudadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
   Samotato     se   Kakudho     se   Gahetvā     
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Bandhujīvo tambapupphi vithi kakkārupupphiyo 
 Mandāravo kadambi ca sulako nāgapupphiyo 
 Punnāgo komudi gāthā chappaññāsa pakittitāti 
   Bandhujīvakavaggo soḷasamo   
  
     Supāricariyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumo nāma nāmena dipadindo narāsabho 
 Pavanā abhinikkhamma dhamamaṃ desesi cakkhumā 
  
      Yakkhānaṃ samayo āsi avidūre mahesino 
 Yena kiccena sampattā ajjhāpekkhiṃsu tāvade 
  
      Buddhassa giramaññāya amatassa ca desanaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano apphoṭhatvā   upaṭṭhahiṃ 
  
      Suciṇṇassa phalaṃ passa upaṭṭhānassa satthuno 
 Tiṃsakappasahassesu duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Ūnatiṃse kappasate samalaṅkatanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā supāricariyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Supāricariyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
     Kaṇaverapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sidudhattho nāma bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Purakkhato sāvakehi nagaraṃ paṭipajajatha 
  
      Rañño antepure āsiṃ gopako abhisammato 
 Pāsāde upaviṭṭhohaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Kaṇaveraṃ gahetvāna bhikkhusaṃghe samokiriṃ 
 Buddhassa visuṃ katvāna tato bhayyo samākiriṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayi   
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattāsitimhito kappe caturo āsuṃ mahiddhikā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṇaverapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kaṇaverapupphayattherassa apadānaṃ ditiyaṃ   
   Apphoṭhetvāna se   Pupphamabhipūjayiṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Khajjakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tissassa kho bhagato pube phalamadāsahaṃ 
 Nāḷikekarañca pādāsiṃ khajjakaṃ abhisammataṃ 
  
      Buddhassa tamahaṃ datvā tissassa tu mahesino 
 Modāmahaṃ kāmakari upapajjiṃ yadicchakaṃ   
  
      Dve navute ito pappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito terasakappambhi rājā indasamo ahuṃ  
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khajjakadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Khajjakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Desapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Atthadassi tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Abbhuggantvāna vehāsaṃ gacchate anilañajase 
  
      Yamhi dese ṭhito satthā abbhuggañachi mahāmuni 
 Tāhaṃ desaṃ apūjesiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate addasaṃ yaṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi desapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekādase kappasate gosujāta sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā desapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Desapujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
   Yamicchakaṃ simu   Ahu simu 
  
                   
  
     Kaṇikāracchadaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vessabhu nāma sambuddho lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Divāvihārāya muni obhāhittha   mahāvanaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃ ocinitvā chattaṃ katvānahaṃ tadā 
 Pupphacchadanaṃ katvāna buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito visatikappamhi soṇṇābhā aṭṭhakhattiyā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhame 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṇikāracchadaniyo   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kaṇikāracchadaniya  ttherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
                   
  
     Sappidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Phusso nāmātha bhagavā āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Gacchate vithiyaṃ viro nibbāpento mahājanaṃ 
  
      Anupubbena bhagavā āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
 Tatohaṃ   pattaṃ paggayha sappitelaṃ adāsahaṃ 
  
      Dve navute ito kappe yaṃ sappimadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Chappaññāse ito kappe eko āsiṃ samodako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sappidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sappidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Yuthikāpupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānaditire anusotaṃ vajāmahaṃ 
 Sayambhuṃ addasaṃ tattha sālarājaṃva phullitaṃ  
  
      Pupphaṃ yuthikamādāya upagacchiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
   Ogāhayi machasaṃ ogāyitvā       Chattiyo machasaṃ   Chattiya machasaṃ   Tato 
 taṃ machasaṃ   Pupphitaṃ     
  
                   
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Sattavisatikappambhito kappe eko samuddharo ahuṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yuthikāpupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
  Yuthikāpupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Dussadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tivarāyaṃ pure ramme rājaputto ahaṃ tadā 
 Paṇṇākāraṃ labhitvāna upasantassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Adhivāsesi bhagavā vatthaṃ hatthena āmasi 
 Siddhattho adhivasetvā vehāsaṃ kabhamuggami 
  
      Buddhassa gacchamānassa dussā dhāvanti pacchato 
 Tattha cittaṃ pāsādesuṃ buddho no aggapuggalo 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃdu ssamaddiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattasaṭṭhimbhito kappe cakkavatti tadā ahaṃ 
 Parisuddhoti nāmena manujindo mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dusasadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dussadāyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Samādapakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare bandhumatiyā mahāpugagaṇo ahu 
 Tesāhaṃ pavaro āsiṃ mama baddhavarā ca te 
  
      Te sabbe sannipātetvā puññakamme samādayiṃ 
 Mālaṃ kassāma saṅghassa puññakkhettamanuttaraṃ 
  
      Sādhuti te paṭissutvā mama chandavasānugā 
 Niṭṭhāpesuṃ   ca taṃ mālaṃ vipassissa adamhase 
  
   Niṭṭhāpetvā simu 
  
                   
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ māpamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi māladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekunasaṭṭhikappambhi   eko āsi janādhipe 
 Ādeyyo nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā samādapako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Samādapakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Pañcaṅguliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tisso nāmāsi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Pavisantaṃ gandhakuṭiṃ vihārakusalaṃ muniṃ 
  
      Sugandhamālamādāya agamāsiṃ jinantikaṃ 
 Appasaddova sambuddhe pañcaṅgulimadāsahaṃ 
  
      Dve navute ito kappe yaṃ gandhamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pañcaṅgulissidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dve sattatimbhito kappe rājā āsi samodabho 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcaṅguliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcaṅguliyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Supāricāri kaṇaveri khajjako desapujako 
 Kaṇikāro sappidado yuthiko dussadāyako 
 Mālo ca pañcaṅguliko catupaññāsa gāthakāti 
   Supāricariyavaggo sattarasamo   
  
     Kumudamāliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Pabbate himavantamhi mahājātassaro ahu 
 Tatthajo rakkhaso āsiṃ ghorarūpo mahabbalo 
  
      Kumudaṃ pupphate tathe cakkamattāni jāyare 
 Ovināmi ca ta ṃpupphaṃ khalito samiti tadā 
  
   Ekunasattatikappe machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Atthadassī tu bhagavā dipadindo narāsabho 
 Pupphaṃ samocitaṃ disvā āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
      Upāgatañca sambuddhaṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Saṅgamma pupphaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Yāvatā himavantantā parisā sā tadā ahu 
 Tāvacchadanasampanno agamāsi tathāgato 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito paṇṇarase kappe sattābhasuṃ janādhipā 
 Sahassarathanāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kumudamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
  Kumudamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Nisseṇidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Koṇḍaññassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Ārohatthāya pāsādaṃ nisseṇi kāritā mayā 
  
      Tena citatappasādena anubhovona sampadā 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Ekaniṃsambhi kappānaṃ sahassamhi tayo ahu 
 Sambahulā nāma rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nisseṇidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nisseṇidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Rattipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ 
 Vipassiṃ addasaṃ buddhaṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
      Rattikaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā kuṭajaṃ dharaniruhaṃ 
 Samulaṃ paggahetvāna upanesiṃ mahesino 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ito ca aṭṭhame kappe suppasantasanāmako 
 Sattarananasampanno rājāhosiṃ mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rattipupphiya thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Rattiyapphiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Udapānadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vipassino bhagavato udapāno kato mayā 
 Piṇḍapātañca datvānana niyyātesiṃ ahaṃ tadā 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kamammakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi udapānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udapānadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Udapānadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Sihāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi padumuttaranāyake 
 Pasannacitto sumano sihāsanamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Pahutagandhamālehi   diṭṭhadhamme sukhāvahe 
 Tattha pujaṃ karitvāna   nibbāyati bahujjano 
  
                   
  
      Pasannacitto sumano vanditvā bodhimuttamaṃ 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
      Paṇṇarasasahassamhi kappānaṃ aṭṭha āsu te   
 Siluccaya sanāmā ca rājāno cakkavattino 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sihāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sihāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
   Bahuhi gandhamālehi machasaṃ   Pujañca katvāna machasaṃ   Āsuno se 
  
                   
  
     Maggadattikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Anomadassī bhagavā dipadindo narāsabho 
 Diṭṭhadhammasukhatthāya abbhokāsambhi caṅkami 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano canditvā pupphamokiriṃ 
 Uddhate pāde pupphāni sisamuddhani   tiṭṭhare 
  
      Visakappasahassambhi ito pañca janā ahu 
 Pupphacchadaniyā nāma cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maggadattiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Maggadattikattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Ekadipiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarassa munino salalo bodhimuttame 
 Pasannacitto sumano ekadipaṃ adāsahaṃ 
  
      Bhave nibabattamānambhi nibbatte puññasañcaye 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Soḷasakappasahasse ito te caturo janā 
 Candābhā nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekadipiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekadipiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Navamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ   
  
                   
  
     Muṇipujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Orena himavantassa nadikā   sampavattatha 
 Tassā cānupakhettambhi sayambhu vasate tadā 
  
      Maṇiṃ paggayha pallaṅkaṃ sādhucittaṃ manoramaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Catunavuto ito kappe yaṃ maṇi abhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca dvādase kappe sataraṃsi sanāmakā 
 Aṭṭha te āsuṃ rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maṇipujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Maṇipujakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sohaṃ mudadhati simu   Nadekā so 
  
                   
  
     Tikicchakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare bandhumatiyā vejjo āsiṃ susikkhito 
 Āturānaṃ sadukkhānaṃ mahājanasukhāvaho   
  
      Vyādhitaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā silavantaṃ mahājutiṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano bhesajjamadadiṃ tadā 
  
      Arogo āsi teneva samaṇo saṃvutindriyo 
 Asoko nāma nāmena apaṭṭhāko vipassito 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yamosadhamadāsabhaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca aṭṭhame kappe sabbosadhasanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikicchako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tikicchakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Saṅghupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vessabhumbhi bhagavati ahosārāmiko ahaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano upaṭṭhiṃ saṃghamuttamaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito te sattame kappe sattevāsuṃ samodakā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saṅghupaṭṭhāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saṅghupaṭṭhākattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Kumudo atha nisseṇi rattiko udapānado 
 Sihāsani maggadado ekadipi maṇippado 
 Tikicchako upaṭṭāko ekunapaññāsa gāthakāti 
   Kumudavaggo aṭṭhārasamo   
  
   Manussānaṃ sukhāvaho  
  
                   
  
     Kuṭajapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ taraṃsiṃva uggataṃ 
 Disaṃ anuvilokentaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajase 
  
      Kuṭajaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā saṃvitthatasamotthataṃ 
 Rukkhato ocinitvāna phussassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Devanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhajujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito sattarase kappe tayo āsiṃsu pupphitā  
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṭajapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kuṭajapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Bandhujīvakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhattho nāma sambuddho sayambhu sabbhi vaṇṇito 
 Samādhiṃ so samāpanno nisīdi pabbatannare 
  
      Jātassare gavesanetā dakajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ 
 Bundhujivakapupphāni addasaṃ samananantaraṃ 
  
      Ubho hatthehi paggayha upagacchiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano siddhatthasāsabhiropayiṃ 
      Catunavute ito   kappe yaṃ puppamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito catuddase   kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Samuddakappo nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bandhujīvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bandhujīvakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Āsuṃ supupphitā machasaṃ   Catunnavutito machasaṃ   Cātuddase machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Koṭumabariyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
 Appameyyaṃva udadhiṃ vitthataṃ   dharaṇiṃ yathā 
  
      Pujitaṃ   devasaṅghena nisabhājāniyaṃ yathā 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ 
  
      Satta pupphāni paggayha koṭumbarasamākuṃla 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikino lokabandhuno 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ  
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito visatikappambhi mahānelasanāmako 
 Eko āsiṃ   mahātejo cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koṭaṭumbariyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Koṭumabariyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Pañcahatthiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tisso nāmāsi bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Purakkhato sāvakehi rathiyaṃ paṭipajjatha 
  
      Pañca uppalatthā ca caturo ṭhapitā mayā 
 Āhutiṃ dātukāmohaṃ paggaṇhiṃ vatasiddhiyā   
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambudadhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe 
 Buddharaṃsyābhiphuṭṭhembhi   pujeyiṃ dipadutatamaṃ 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ puphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito terasakappambhi pañcāsusabhasammatā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcahatthiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcahatthiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Udadhataṃ     ubbataṃ se   Pujitaṃ machasaṃ   Mabhiropayiṃ machasaṃ   Āsi 
 machasaṃ   Hitasiddhiyā syā   Budadharaṃsihi phuṭṭhosmi machasaṃ khudadharaṃsibha 
 phuṭṭhemahi     
  
                   
  
     Isimuggadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva sitaraṃsiṃva   bhānumaṃ 
 Kakudhaṃ vilasantiṃva padumuttaranāyakaṃ 
  
      Isimuggāni piṃsetvā   madhukhudde aniḷake 
 Pāsādeva ṭhito santo adāsiṃ lokabandhuno 
  
      Aṭṭhasatasahassāni ahesuṃ buddhasāvakā 
 Sabbesaṃ pattapuraṃ taṃ   tato cāpi bahuttaraṃ 
  
      Tena cittappasādena sukkamūlena codito 
 Kappānaṃ satasahasasaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Cattārisamhi sahasesa kappānaṃ aṭṭhatiṃse te 
 Isimuggasanāmā te   cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā isimuggadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Isimuggadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Bodhiupaṭṭhākattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare rammavatiyā āsiṃ murajavādako 
 Niccupaṭṭhānayuttomhi gatohaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
  
      Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upaṭṭhitvā sukkamūlena codito 
 Aṭṭhārasakappasate duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Pañcadase   kappasate ito āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Murajo   nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhiupaṭṭhāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bodhiupaṭṭhākattherassa apadānaṃ jaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Ekacintikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Yadā dovo devakāyā cavate āyusaṅkhayā 
 Tayo saddā niccharanti devānaṃ anumodataṃ 
  
      Ito bho sugatiṃ gaccha manussānaṃ sahavyataṃ 
 Manussabhuto saddhamme saddhamanuttaraṃ   
  
   Vataraṃsiṃva machasaṃ   Pisetthā machasaṃ saṃditvā se saṃdetvā     itimuggaṃ 
 nimattetvā syā saṃdetvā     itimuggaṃ nimattetvā syā   Purettaṃ machasaṃ     se   
 Mahisamattanāmā syā     se   Pañcarase machasaṃ   Damako syā   Labha saddhaṃ 
 anuttaraṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Sā te saddhātiviṭṭāssa   mulajātā patiṭṭhitā 
 Yāvajīvaṃ asaṃhirā saddhamme suppavedite 
  
                   
  
      Kāyena kusalaṃ katvā vādāya kusalaṃ bahuṃ 
 Manasā kusalaṃ katvā avyāpajjhaṃ   nirūpadhiṃ 
  
      Tato opadhikaṃ puññaṃ katvā dānena taṃ bahuṃ 
 Aññepi macce saddhamme brahmacariye nivesaya 
  
      Imāya anukampāya devā devaṃ yadā vidu 
 Vacantaṃ anumodanti ehi devapuraṃ puna   
  
      Saṃvego me   tadā āsi devasaṅghe samāgate 
 Kaṃ su nāma ahaṃ yoniṃ gamissāmi ito cuto 
  
      Mama saṃvegamaññāya samaṇo bhāvitindriyo 
 Mamuddhi tukāmo so āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
      Sumano nāma nāmena padumuttarasāvako 
 Atthadhammānusāsitvā saṃvejesi mamaṃ tadā 
  
      Tassā haṃ vacanaṃ sutvā buddhe citataṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Taṃ dhirimabhivādetvā tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Upapajjiṃ sa tattheva sukkamūlena codito 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekacittiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekacintikattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Tikaṇaṇipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Devabhuto ahaṃ santo accharāhi purakkhato 
 Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna buddhaseṭṭhamanussariṃ 
  
      Tikaṇṇipupphaṃ paggayha sakaṃ cittaṃ padāsiya  
 Buddhamhi abhiropesiṃ vipassimhi tarāsabhe 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tesattatimbhito kappe caturāsuṃ ramuttamā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikaṇṇipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tikaṇṇipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Niviṭṭhassaṃ simu   Abyāpajjaṃ machasaṃ avyāpajjaṃ   Deva punappunaṃ machasaṃ 
   Saṃviggohaṃ sā   Pasādayiṃ machasaṃ   Ekanavutito kappe yaṃ pupaphamabhipujayiṃ 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Ekacāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tāvatiṃsesu devesu mahāghoso tadā ahu 
 Buddho ca loke nibbāti mayaṃ vambha sarāgino 
  
      Tesaṃ saṃvegajātānaṃ sokasallasamaṅginaṃ 
 Sabalena upatthaddho agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃ 
  
      Mandāravaṃ gahetvāna saṇhitaṃ   abhinimmitaṃ 
 Parinibbāṇakālambhi buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Sabbe devānumodiṃsu accharāyo ca me tadā 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhikappasahassambhi ito soḷasa te janā 
 Mahāmallajanā nāma cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekacāriyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekacāriyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Tivaṇṭipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Abhibhuto panijjhanti   sabbe saṅgamma te mamaṃ  
 Tesaṃ nijjhāyamānānaṃ pariḷāho ajāyatha 
  
      Sunando nāma nāmena buddhassa sāvako tadā 
 Dhammadassissa munino āgacchi mama santike 
  
      Ye me baddhacarā āsuṃ te me pupphaṃ aduṃ tadā 
 Tāhaṃ pupphaṃ gahetvāna sāvake abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Sohaṃ kālakato tattha punāpi upapajjahaṃ 
 Aṭṭhārase kappasate vinipātaṃ na gacchahaṃ 
  
      Teraseto kappasate aṭṭāsuṃ dhumaketuno 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tivaṇaṭipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tivaṇaṭipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Kuṭajo bandujivi ca koṭumbarikahatthiyo 
 Isimuggo ca bodhi ca ekacitti tikaṇṇiko 
 Ekacārī tivaṇaṭī ca gāthā dvāsaṭṭhi kittitā 
   Kuṭajapupphiyavaggo ekunavisatimo   
  
   Saṅgitā machasaṃ saṅgitaṃ syā   Abhibhuṃ vopanijjhanti       Abhibhuṃ theraṃ 
 panijjhāma sabbe te mayaṃ syā 
  
                   
  
    Tamālapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Cullāsitisahassāni thamhā sovaṇṇamayā ahu 
 Devalaṭṭhipaṭibhāgaṃ vimānaṃ me sunimmitaṃ 
  
      Tamālapupphaṃ paggayha vippasannena cetasā 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito visatime kappe candatittoti ekako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tamālapphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tamālapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Tiṇasattharadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ dāyavāsiko   isi tiṇaṃ lāyati satthuno 
 Sabbe padakkhiṇāvattā   puthavyā   nipatiṃsu te 
  
      Tamahaṃ tiṇamādāya santhariṃ dhara ṇuttame 
 Tiṇeva tālapattāni āharitvānahaṃ tadā 
  
      Tiṇena chadanaṃ katvā siddhatthassa adāsahaṃ 
 Sattāhaṃ dhārayuṃ tassa satthuno devamānusā 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ tiṇaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pañcasaṭṭimbhito kappe cattārosuṃ mahaddhanā 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇasattharadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiṇasattharadākattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
  Tiṇasanthārakatthera apadānaṃ machasaṃ   Yadā vanavāsi machasaṃ   Sabbe 
 Padakkhiṇāvaṇaṭā machasaṃ   Pathabyā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Khaṇḍaphulliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Phassassa kho bhagavato thupā āsi mahāvane 
 Kuñajarehi tadā bhinno parūḷhapādapo   tahiṃ 
  
      Misamañña samaṃ katvā sudhāpiṇḍaṃ adāsahaṃ 
 Tilokagaruno tassaguṇhi paritosito 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sudhāpiṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattasattatikappambhi jitasenāsuṃ soḷasa 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khaṇḍaphulliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Khaṇḍaphulliyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Asokapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tivarāyaṃ   pure ramma rājuyyānamahu tadā 
 Uyyānapālo tatthāsiṃ rañño baddhacaro ahaṃ 
  
      Padumo nāma nāmena sayambhu sappabho ahu 
 Nisinnaṃ puṇḍarikambhi chāyā na jahi taṃ muniṃ 
  
      Asokaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā piṇḍibhāraṃ sudassanaṃ 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ jalajuttamanāmino 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphavabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattatiṃsambhito kappe soḷasa aruṇañajahā  
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā asokapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Asokapujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Parūḷeyā pādapo machasaṃ saṃrūḷho pādapo     se   Tivarāyaṃ machasaṃ 
 Tipurāyaṃ syā   Araṇañajahā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Aṅkolakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Aṅkolaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā mālāvaraṃ sakosakaṃ   
 Ovinitvāna taṃ pupphaṃ agamaṃ buddhasantikaṃ 
  
      Siddhattho tamhi samaye paṭilino   mahāmuni 
 Muhuttaṃ patimānetvā guhāyaṃ pupphamokiriṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamokiriṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Chattiṃsambhi ito kappe āseko devagajjito 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aṅkolako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Aṅkolakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Kisalayapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
      Nagare dvāravatiyā mālāvaccho mamaṃ ahu 
 Udapāno ca tattheva pādapānaṃ virohano 
  
      Sabalena upatthaddho siddhattho aparājito 
 Mamānukampamāno so gacchate anilañajase 
  
      Aññaṃ kiñci na passāmi pujāyoggaṃ mahesino 
 Asokapallavaṃ disvā ākāse ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Buddhassa te kisalayā gacchato yanti pacchato 
 Sohaṃ disvāna taṃ iddhiṃ   aho buddhassuḷāratā 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe pallavaṃ abhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Sattavisa   ito kappe eko ekassaro   ahu 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kisalayapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tisalayapujakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
  
   Samogamaṃ syā   Patilino machasaṃ   Pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ machasaṃ 
   Tāhaṃ disvāna saṃvijiṃ machasaṃ   Sattatiṃse machasaṃ   Ekissaro machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Tindukadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Giriduggavaro āsiṃ makakaṭo thāmavegiko 
 Phalinaṃ tindukaṃ disvā buddhaseṭṭhaṃ anussariṃ 
  
      Nikkhamitvā katipāhaṃ viciniṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano siddhatthaṃ tibhavantuguṃ 
  
      Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro 
 Khiṇāsavasahassehi āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
      Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna phalahattho upāgamiṃ 
 Paṭiggahesi bhagavā sabbaññu vadataṃ varo 
  
                   
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānayassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattapaññāsakappambhi upavanda sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tindukadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tindūkadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Muṭṭhipujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Pacchime anukampāya padhānaṃ padahi jino 
  
      Tassa caṅkammānassa dipadindassa tādino 
 Girinelassa pupphānaṃ muṭṭiṃ buddhasa ropayiṃ 
  
      Tena cittappasādena sukkamūlena codito 
 Tiṃsakappasahassāni duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Tevisatikappasate sunelo nāma khattiyo 
 Sattaratanasampanno eko mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā muṭṭhipujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Muṭṭhipujakattherassa apadānaṃ a maṃ   
  
                   
  
     Kiṅkaṇipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumaṅgaloti nāmena sayambhu aparājito 
 Pavanā nikkhamitvāna nagaraṃ pāvisi jino 
  
      Piṇḍacāraṃ caritvāna nikkhamma nagarā muni 
 Katakiccova sambuddho so vasi vanamantare 
  
                   
  
      Kiṅkaṇipupphaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano sayambhussa mahesino 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Chaḷāsitambhito kappe apilāpiya   nāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kiṅkaṇipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kiṅkaṇipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Yuthikāpupphiyattherāpadānaṃ   
      Padumuttaro nāma jino āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Pavanā kikkhamitvāna vihāraṃ yāti cakkhumā 
  
      Ubho hatthehi paggayha yuthikaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ mettacittassa tādino 
  
      Tena citatappasādena abhibhotvāna pasampadā 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ duggatiṃ nupapajjahaṃ 
  
      Ito paññāsakappesu eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Samittanandano nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yuthikāpupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Yuthikāpupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
  
   Kiṃkaṇikapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ machasaṃ   Apilāsisa machasaṃ   
 Yuthikapupaphiyattherāpadānaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Tamāli tiṇasanthāro khaṇiḍuphalli asokiyo 
 Aṅkolaki kisalāyo tinduko nelapupphiyo 
 Kiṅkaṇiko yuthiko ca gāthā paññasa aṭṭha ca 
   Tamālapupphiyavaggo visatimo   
  
                   
  
 Atha vagguddānaṃ 
 Bhikkhādāyī parivāro sereyyo sobhito tathā 
 Chatto ca bandhujīvo ca   supāricariyopi ca 
 Kumado kuṭajo ceva tamāli dasamo kato 
 Chasatāni ca gāthānaṃ chasaṭṭhi ca tatutatriṃ 
   Bhikkhāvaggadasakaṃ   
   Dutiyaṃ satakaṃ samattaṃ   
  
     Kaṇikārapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kanikāraṃ pupphitaṃ disvā ocinitvānahaṃ tadā 
 Tissassa abhiropesiṃ oghatiṇṇassa tādino 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pañcatiṃse ito kappe aèṇapāṇiti vissuto 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṇikārapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kaṇikārapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Miṇelapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo bhagavā sataraṃsi patāpavā 
 Caṅkamanaṃ samārūḷho mettacitto sikhisabho 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano vanditvā   ñāṇamuttamaṃ 
 Minelapupphaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekaṃtise ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
   Chattañca bandhujīviñca machasaṃ   Thometva syā 
  
                   
  
      Ekunatiṃse kappamhi sumedhayasa   nāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā minelapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Minelapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Kiṅkiṇikapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso sababaññu lokanāyako 
 Odakaṃ dahamogayha sināyi lokanāyako 
  
      Paggayha kiṅkiṇiṃ   pupphaṃ vipassissā bhiropayiṃ 
 Udaggacitto sumano dipadindassa tādino 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattavisatikappambhi rājā bhimaratho ahu 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kiṅkiṇikapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kiṅkiṇikapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Taraṇiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Atthadassitu bhagavā dipadindo narāsabho 
 Purakkhato sāvakehi gaṅgātiramupāgami 
      Samatittikā kākapeyyā gaṅgā āsi duruttarā 
 Uttārayiṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ buddhaṃ ca dipaduttamaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi taraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Teraseto kappasate pañca sabbhogavā   ahuṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
   Sumeghaghana nāmako machasaṃ  kiṅkaṇipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ machasaṃ   
 Kiṅkaṇiṃ machasaṃ   Sabbobhavā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pacchime ca bhave asmiṃ jātohaṃ brāhmaṇe kule 
 Saddhiṃ tihi sahāyehi pabbajiṃ satthusāsane 
  
 Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā taraṇiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Taraṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Nigguṇḍipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vipassassa bhagavato āsimārāmiko ahaṃ 
 Nigguṇḍipupphaṃ paggayaṃha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pañcatiṃse ito kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Mahāpatāpo nāmena   cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nigguṇḍipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nigguṇḍipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Udakadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Bhuñjannaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā vippasannamanāvilaṃ 
 Ghaṭenodakamādāya siddhatthassa adāsahaṃ 
  
      Nimmalo homahaṃ ajja vimalo khiṇasaṃsayo 
 Bhave nibbattamānambhi phalaṃ nibbattate subhaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe udakaṃ yaṃ tadā adaṃ    
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi udakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekasaṭṭhimbhato kappe ekova vimalo ahuṃ 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Udakadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
   Mahāpatāpanāmena machasaṃ   Udakaṃ yamadāsahaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Salalamāliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
 Obhāsontaṃ disā sabbā siddhatthaṃ narasārathiṃ 
  
      Dhanumadvejjhaṃ katvāna usuṃ sannayhahaṃ tadā 
 Pupphaṃ savaṇaṭaṃ chetvāna buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ   
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekapaññāsito kappe eko āsiṃ junindharo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sallamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sallamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Koraṇḍapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Akkañatañca padaṃ disvā cakkālaṅkāra bhusitaṃ 
 Padenānupadaṃ yanto vipassissa mahesino 
  
      Koraṇḍaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā samulaṃ pujitaṃ mayā 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cattena avandiṃ padamuttamaṃ 
  
      Rakanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi padapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattapaññāsakappamhi eko vitamalo ahu 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koraṇḍapūpphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Koraṇḍapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
   Mabhiropayiṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Ādhāradāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ādhārakaṃ mayā dinnaṃ sikhino lokabandhuno 
 Dhāremi phaṭhaviṃ   sabbaṃ kevalaṃ vasudhaṃ imaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Sattavise ito kappe ahesuṃ caturo janā 
 Samantavaraṇā   nāma cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ādhāradāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ādhāradāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Vātātapanivāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tissassa tu bhagavato devadevassa tādino 
 Ekacchattaṃ mayā dinnaṃ vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Nivutaṃ hoti me pāpaṃ kusalassupasampadā 
 Ākāse chattaṃ dhārenti pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Carimaṃ vattate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ chattamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dvesattatimbhito kappe aṭṭhāsiṃsu janādhipā 
 Mahānidānanāmena rājāno cakkavattino 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vātātapanivāriyo  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Vātāpanivāriyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Kaṇikāro minelañca kiṅkiṇi taraṇenaca 
 Nigguṇḍipupphi dakado salalo ca kuraṇḍako 
 Ādhārakotapavāri   aṭṭhatāḷisa gāthakā 
   Kaṇikārapupphiyavaggo ekavisatimo 
  
   Pathaviṃ machasaṃ   Samantavaraṇa machasaṃ  pāpanivāriyattherādānaṃ machasaṃ   
 Pāpacāri machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Hatthiyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato dipadindassa   tādino 
 Nāgaseṭṭho mayā dinnā īsādanto urūḷhavā 
  
      Uttamatthaṃ anubhomi santipadamanuttaraṃ 
 Aggadānaṃ   mayā dinnaṃ sabbalokabhitesino 
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ nāgamadadiṃ   tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi nāgadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhasattatikappambhi soḷasāsiṃsu khattiyā 
 Samantapāsādikā nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā hatthidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Hatthidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Pānadhidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Āraññakassa   isino cirarattatapassino 
 Vuddhassa   bhāvitattassa adāsiṃ pānadhiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena dipadinda lokajeṭṭha narāsabha 
 Sabbaṃ yānaṃ anubhomi pubbakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Catunavute   ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pānadhissa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattasattatito kappe aṭṭha āsiṃsu khattiyā 
 Suyānā nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pānadhidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pānadhidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Dvipadindassa machasaṃ   Nāgadānaṃ   Dānamadadiṃ simu   Āraññikassa machasaṃ 
   Dhammassa syā ka   Dibbayānaṃ machasaṃ   Catunevute 
  
                   
  
     Saccasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vessabhu tambhi samaye bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato 
 Deseti ariyasaccāni nibbāpento mahājanaṃ 
  
      Paramakāruññapattombhi samitiṃ agamāsabhaṃ 
 Sohaṃ nisinnako santo dhammassosiṃ satthuno 
  
      Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna devalokamagacchahaṃ 
 Tiṃsakappāni devesu avasiṃ tatthahaṃ pure 
  
      Ekatiṃse   ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saccasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Chabbisambhi ito kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Ekaphusitanāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saccasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saccasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Ekasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Dumagge paṃsukulikaṃ laggaṃ disvāna satthuno 
 Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna paṃsukulaṃ avandihaṃ   
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pañcavise ito kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Amitābhoti nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Ekattiṃse machasaṃ   Avandahaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Raṃsisaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Udentaṃ sataraṃsiṃva sitaraṃsiṃva   bhānumaṃ 
 Vyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ sujātaṃ pabbatannare 
  
      Buddhassa ānubhāvo so jalate pabbatantare 
 Raṃse citataṃ pasādetvā kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ 
  
      Avasesesu kappesu kusalaṃ sukataṃ   mayā 
 Tena cittappasādena buddhānussatiyā pi ca 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahasseto yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhasaññāyidaṃ   phalaṃ 
  
      Sattapaññāsakappambi eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Sujāto nāma nāmena cakakvatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṃsisaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Raṃsisaññakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Saṇṭhitattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Assatthe haritobhase saṃviruḷhamhi pādape 
 Ekaṃ buddhagataṃ saññaṃ alabhissa   patissato 
  
      Ekatiṃse   ito kappe yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā 
 Tassā saññāya vāhasā patto me āsavakkhayo 
  
      Ito terasakappambhi dhaniṭṭho nāma khattiyo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saṇṭhito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saṇṭhitattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
   Vitaraṃsiṃva machasaṃ   Caritaṃ machasaṃ karitaṃ simu   Buddhapūjāyidaṃ simu   
 Alabhiṃhaṃ machasaṃ   Ekantiṃse machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Tālavaṇṭadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tālavaṇṭaṃ mayā dinnaṃ tisasassā diccabandhuno 
 Gimhanibbāpanatthāya pariḷābhopasantiyā 
  
      Santibbāpemi rāgaggiṃ dosaggiñca taduttariṃ 
 Nibbāpemi ca mohaggiṃ tālavaṇṭassadaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsanaṃ 
  
      Dve navute ito kape yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Daggatiṃ nābhijānāmi budadhapujiyidaṃ   phalaṃ 
  
      Tosaṭṭimbhi ito kappe mahānāma sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tālavaṇṭadāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tālavaṇṭadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Akkantasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kusāṭakaṃ gahetvāna upajjhāyassahaṃ pure 
 Mantaṃ ca anusikkhāmi kaṇḍabhedassa   pattiyā 
  
      Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ 
 Usabhaṃ pavaraṃ aggaṃ tissaṃ buddhaṃ gaṇuttamaṃ 
  
      Kusāṭakaṃ pattharitaṃ akkamantaṃ naruttamaṃ 
 Samuggataṃ mahāvīraṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Disvā taṃ lokapajjotaṃ vimalaṃ candasannibhaṃ 
 Avandiṃ satthuno pāde vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Catunavute   ito kappe yaṃ adāsiṃ kusāṭakaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kusāṭakassadaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattatiṃse ito kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Sunando nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā akkattasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Akkantasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Tālavaṇṭayasidaṃ machasaṃ   Ganthādosassa machasaṃ   Catunnavute machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Sappidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nisinno pasādavare nārigaṇapurakkhato 
 Vyādhitaṃ samaṇaṃ disvā abhināmesahaṃ   gharaṃ 
  
      Upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Sappitelaṃ mayā dinnaṃ siddhatthassa mahesino 
  
      Passaddhadarathaṃ disvā vippasannamukhindriyaṃ 
 Vanditvā satthuno pāde anusaṃsāvayiṃ pure 
  
      Disvā maṃ suppasannattaṃ   iddhiyā pāramiṅgato 
 Nabhaṃ abbhuggami dhīro haṃsarājāva ambare 
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sappitelassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito sattarasesa kappe jutideva   sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sappidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sappidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Pāpanivāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Piyadassissa bhagavato caṅkamaṃ sodhitaṃ mayā 
 Naḷakehi paṭicchannaṃ vātātapanivāraṇaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pāpaṃ vivajjanatthāya kusalassupasampadā 
 Kilesānaṃ pahānāya padabhiṃ satthusāsane 
  
      Ito ekādase kappe yaṃ aggidevoti vissuto 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāpanivāriyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pāpanivāriyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Hatthi pānadhi saccañca ekasaññi ca raṃsiyo 
 Saṇṭhito tālavaṇṭi ca   tathā akkattasaññako 
 Sappi pāpanicāri ca catupaññāsa gāthakāti 
   Hatthivaggo bāvisatimo   
  
   Abhimānesaṃ simu   Suppasananattaṃ syā    Dutideva syā tunideva ka   
 Tālavaṇṭañca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Ālambanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Atthadassissa   bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Ālambanaṃ mayā dinnaṃ dipadindassa tādino 
  
      Dharaṇiṃ paṭipajjāmi vipulaṃ sāgarapparaṃ 
 Pāṇesu ca issariyaṃ vattemi vasudhāya ca 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Tisesā vijjā anuppattā kata buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Ito dvesaṭṭhikappambhi tayo āsiṃsu khatatiyā 
 Ekāpassata nāmā te cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ālambanadāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ālambanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Ajinadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse   ito kappe gaṇasatthā ahosahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ 
  
      Cammakhaṇḍaṃ mayā dinnaṃ sikhino lokabandhuno 
 Tena kammena dipadinde   lokajeṭṭhe narāsabhe 
  
                   
  
      Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna kilesā jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kape ajinaṃ yamadāsahaṃ 
 Daggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ajinassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito pañcamake kappe rājā āsiṃ sudāyako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ajinadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ajinadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Atthadassi simu   Ekattiṃse machasaṃ   Dvipadinda machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Davirataniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ budadhaṃ āhuninaṃ paṭiggahaṃ 
  
      Maṃsapesi mayā dinanā vipassissa mahesino 
 Sadevakasmiṃ lokasmiṃ issaraṃ kārayāmahaṃ 
  
      Iminā maṃsadānena ratanaṃ nibbattate mama 
 Duveme ratanā loke diṭṭhadhammassa pattiyā 
  
      Tehaṃ sabbe anubhomi maṃsadānassa sattiyā 
 Gatañca mudukaṃ mayhaṃ paññā nipuṇavedini   
  
      Ekanavute ito   kape yaṃ maṃsamadadiṃ ahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi maṃsadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito catutthake kappe eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Mahārohita nāmo so cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dviratatiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dviratatiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Ārakkhadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato vedi kārāpitā   mayā 
 Ārakkho ca mayā dinno sugatassa mahesino 
  
      Tena kammavisesena na passe   bhayabheravaṃ 
 Kubhiñci uppannassa kāso mayhaṃ na vijjati 
  
                   
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ vediṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ    
 Daggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito chaṭṭambhi kappambhi apassena sanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ārakkhadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ārakkhadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
  Devarataniyathera machasaṃ   Nipuṇavedanaṇi machasaṃ   Ekanavutito machasaṃ   
 Vedikā kāritā syā   Na passiṃ machasaṃ   Catunnavutito machasaṃ   Pure machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Avyādhikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vipassissa bhagavato aggisālamadāsahaṃ 
 Vyādhitānañca āvāsaṃ uṇhodakapaṭiggahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena yaṃ mayhaṃ attabhāvo sunimmito 
 Vyādhāhaṃ nābhijanāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito   kappe yaṃ sālamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi aggisālāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito sattamake kappe ekosiṃ aparājito 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avyādhiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Avyādhikattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Aṅkolapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nārado iti me nāmaṃ kassapo iti maṃ vidu 
 Addasaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ vipassiṃ devasakkataṃ 
  
      Anubyañajanadharaṃ buddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ 
 Aṅkolapupphaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catusattatito kappe romaso nāma khattiyo 
 Āmuttamālābharaṇo sayoggabavāhato 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aṅkolapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Aṅkolapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
  Abyādhika machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyayattherāpadānaṃ  
  
      Uyyānabhumiṃ niyyanto addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Vaṭaṃsakaṃ gahetvāna sovaṇṇaṃ sādhunimmitaṃ 
  
      Sighaṃ tato samoruyha   hatthikkhanvadhagato ahaṃ 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sikhino lokabandhuno 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ    
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattavise ito kapepa eko āsiṃ janādhipo 
 Mahāpatāpa nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sovaṇṇavaṭaṃsakiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Miñajavaṭaṃsakiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi sikhimhi vadataṃ vare 
 Vaṭaṃsakehi ākiṇṇaṃ bodhipujamakāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bodhipujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito chabbisatikappe ahuṃ meghabbha nāmako 
 Sattarananasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā miñajavaṭaṃsakiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Miñajavaṭaṃsakiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Sukatāveliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Asitonāma nāmena mālākāro ahuṃ   tadā 
 Āvelaṃ paggahevona rañño dātuṃ vajāmahaṃ 
  
      Asampattamhi rājānaṃ addasaṃ sikhināyakaṃ 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse   ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
  Vaṭaṃsakiyattherāpadānaṃ simu   Samāruyha machasaṃ   Pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 machasaṃ  Pupphapujāyidaṃ machasaṃ   Ahaṃ machasaṃ   Ekattiṃse machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pañcavise ito kappe rājāhosiṃ mahabbalo 
 Vehāro nāma cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sukatāveliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sukatāveliyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Ekavandiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ vessabhuṃ vijitāvitaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandihaṃ   
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catuvīsatikappamhi vigatānandanāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekavandiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekavandiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Ālambanañca ajinaṃ maṃsadā rakkhadāyako 
 Avyādhi aṅkolaṃ   soṇṇaṃ miñajaṃ āvela vandanaṃ 
 Pañcapaññasa gāthāyo gaṇitā atthadassihi 
   Ālambanadāyakavaggo tevisatimo   
  
                   
  
     Udakāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma phalakaṃ satthariṃ ahaṃ 
 Udakañca upaṭṭhāsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āsane coke phalaṃ 
  
      Ito paṇṇarase kappe abhisāmasamavhayo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
   Buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ machasaṃ   Cakulaṃ syā 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Udakāsanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Bhājanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ   
  
      Nagare bandhumatiyā kumbhakāro ahaṃ tadā 
 Bhājanaṃ anupālesiṃ bhikkhusaṅghassa tāvade 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe bhājanaṃ anupālayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhājanassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tepaññāse ito kappe anantajāli nāmako 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhājanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bhājanadākattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Sālapupiyattherāpādanaṃ 
      Aruṇavatiyā nagare ahosiṃ pupiko ahaṃ 
 Mama dvārena gacchantaṃ sikhinaṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ 
  
      Buddhassa pattaṃ paggayha sālapupaṃ   adāsahaṃ 
 Sammaggatassa buddhassa vippasannena cetasā 
  
                   
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ khajjakamadāsahaṃ    
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sālapupassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito cuddasakappambhi asosiṃ amitañajalo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime
