 Parakammāyane yutto parabhattaṃ apassino 
  
      Rahogato nisīditvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
  Buddho loke samuppanno adhikāro ca natthi me 
  
                   
  
      Kālo gatiṃ   sodhetuṃ khaṇo me paṭipādito 
 Dukkho nirayasamphasso apuññānaṃ hi pāṇinaṃ  
  
      Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃ 
 Ekāhaṃ kammaṃ yācitvā vipinaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tiṇakaṭṭhañca valliñcaña āharitvānahaṃ tadā 
 Tidaṇḍake ṭhapetvāna akaṃ tiṇakuṭiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Saṅghassatthāya kuṭikaṃ niyyātetvāna taṃ ahaṃ 
 Tadaheyeva āgantvā kammasāmiṃ upāgamiṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
 Kattha me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ tiṇakuṭikāya nimmitaṃ   
  
      Sahassakaṇḍaṃ satabheṇḍu dhajālu haritāmayaṃ  
 Satasahassaniyyuhā vyamhe pātubhaviṃsu me 
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya pāsādo upatiṭṭhati 
  
      Bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso na vijjati 
 Tāsaṃ mama na jānāmi tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sīhavyagghā ca dipi ca acchakokataracchakā 
 Sabbe maṃ parivajjenti tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Siriṃsapā   ca bhūtā ca abhikumbhaṇḍarakkhasā 
 Te pi maṃ parivajejanati tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Na pāpasupinassāhaṃ   sarāmi dassanaṃ mama 
 Upaṭṭhitā sati mayhaṃ tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tāyeva tiṇakuṭikāya anubhotvāna sampadā 
 Gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikariṃ ahaṃ 
  
   Kālo me gatiṃ machasaṃ   Kuṭikāya sunimmitaṃ machasaṃ   Sahassakaṇḍo 
 satabheṇḍu dhajāluharitāmayo simu   Sarisapā machasaṃ   Na pāpasupinasasāni 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇakuṭikāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇakuṭidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiṇaduṭidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Uttareyyadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā ahosiṃ brāhmaṇo tadā 
 Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragu 
  
      Purakkhato sasissehi jātimā ca susikkhito 
 Toyābhisevanatthāya nagarā nikkhamiṃ tadā 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragu 
 Khiṇāsavasahassehi nagaraṃ pāvisi jino 
  
      Suvārurūpaṃ disvāna anejakāritaṃ   viya 
 Parivutamarahantehi disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
  
      Sirasi   añjaliṃ katvā namassitvāna subbataṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano uttariyamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Ubho satthehi paggayha sāṭakaṃ ukkhipiṃ ahaṃ 
 Yāvatā buddhaparisā tāva chādesi pāṭako 
  
      Piṇḍacāraṃ carantassa mahābhikkhugaṇādino 
 Chadaṃ karonto aṭṭāsi hāsayanto mamaṃ tadā 
  
      Gharato nikkhamantassa sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Vithiyaṃva ṭhito satthā akā me   anumodanaṃ 
  
       Pasannacitto sumano yo me pādāsi sāṭakaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramisasti 
 Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
  
      Devaloke vasantassa puññakammasamaṅgino 
 Samantā yojanasataṃ dusasacchannaṃ bhavissati 
  
      Chattiṃsakkhatatuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
   Aneñajakāritaṃ machasaṃ   Sirasmiṃ machasaṃ   Akāsi anumodanaṃ syā 
  
                   
  
      Bhave saṃsaramānassa puññakammasamaṅgino 
 Manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ nibbattissati tāvade 
  
      Koseyyakambaliyāni khomakappāyikāni ca 
 Mahagghāni ca dussāni paṭilacchatayaṃ naro   
  
                   
  
      Manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilacchatayaṃ naro 
 Ekadussassa vipākaṃ anubhossati sabbadā 
  
      So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikarissati  
  
      Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ sabbaññussa mahesino 
 Ekāhaṃ sāṭakaṃ datvā pattomhi amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Maṇḍapepa rukkhamule vā vasato suññake ghare 
 Dhāreti dussachadanaṃ samantā vyāmato mama 
  
      Aviññattaṃ nivāsemi cīvaraṃ paccayañcahaṃ 
 Pābhi   antassa pānassa uttareyyasasidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vanthadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttareyyadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Uttareyyadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Dhammasavaṇiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragu 
 Catusaccaṃ pakāsento santāresi bahuṃ janaṃ 
  
      Ahaṃ tena samayena jaṭilo uggatāpano 
 Dhunanto vākacirāni gacchāmi ambare tadā 
  
      Buddhaseṭṭhassa upari gantuṃ na visahāmahaṃ 
 Pakkhiva selamāsajja   gamanaṃ nālabhiṃ   tadā 
  
      Na me idaṃ bhūtapubbaṃ iriyassa vikopanaṃ 
 Dake yathā ummujjitvā evaṃ gacchāmi ambare 
  
   Paṭilacchatiyaṃ naro machasaṃ   Lābhimhi syā   Selamāpajja   Na labhāmahaṃ 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Uḷārabhuto manujo heṭṭhāsino bhavissati 
 Handamenaṃ gavesissaṃ api atthaṃ labheyyahaṃ 
  
      Orohanto antalikkhā sadadamassosiṃ satthuno 
 Aniccataṃ kathentassa tamahaṃ uggahiṃ tadā 
  
      Aniccasaññamuggayha agamāsiṃ mamassamaṃ 
 Yāvatāyuṃ vasitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Carime catatamānambhi taṃ dhammasamaṇaṃ sariṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatte tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ 
 Ekapaññāyakkhattañca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
  
      Ekasattakikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Pitu gehe   nisīditvā samaṇo bhāvitindriyo 
 Gāthāya paridīpento aniccatamudāhari  
  
      Anussarāmi taṃ saññaṃ saṃsaranto bhavābhave 
 Na koṭiṃ paṭivijjhāmi nibbāṇaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Aniccā vata saṅkhārā uppādavayadhammino 
 Uppajjatvā nirujjhanti tesaṃ vupasāmo sukho 
  
      Saha gāthaṃ suṇitvāna pubbakammaṃ anussariṃ 
 Ekāsane nisīditvā arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Upasampādayī buddho guṇamaññāya cakkhumā 
  
      Dārakova ahaṃ santo karaṇiyaṃ samāpayiṃ 
 Kiṃ me karaṇiyaṃ   ajja sakyaputatassa sāsane 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saddhammasamaṇe phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammasavaṇiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dhammasavaṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
   Ghare simu   Aniccavatthudāhari syā   Karaṇiyaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Ukkhittapadumiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā ahosiṃ māliko tadā 
 Ogāhitvā   padumasaraṃ satapatte   ocināmahaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragu 
 Saha satasahassehi santacittehi tādihi 
  
      Khiṇāsavehi suddhehi chaḷabhiññehi so tadā  
 Mama vuddhiṃ samatvesaṃ āgacchi mama santike   
  
      Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Maṇṭe chetvā satapattaṃ ukkhipiṃ ambare tadā 
  
      Yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Sayaṃ gantvā satapattā matthake dhārayantu te 
  
      Adhiṭṭhahi mahāvīro lokejeṭṭho narasabho 
 Buddhasa ānubhāvena matthake dhārayiṃsu te 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ deṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Tassa me sukataṃ vyamhaṃ satapattanti vuccati 
 Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ 
  
      Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ akārayiṃ 
 Pañcasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
 Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatamattano 
  
      Tenevekapadumena anubhotvāna sampadā 
 Gotamassa bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikariṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Kilosā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekapadumassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ukkhittapadumiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ukkhittapadumiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
   Ogāhetvā machasaṃ   Satapantaṃ machasaṃ   Chaḷabhiññehi jhāyihi machasaṃ   
 Santikaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Gandhadhupo ca udakaṃ   punnāgaekadusasiko 
 Phusito ca pabhaṅkaro kuṭido uttariyako 
 Savaṇi ekapadumi gāthāyo tattha piṇḍitā 
 Ekaṃ gāthāyatañceca catutāḷisameva ca 
   Gandhadhupiyavaggo   catuttiṃsatimo   
  
     Ekapadumiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragu 
 Bhavābhave vibhāvento tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
  
      Haṃsarājā tadā homi dijānaṃ pavaro ahaṃ 
 Jātassaraṃ samogayha kiḷāmi haṃsakiḷitaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Jātassarassa upari āgacchi tāvado jano 
  
      Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ sayambhuṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Vaṇṭe chetvāna padumaṃ satapattaṃ manoramaṃ 
  
      Mukhatuṇḍena paggayha pasanno lokanāyake 
 Ukkhipitvāna gagane buddhaseṭṭhamapujayiṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā akā me anumodānaṃ 
  
       Iminā ekapadumena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ vinipātaṃ na gacchasi  
  
      Idaṃ vavona sambuddho japajuttamanāmako 
 Mama kammaṃ pakittetvā agamā yena patthitaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapadumiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekadumiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Gandhokapujani ca     se   Gandhodakavaggo     ma se 
  
                   
  
     Tiuppalamāliyattherāpadānaṃ   
  
      Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ vānaro tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
  
      Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā sālarājaṃva phullitaṃ 
 Lakkhaṇabyañajanupetaṃ disvā attamano ahuṃ 
      Udaggacitto sumano pitiyā haṭṭhamānaso 
 Tīṇi uppalapupphāni matthake abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Pupphāni abhiropetvā vipassissa mahesino 
 Sagāravo gavitvāna   pakkamiṃ   uttarāmukho 
  
      Gacchanto patikuṭiko vippasannena cetasā 
 Selannare patitvāna   pāpuṇiṃ jīvitakkhayaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
      Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Tatānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca cakkavattī ahosahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiuppalamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiuppalamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Dhajadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tisso nāma ahu satthā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Tassopadhikkhaye disvā dhajamāropitaṃ mayā 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetatāpaṇidhihi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
  
   Tiṇuppalamāliyattherāpaadānaṃ machasaṃ   Bhavitvāna machasaṃ   Pakkāmiṃ 
 machasaṃ   Papatitvā syā 
  
                   
  
      Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
 Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatamattano 
  
      Dvenanute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Icchamānovahaṃ ajja sakānanaṃ sapabbataṃ 
 Khomadussena chādeyyaṃ tadā mayhaṃ kate phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhajadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dhajadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Tikiṅkiṇipujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Hivamantassāvidure bhūtagaṇo nāma pabbato 
 Tatthadadasaṃ paṃsukūlaṃ dumaggamhi vilaggitaṃ 
  
      Tīṇi kiṅkiṇupupphāni ocinitvā ahaṃ tadā 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena paṃsukulamapujayiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇṇaṃ pupphānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikiṅkiṇipujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tikiṅkiṇipujakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Naḷāgārikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre hārito nāma pabbato 
 Sayambhu nārado rukkhamule visi tadā 
  
      Naḷāgāraṃ karitvāna tiṇena chādayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Caṅkamaṃ sodhayitvāna sayambhussa adāsahaṃ 
  
      Catuddasasu kappesu devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ 
 Catusattatikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Sattasattatikkhattuñca   cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ indalaṭṭiva uggataṃ 
 Sahassathambhaṃ atulaṃ vimānaṃ sapabhasasaraṃ 
  
      Dve sampatti anubhotvā sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Padhānapabhitattomhi upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāḷāgāriko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nāḷāgārikattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Campakapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
      Himavantassa avidūre cāpalo   nāma pabbato 
 Buddho sudassano nāma vihāsi pabbatantare 
  
      Pupphaṃ hevamataṃ   gayha gacchaṃ vehāsenahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
  
      Satta campakapupphāni sīse katvānahaṃ tadā 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ sayambhussa mahesino 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ    
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā campakapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Campakapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Padumapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre romaso nāma pabbato 
 Buddhopi samanave nāma abbhokāse vasi tadā 
  
      Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna padumaṃ dhārayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Ekāhaṃ dhārayitvāna puna bhavanamupāgamiṃ 
  
   Catusattatatikkhattuñca machasaṃ   Chāpalo syā jāpalo machasaṃ 
   Hemavantaṃ machasaṃ   Pupphamabhiropayiṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Padumapujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre lambako nāma pabbato 
 Upatisso nāma sambuddho abbhokāsamhi caṅkami 
  
      Migaluddo tadā āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ 
 Disvāna taṃ devadevaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Vippasannena cittena tadā tadada mahesino 
 Nisidanatthaṃ buddhassa tiṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ 
  
      Datvāna devadevassa bhiyyo cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Sambuddhamabhivādetvā sakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho 
  
      Aciraṃ gatamattaṃ maṃ migarājā aheṭhayī  
 Sihena pātito   santo tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Āsanne me kataṃ kammaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe anāsave 
 Sumutto saravegova devalokamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Yupo tattha subho āsi puññakammābhinimmito 
 Sahassakaṇḍo satabheṇḍu dhajālu haritāmayo 
  
      Pabhā niddhāvate tassa sataraṃsiva uggato 
 Ākiṇṇo devakaññābhi āmodiṃ kāmakāmahaṃ 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Āgantvāna manussattaṃ pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe nisidanamadāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tiṇamuṭṭhisasidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇamuṭṭhidāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Apothayi machasaṃ   Pothito machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Tindukaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
  
      Tindukaṃ saphalaṃ disvā bhinditvāna sakeṭakaṃ    
 Pasannacitto sumano vessabhussa adāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tindukaphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tindukaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Ekañajaliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Revato   nāma sambuddho nadikule vasī tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ pitaraṃsiṃva bhānumaṃ 
  
      Ukkāmukhapahaṭṭhaṃva khadiraṅgārasannibhaṃ 
 Osadhiṃva virocantaṃ ekañajalimakāsabhaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yamañajalimakāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi añajaliyā idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekañajaliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekañajaliyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Padumi uppalamāli dhajo niṅkiṇiko nāḷo 
 Campako padumo muṭṭi tindukakeñajali tathā 
 Cha ca saṭṭhi ca gāthāyo gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi 
   Ekapadumiyavaggo pañcatiṃsatimo 
  
   Sakosakaṃ machasaṃ   Romaso machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Saddasaññakattherāpadānaṃ 
      Migaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānate ahaṃ 
 Tatthadadasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ devasaṅghapurakkhataṃ 
  
      Catusaccaṃ pakāsentaṃ uddharantaṃ mahājanaṃ 
 Assosiṃ madhuraṃ vācaṃ karecikarutopamaṃ  
  
      Brahmassarassa munino sikhino lokabandhuno 
 Ghose cittaṃ pasādetvā pattombhi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pasādassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saddasaññako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saddasaññakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Yavakalāpiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare aruṇavatiyā āsiṃ yāvasiko   tadā 
 Panthe disvāna sambuddhaṃ yavakalāpamavatthariṃ 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko sikhi lokagganāyako 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya nisīdi yavasanthare 
  
      Disvā nisinnaṃ vimalaṃ mahājhāyiṃ vināyakaṃ 
 Pāmujjaṃ   janayitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi yavatthare idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā yavakalāpiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pavakalāpiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Yavasiko sabbattha   Pāmojjaṃ machasaṃ  karavikarudopamaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Kiṃsukapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kiṃsukaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā paggahetvāna añjaliṃ 
 Buddhaṃ saritvā siddhatthaṃ ākāse abhipujayiṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kiṃsukapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kiṃsakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Sakoṭakakoraṇḍadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Akkantañca padaṃ disvā sikhino lokabandhuno 
 Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā padaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ 
  
      Koraṇḍaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā pādapaṃ dharaṇiruhaṃ 
 Sakoṭakaṃ gahetvāna pade cakkamapūjayiṃ   
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi padapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakoṭakakoraṇḍadāyako  thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sakoṭakakoraṇḍadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
     Daṇḍadāyakattharāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kānanaṃ vanamogayha veḷuṃ chetvānahaṃ tadā 
 Ālambataṃ gahetvāna   saṅghassa adadaṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tena cittappasādena subbate abhivādiya 
 Ālambanampi datvāna pakkamiṃ uttarāmukho 
  
   Padacakkaṃ apūjayiṃ machasaṃ   Sakosakakoraṇḍadāyako machasaṃ   Karitvāna 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ daṇḍamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi daṇḍadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā daṇḍadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Daṇḍadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Ambayāgudāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sataraṃsi nāma sambuddho sayambhu aparājito 
 Vuṭṭahitvā samādhimhā bhikkhāya maṃ upāgami 
  
      Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna ambayāguṃ adāsahaṃ 
 Vippasannamanaṃ tassa vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ambayāguyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambayāgudāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ambayāgudāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Supuṭakapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Divāvihārā nikkhanto vipassi lokanāyako 
 Bhikkhāya vicaranto so mama santikamupāgami 
  
      Kato patito sumano buddhaseṭṭassa tādino 
 Loṇasupuṭakaṃ datvā kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ supuṭakamadāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi puṭakassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā supuṭakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Supuṭakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Mañcadāyakattharāpadānaṃ 
      Vipassino bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Ekaṃ mañcaṃ mayā dinnaṃ pasannena sapāṇinā 
  
      Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ dibbayānaṃ samajjhagaṃ 
 Tena mañcakadānena pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ mañcamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi mañcadānasasidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mañcadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mañcadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Saraṇagamaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Āruhimha tadā nāmaṃ bhikkhu cājivako cahaṃ 
 Nāvāya bhijjamānāya bhikkhu me saraṇaṃ adā 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ ca me saraṇaṃ adā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saraṇagamane phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Saraṇagamaniyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Piṇḍajapātikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tisso nāmāsi sambuddho vihāsi vipite tadā 
 Tusitā hi idhāgantvā piṇḍapātamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Sambuddhamabhivādetvā tissaṃ nāma mahāyasaṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piṇaḍapātiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Piṇḍapātikattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Saddasaññi yavasiko kiṃsu koraṇḍapupphiyo 
 Ālambano ambayāgu supaṭī mañcadāyako 
 Saraṇa piṇḍapāto da gāthā tāḷisameva ca 
   Saddasaññakavaggo jattiṃsatimo   
  
                   
  
     Mandāravapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Tāvatiṃsā idhāgantvā maṅgalo nāma māṇavo 
 Mandāravaṃ gahetvāna vipassissa mahesino 
  
      Samādhināna nisinnassa matthake dhārayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Sattāhaṃ dhārayivona devalokaṃ punāgamiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mandāravapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mandāravapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Kakkārupupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Yāmā devā idhāgantvā gotamaṃ sirivacchasaṃ 
 Kakkārupupphaṃ   paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ buddhamabhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kakkārupupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kakkārupuppiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Bhisamuḷāladāyakattharāpadānaṃ 
  
      Phusso nāmāsi sambuddho sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Vivekakāmo sappañño āgacchi mama santike 
  
      Tasmiṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā mahākāruṇike jite 
 Bhisaṃ muḷālaṃ paggayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
  
   Kakkārumālaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ bhisamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisamuḷāladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bhisamuḷāladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Kesarapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ   
  
      Vijjādharo tadā asiṃ himavattambhi pabbate 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ caṅkamantaṃ mahāyasaṃ 
  
      Tīṇi kesaripupphāni   sise katvānahaṃ tadā 
 Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ vessabhuṃ abhipujayiṃ 
  
      Ekatise ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kesarapupphiyo   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kesarapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Aṅkolapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumo nāma sambuddho cittakūṭe vasi tadā 
 Disvāna tamahaṃ buddhaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ   
  
      Aṅkolaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā ocinitvānahaṃ tadā 
 Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ pujesiṃ padumaṃ jinaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā aṅkolapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Aṅkolapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
   Kesaripupphāni simu   Kesaripupphiyo simu   Upagacchahaṃ simu 
  kesaripupphiyattherāapadāna simu 
  
                   
  
     Kadambapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe 
 Kañcanagaghiyasaṅkāsaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ 
  
      Nisajja pāsādavare addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Kadambapupphaṃ paggayha vipassiṃ abhipujayiṃ 
  
                   
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kadambapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kadambapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Uddālapupaphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Anomo   nāma sambuddho gaṅgākule vasī tadā 
 Uddālakaṃ gahetvāna pujayiṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uddālapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Uddālapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Ekacampakapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Upasanto ca sambuddho vati pabbatantare 
 Ekaṃ campakamādāya   upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano paccekamunimuttamaṃ 
 Ubhohatthehi paggayha pujayiṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekacampakapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekacampakapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sujāto syā   Ekacampakamādāya machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Timirapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānaditire anusotaṃ cajāmahaṃ 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ sālarāpaṃva phullitaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pasannacitto sumano paccekamunimuttamaṃ 
 Gahetvā timiraṃ pupphaṃ matthake okiriṃ ahaṃ 
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujayidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā timirapupaphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Timirapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Salalapupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ kintaro tadā 
 Tatthaddasaṃ devadevaṃ caṅkamantaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
      Ocinitvāna salaṃ pupphaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ 
 Upasiṅghi mahāviru salalaṃ devagandhikaṃ 
  
      Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho vipassi lokanāyako 
 Upasiṅghi mahāvīro pekkhamānassa me sato 
  
      Pasantacitto sumano vanditvā dipaduttamaṃ 
 Añajalimpaggahetvāna puna pabbatamāruhiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā salalapupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sallapupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Mandāravañca kakkāru bhisa kesarapupphiyo 
 Aṅkolako kadamabi ca uddāla ekacampako 
 Timiraṃ salalañceva gāthā tāḷisa evaṃ ca 
   Mandāravapupphiyavaggo sattatiṃsatimo   
  
                   
                   
  
     Bodhivandakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Pāṭiliṃ haritaṃ disvā pādapaṃ dharaṇiruhaṃ 
 Ekaṃsaṃ añjaliṃ katvā avandiṃ pāṭaliṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna garuṃ katvāna mānasaṃ 
 Antosuddhaṃ bahisuddhaṃ suvimuttamanāsavaṃ 
  
      Vipassiṃ lokamahitaṃ karuṇāñāṇasāgaraṃ 
 Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ avandiṃ pāṭaliṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ bodhimabhivandahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi vandānāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhivandako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bodhivandakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
     Pāṭalipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vipassi nāma bhagavā sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Purakkhato sasissehi bandhumaṃ pāvisi jino   
  
      Tīṇi pāṭalipupphāni ucchaṅge ṭhapitāni me 
 Sīsaṃ nahātukāmova   nadititthaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
      Nikkhamma bandhumatiyā addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Indivaraṃva jalitaṃ ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ 
  
      Vyagghusabhaṃva pavaraṃ abhijātaṃva kesariṃ 
 Gacchantaṃ samaṇānaggaṃ bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ 
  
      Tasmiṃ pasanto sugate kilesamaladhovane 
 Gahetvā tīṇi pupphāni buddhaseṭṭhamapujayiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭalipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pāṭalipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Pāvisi bandhumaṃ jino machasaṃ   Nahāyitukāmova machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Tiuppalamāliyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānaditire ahosiṃ vānaro tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
  
      Obhāsentaṃ disā sabbā sāralarajaṃva phullitaṃ 
 Tīṇi uppalapupphāni matthake abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Udaggacitto sumano pitiyā haṭṭhamānaso 
 Tīṇi uppalapuphāni matthake abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Pujayitvāna pupphāni phussassāhaṃ mahesino 
 Sagāravo bhavitvāna pāpuṇiṃ jīvitakkhayaṃ 
  
      Gacchanto paṭikuṭiko vippasanne cetasā 
 Selantare patitvāna pāpuṇiṃ jīvitakkhayaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetakāpaṇidhihi ca 
 Jahitvā purimaṃ jātiṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
      Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Satānaṃ pañcakkhattañca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
  
      Dvenavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiuppalamāliyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tiuppalamāliyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Paṭaṭipupphiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Yadā nibbāsi   sambuddho masi padumuttaro 
 Samāgamma janā sabbe sarīraṃ niyaranti te 
  
      Nīharante sarīrambhi vajjamānāsu bherisu 
 Pasannacitto sumano paṭṭipupphaṃ apūjayiṃ   
  
      Satasahasse ito kapepa yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ 
 Duttiṃ nābhijānāmi sarīrapujite phalaṃ 
  
   Tiṇuppalamāliyatherāpadānaṃ machasaṃ   Disvānattamano machasaṃ   Nibbāyi 
 machasaṃ   Paṭṭipupphamabhipūjayiṃ simu 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṭṭipupphiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Paṭṭipupphiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Sattapaṇaṇiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumano nāma sambuddho uppajji lokanāyako 
 Pasannacitto sumano sattapaṇṇimapujayiṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe sattapaṇṇimapujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sattapaṇṇissidaṃ   phalaṃ 
  
       Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
       Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattapaṇṇiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sattapaṇṇiyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Gandhamuṭṭhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Citake kariyamāne nānāgandhe samāhaṭe 
 Pasannacitto sumano gandhamuṭṭhimapujayiṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe citakaṃ yaṃ apūjayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Sattapaṇṇāpujāyidaṃ phalaṃ machasaṃ              uppaṭipāṭiyā āgataṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā gandhamuṭṭhiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Gandhamuṭṭhiyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Citakapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Parinibbute bhagavati jalajuttama nāmake 
 Āropitambhi citake sālapupphamapujayiṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe sattapaṇṇimapujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi citapujayidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā citakapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Citakapujakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Sumanatālavaṇaṭiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhathesa bhagavato tālavaṇṭamadāsahaṃ 
 Sumanehi paṭicchannaṃ dhārayāmi mahārahaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe tālavaṇṭamadāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tālavaṇṭassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanatālavaṇṭiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sumanatālavaṇṭiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Sumanadāmiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato nhātakassa tapassino 
 Katvāna sumanadāmaṃ dhārayiṃ purato ṭhito 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dāmamabhidhārayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sumanādhāraṇe    phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanadāmiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sumanadāmiyattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Kāsumāriphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ nisinnaṃ pabbatantare 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Kāsumāriphalaṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsasahaṃ 
  
      Ekitiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
   Yaṃ dāmaṃ dhārayiṃ tadā machasaṃ   Sumanadhāraṇe phalaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kāsumāriphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kāsumāriphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Bodhi pāṭali uppalī paṭṭi ca sattapaṇṇiyo 
 Gandhamuṭṭhi ca citako tālaṃ sumanadāmako 
 Kāsumāriphali ceva gāthā ekunasaṭṭhikā 
   Bodhivandakavaggo aṭṭatiṃsatimo   
  
     Avaṇaṭaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sataraṃsi nāma bhagavā sayambhu aparājino 
 Vivekakāmo sambuddho gocarāyābhinikkhami 
  
      Phalahattho ahaṃ disvā upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Pasannacittā sumano avaṇṭaṃ adadiṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ ahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avaṇaṭaphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Avaṇaṭaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Labujadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare bandhumatiyā āsiṃ ārāmiko tadā 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ gacchantaṃ anilañajase 
  
      Labujassa phalaṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhadhammasukhāvahaṃ 
 Ākase ṭhitako santo paṭigaṇhi mahāyaso 
  
      Vittisañajananaṃ mayhaṃ diṭṭhadhammasukhāvahaṃ 
 Phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Adhigacchiṃ tadā pitiṃ vipulañca sukhuttamaṃ 
 Uppajjateva ratanaṃ nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassida  phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā labujadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Labujadāyakatherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
     Udumbaraphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vinatānadiyā tīre vihāsi purisuttamo 
 Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ 
  
      Tasmiṃ pasannamanaso kilesamaladhovane 
 Udumbaraphalaṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udumbaraphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Udumbaraphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                   
  
      Pilakkhaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vanante buddhaṃ disvāna atthadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano pilakkhassa phalaṃ adaṃ   
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pilakkhaphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pilakkhaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Phārusaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ āhutinaṃ paṭiggahaṃ 
 Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ phārusaphalamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ ahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
   Pilakkhassādadiṃ phalaṃ machasaṃ  phārusadāyakattherāapadāna machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā phārusaphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Phārusaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Valliphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
      Sabbe janā samāgamma agamiṃsu vanaṃ tadā 
 Phalamanvesamānā te alabhiṃsu phalaṃ tadā 
  
      Tatthadadasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano valliphalamadāsahaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ palamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānasasidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā valaliphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Valaliphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Kadaliphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jalitaṃ puṇṇamāseva   candimaṃ 
 Jalantaṃ diparukkhaṃva addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Kadaliphalaṃ paggayha adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano candivatvāna apakkamiṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Puṇṇamāyeva machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kadaliphaladāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kadaliphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
     Panasaphaladāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ajjuno nāma sambuddho bhimavante vasi tadā 
 Caraṇena ca sampanno samādhikusalo muni 
  
      Kumbhamattaṃ gahetvāna panasaṃ jivajivakaṃ 
 Chattapaṇṇe ṭhapetvāna adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā panasaphaladāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Panasaphaladāyakattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
     Soṇakoṭivisattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Vipassino pāvacane ekaṃ leṇaṃ mayā kataṃ 
 Cātuddisassa saṅghassa bandhumārājadhāniyā 
  
      Dussehi bhumiṃ leṇassa santharitvā pariccajiṃ 
 Udaggacitto sumano akāsiṃ paṇidhiṃ tadā 
  
                   
  
      Ārādhayeyyaṃ sambuddhaṃ pabbajjañca labheyyahaṃ 
 Anuttarañca nibbāṇaṃ phuseyyaṃ santimuttamaṃ 
  
      Teneva sukkamūlena kappaṃ   navuti saṃsariṃ 
 Devabhuto manusso vā katapuñño virocahaṃ 
  
      Tato kammāvasesena idha pacchimake bhave 
 Campāyaṃ aggaseṭṭhissa jātombhi ekaputtako 
  
      Jātamattassa me sutvā pitu chando ayaṃ ahu 
 Dadāmahaṃ kumārassa visakoṭi anutakā 
  
      Caturaṅgulā ca me lomā jātā pādatale ubho 
 Sukhumā mudusamphassā tulapicusamā subhā 
  
      Atitā navuti kappā ayamekova   uttari 
 Nābhijānāmi nikkhitte pāde bhumyā asanthate 
  
      Ārādhito me sambuddho pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Arahattañca me pattaṃ sitibhutombhi nibbuto 
  
      Aggo āraddhaviriyānaṃ   nidadiṭṭho sabbadassinā 
 Khiṇāsavo ca   arahā chaḷabhiñño mahiddhiko 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi lenadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Thero koṭiviso   soṇo bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato 
 Pañcahaṃ puṭṭho viyākāsi anotatte mahāsareti 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇo koṭiviso thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Soṇakoṭivisattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
   Kappe machasaṃ   Aayaṃ ekoca machasaṃ   Āraddhaviriyānaṃ machasaṃ   
 Khiṇāsavomhi machasaṃ   Koṭiviso machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Pubbakammapilotikāpadānaṃ 
  
      Anotattasarāsante ramaṇiye silātale 
 Nānāratanapajjote nānāgandhavanannare 
  
      Mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena pareto lokanāyako 
 Āsino vyākari tattha pubbakammāni attano 
  
      Suṇātha bhikkhavo mayhaṃ yaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā 
 Pilotikassa kammassa buddhattepi vipaccati  
  
      Munāḷi nāmahaṃ dhutto pubbe aññāsu jātisu 
 Paccekabuddhaṃ sarabhuṃ   abbhācikkhiṃ adūsakaṃ 
  
      Tena kammavipākena niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ 
 Abbhakkhānaṃ mayā laddhaṃ sundarikāya kāraṇā 
  
      Tena kammāvasesena idha pacchimake bhave 
 Abbhakkhānaṃ mayā laddhaṃ sundharikāya kāraṇā 
  
      Sabbābhibhussa buddhassa nando nāmāsi sāvako 
 Taṃ abbhakkhāya niraye ciraṃ saṃsaritaṃ mayā 
  
      Dasavassasahassāni niraye saṃsariṃ ciraṃ 
 Manussabhāvaṃ laddhāhaṃ abbhakkhānaṃ bahuṃ labhiṃ 
  
      Tena kammāvasesena ciñcamānavikā mamaṃ 
 Abbhakkhāsi   abhutena janakāyassa aggato 
  
      Brāhmaṇo sutavā āsiṃ ahaṃ sakkatapujito 
 Mahāvane pañcasate mante vācemi māṇave 
  
      Tatthāgato isi bhimo pañcabhiñño mahiddhiko 
 Tañcāhamāgataṃ disvā abbhācikkhimadūsakaṃ 
  
      Tatohaṃ avacaṃ sisse kāmabhogi ayaṃ isi 
 Mayhampi bhāsamānassa anumodiṃsu māṇavā 
  
      Tato māṇavakā sabbe bhikkhamānā   kule kule 
 Mahājanassa āhaṃsu kāmabhogī ayaṃ isi 
  
   Suṇātha bhikkhave mayhaṃ kammaṃ pakataṃ mayā ekaṃ araññikaṃ bhikkhuṃ disvā 
 dinnaṃ pilotikaṃ patthitaṃ paṭhamaṃ buddhaṃ buddhatatāya mayā tadā pitikessa 
 kammassa buddhattepivipaccati gopālako pure āsiṃ gāciṃ pājeti gocaraṃ pivantiṃ udakaṃ 
 ācilaṃ gāviṃ disvā nivārayiṃ tena kamamavipākena idha pacchimake bhave pipāsito 
 yadicchakaṃ na hi pātuṃ labhāmahaṃ syā 
   Surabhiṃ machasaṃ   Saṃsaritaṃ machasaṃ   Abbhācikkhi machasaṃ   Bhikkhamānaṃ 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Tena kammavipakena pañca bhikkhusatā ime 
 Abbhakkhānaṃ labhuṃ sabbe sundarikāya kāraṇā 
  
      Vemātubhātaraṃ pubbe dhanahetu haniṃ ahaṃ 
 Pakkhipiṃ giriduggasmiṃ silāya ca apiṃsayiṃ 
  
      Tena kammavipakena devadatto sīlaṃ khipi 
 Aṅguṭṭhaṃ piṃsayi pāde mama pāsāraṇasakkharā 
  
      Purebhaṃ dārako hutvā kiḷamāno mahāpathe 
 Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna magge sakalikaṃ khipiṃ   
  
      Tena kammavipākena idha pacchimake bhave 
 Vadhatthaṃ maṃ devadatto abhimāre payojayi 
  
      Hatthāroho pure āsiṃ paccekamunimuttamaṃ 
 Piṇḍāya vicarantaṃ taṃ āsādesiṃ gajetahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammavipākena bhanto nālāgiri gajo 
 Giribbaje puracare dāruṇo maṃ upāgami   
  
      Rājāhaṃ patthivo   āsiṃ sattinā purisaṃ hatiṃ 
 Tena kammavipākena niraye paccisaṃ bhusaṃ 
  
      Kammuno tassa sesena idāni sakalaṃ mama 
 Pāde chaviṃ pakopesi   na hi kammaṃ vinassati 
  
      Ahaṃ kevaṭṭagāmasmiṃ ahuṃ kevaṭṭadārako 
 Macchake ghātite disvā janayiṃ somanassakaṃ 
  
      Tena kammavipākena sisadukkhaṃ ahu mama 
 Sabbe sakkā ca haññiṃsu yadā hati viḍuḍabho   
  
      Phussassāhaṃ pāvacane sāvake paribhāsayiṃ 
 Yavaṃ khādatha bhuñjatha mā ca bhujajatha sālayo   
  
                   
  
      Tena kammavipākena temāsaṃ khāditaṃ yavaṃ 
 Nimantito brāhmaṇena verañajāyaṃ vasiṃ   tadā 
  
      Nibbuddhe vattamānambhi mallaputtaṃ niheṭhayiṃ  
 Tena kammavilākena piṭṭhidukkhaṃ mamaṃ ahuṃ 
  
   Dabhiṃ syā   Samupāgami machasaṃ   Pattiko syā   Pakappesi machasaṃ   
 Viḍḍubho machasaṃ   Sāliyo simu   Vasaṃ simu   Nisedhayiṃ syā 
  
                   
  
      Tikicchako ahaṃ āsiṃ seṭṭhiputtaṃ viceyiṃ 
 Tena kammavipākena hoti pakkhandikā mama 
  
      Avacāhaṃ jotipālo sugataṃ kassapaṃ tadā 
 Kuto nu bodhi muṇḍassa bodhi paramadullabhā 
  
      Tena kammavipākena acariṃ dukkaraṃ bahuṃ 
 Chabbassānuruvelāyaṃ tato bodhimapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Nāhaṃ etena maggenana pāpuṇiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ 
 Kummaggena gavesissaṃ pubbakammena cārito 
  
      Puññapāpaparikkhiṇo sabbasantāpavajjito 
 Asoko anupāyoso nibbāyissamanāsavo 
  
      Evaṃ jino viyākāsi bhikkhusaṅghassa aggato 
 Sabbābhiññābalappatto anotatte mahāsare 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhagavā attano pubbacaritaṃ pubbakammapilotikaṃ  nāma dhammapariyāyaṃ 
 abhāsi Pubbakammapilotikaṃ nāma buddhāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Avaṇṭaṃ labujañceva udumbarapilakkhu ca 
 Phāru valli ca kādali panaso koṭivisako 
 Pubbakammapiloti ca apadānaṃ mahesino 
 Gāthāyo ekanavuti gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi 
   Avaṇṭaphalavaggo ekunavatatālisatimo   
  
                   
  
     Piḷindicchattherāpadānaṃ 
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā āsiṃ dovāriko ahaṃ 
 Akkhohaṃ amitaṃ bhogaṃ ghare santivitaṃ mama 
  
      Raho gato nisīditvā sampahaṃsitva   mānasaṃ 
 Nisajja pāsādavare evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
  
      Bahu   medhigatā bhogā phītaṃ antepuraṃ mama 
 Rājāpi sannimantesi aānando paṭhavissaro   
  
   Kammapilonikaṃ machasaṃ   Pahaṃsitvāna machasaṃ   Pahu machasaṃ   
 Pathavisasaro machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Ayañca buddho uppanno adhiccuppattiko muni 
 Saṃvijjanti ca me bhogā dānaṃ dassāmi satthuno 
  
      Padumana rājaputtena dinnaṃ dānavaraṃ jane 
 Hatthināge ca pallaṅke apassenañcanappakaṃ 
  
      Ahampi dānaṃ dassāmi saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ bhavissaṃ ādikammiko 
  
      Cintetvāhaṃ bahuvidhaṃ yāge yassa sukhaṃ phalaṃ 
 Parikkhāradānamadadakkhiṃ mama saṅkapappuraṇaṃ 
  
      Parikkhārāni dassāmi saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Adinnapubbamaññesaṃ bhavissaṃ ādikammiko 
  
      Naḷakāre apāgamma chattaṃ kāreyiṃ tāvade 
 Chattasatasahassāni ekato sannipātayiṃ 
  
      Dussasatasahassāni ekato sannipātayiṃ 
 Pattasatasahassāni ekato sannipātayiṃ 
  
      Vāsiyo satthake cāpi suciyo takhacheke   
 Heṭṭhā chatte laggāpesiṃ   kāretvā tadanucchave 
  
      Vidhupane tālavaṇeṭa morahatthe ca cāmare 
 Parissāvane teladhare   kārayiṃ tadanucchave 
  
      Sucighare aṃsakhandhe athopi kāyabandhane 
 Ādhārake ca sukate kārayiṃ tadanucchave 
  
      Paribhogabhājane ca athopi lohathālake 
                   
 Bhesajje purayitvana heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapesahaṃ 
  
      Vacaṃ usiraṃ laṭṭhimadhuṃ pipphali marivacāti ca 
 Haritakiṃ siṅgiveraṃ   sabaṃ puresiṃ bhājane 
  
      Osadhañajananāḷi ca   salākā dhammakuttarā 
 Kuñcikā pañcavaṇṇehi sibbite kuñcikāghare 
      Āyoge dhumanette ca athopi dipadhārake 
 Tumbake ca karaṇḍe ca kārayiṃ tadanucchave 
  
   Nakhachedane machasaṃ   hapāpesiṃ machasaṃ   Teladhāre machasaṃ   Siṅgiveraṃ 
 machasaṃ   Upāhanā machasaṃ   Osadhaṃ añajanāpi ca syā 
  
                   
  
      Saṇḍāse pipphale ceva athopi malahārake 
 Bhesajjathavike ceva kārayiṃ tadanucchave 
  
      Āsandiyo piṭhake ca pallaṅke caturomaye 
 Tadanucchave kārayitvā heṭṭhāchatte ṭhapesahaṃ 
      Uṇṇābhisi tulabhisi athopi piṭhikābhisi  
 Bimbohane   ca sukate kārayiṃ tadanucchave 
  
      Kuruvinde madhusitthe telaṃ hatthappatāpakaṃ 
 Sipāṭi phalake suci mañcamattharaṇena ca 
  
      Senāsane pādapuñecha sayanāsanadaṇḍake 
 Dantapoṇe ca āṭali sisālepanagandhake 
  
      Araṇi palālapiṭhe   ca pattapidhānathālake 
 Udakassa kaṭacchu ca cuṇṇakaṃ rajanammaṇaṃ   
  
      Sammajjanaṃ   udapattaṃ tathā vassikasāṭikaṃ 
 Nisidanaṃ kaṇḍuchādi atha antaravāsakaṃ 
  
      Uttarāsaṅgasaṅghāṭi natthukaṃ mukhasodhanaṃ 
 Bilaṅgaloṇaṃ putaṃ ca madhuñca dadhipānakaṃ 
  
      Dhupaṃ sitthaṃ piloticañca mukhapuñacha nasuttakaṃ 
 Dātabbaṃ nāma yaṃ atthi yaṃ ca kappati sutthuno 
  
      Sabbametaṃ samānetvā ānandaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ 
                   
 Upasaṅkamma rājānaṃ janetāraṃ mahesino  
 Sirasā abhivādetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Ekato jātasaṃvaddhā ubhinnaṃ ekato manaṃ  
 Sādhāraṇā sukhadukkhe ubho ca anuvattakā 
  
      Atthi cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ tavādheyyaṃ arindama 
 Yadi sakosi taṃ dukkhaṃ vinodeyyāsi khattiya 
  
      Tava dukkhaṃ mamaṃ   dukkhaṃ ubhinnaṃ ekato manaṃ  
 Niṭṭhitanti vijānāhi mamādheyyaṃ sace tuvaṃ 
  
      Jānābhi me mahārāja dukkhaṃ me dubbinodayaṃ 
 Pahu samano gajjassu ekaṃ te duccajaṃ varaṃ 
  
   Piṭhakābhisi syā   Bibbohane syā   Phalapiṭhe machasaṃ   Rajanambaṇaṃ machasaṃ 
   Samamuñajanaṃ syā   Mahesinaṃ simu mahāyasaṃ syā   Yaso syā   Mama   Mano 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yāvatā vijitaṃ atthi mama jīvitaṃ 
 Etehi yadi te attho dassāmi avikampito 
  
      Gajjitaṃ kho tayā deva micchā taṃ bahugajjitaṃ 
 Jānissāmi tuvaṃ ajja sabbadhamme patiṭṭhitaṃ 
  
      Atibālhaṃ tipiḷesi dadamānassa me sato 
 Kinte me pilitenattho patthitaṃ te kathehi me 
  
      Icchāmahaṃ mahārājā buddhaseṭṭhamanuttaraṃ 
 Bhojayissāmi sambuddhaṃ vajjaṃ me māhu jīvitaṃ 
  
      Aññaṃ tehaṃ varaṃ dammi mā yācittho tathāgataṃ  
 Adeyyo kassaci buddho maṇijotiraso yathā 
  
      Nanu te gajjitaṃ deva yāva jīvitamattano  
 Jīvitaṃ dadamānena yuttaṃ dātuṃ tathāgataṃ 
  
      hapaniyo mahāvīro adeyyo kassaci jino 
 Na me paṭissuto buddho carassu amitaṃ dhanaṃ 
  
      Vinicchayaṃ pāpuṇāma puccissāmi vinicchaye 
 Yathāsantaṃ  kathessanti paṭipucchāma taṃ tathā 
  
      Rañño hatthe hahetthāna agamāsiṃ vinicchayaṃ 
 Parato   akkhadassānaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
                   
  
      Suṇantu me akkhadassā jīvitampi pacārayi  
 Na kiñci ṭhapayitvāna rājā varamadāsi me  
  
      Tassa me varadinnassa buddhaseṭṭhaṃ variṃ ahaṃ 
 Sudinno hoti me buddho athavā   saṃsayaṃ mama 
  
      Sossāma tava vacanaṃ bhumipālassa rājino 
 Ubhinnaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā chindissāmettha saṃsayaṃ 
  
      Sabbaṃ deva tayā dinnaṃ imassa sabbagāhikaṃ  
 Na kiñci ṭhapayitvāna jīvitampi pavārayi 
  
   Ayācito tathāgato syā   Javitamatthikaṃ syā   Yathāsaṇḍaṃ machasaṃ   Rājā 
 varamadāsi me machasaṃ   Jīvitampi pavārayi machasaṃ   Sabbagāhitaṃ syā     Se 
    purato 
  
                   
  
      Kicchappattova hutvāna yāci caramanuttaraṃ  
 Imaṃ sudukkhitaṃ ñātvā adāsiṃ sabbagābhikaṃ 
      Parājāyo tavaṃ   deva assa deyyo tathāgato 
 Ubhinnaṃ saṃsayo jinno yathāsantambhi   tiṭṭhatha 
  
      Rājā tattheva ṭhatvāna akkhadasestadabravi 
 Sammā mayhampi deyyātha puna buddhaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Puretvā tava saṅkappaṃ bhojayitvā tathāgataṃ 
 Puna deyyāsi sambuddhaṃ ānandassa yasasino 
  
      Akkhadassebhivādetvā ānandañcāpi khattiyaṃ 
 Tuṭṭho pamudito hutvā sambuddamupasaṅkamiṃ 
  
      Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
 Sirasā abhivādetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Vasisatasahassehi adhivāsehi cakkhuma 
 Hāsayanto mamaṃ   cittaṃ nivesanamupehi me 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya adhivāsesi cakkhumā 
  
      Adhivāsanamaññāya abhivādiya satthuno 
 Haṭṭho udaggacittohaṃ nivesanamupāgamiṃ 
  
      Mittāmacce samānetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
 Sudullabho mayā laddho maṇi jotiraso yathā 
  
      Kena taṃ pujayissāma appameyyo anupamo 
 Atulo asamo dhīro jino appaṭipuggalo 
  
      Tathā samasamo ceva adutiyo narāsabho 
 Dukkaraṃ adhikāraṃ hi buddhānucchavikaṃ mayā 
  
                   
  
      Nānāpupphe samānetvā karoma pupphamaṇḍapaṃ 
 Buddhānucchavikaṃ etaṃ sabbapujā bhavissati 
  
   Yāvajivamanuttaraṃ syā   Tuvaṃ machasaṃ   Yathāsaṇḍamhi machasaṃ   Mama 
 cittaṃ machasaṃ 
                   
  
      Uppalaṃ padumaṃ cāpi vassikaṃ adhimuttakaṃ 
 Campakaṃ nāgapupphañca maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Satāsanasahassāni chattacachāyāya paññapiṃ 
 Pacchimaṃ āsanaṃ mayhaṃ adhikaṃ satamagghati 
  
      Satāsanasahassāni chattacchāyāya paññapiṃ 
 Paṭiyādetvā antapānaṃ kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Ārocitambhi kālambhi padumuttaro mahāmuni 
 Vasi satasahassehi nivesanamupesi me 
  
      Dhārentamupicchatte   suphullapupphamaṇḍape 
 Visasatasahassehi nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Chattasatasahassāni satasahassamāsanaṃ 
 Kappiyaṃ anavajjañca paṭigaṇhābhi cakkhuma 
  
      Padumuttaro lovidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mamaṃ tāretukāmo so sampaṭicchi mahāmuni 
  
      Bhikkhuno ekamekassa paccekaṃ pattadāsahaṃ 
 Jabhiṃsu pubbakaṃ   pattaṃ lohapattamadhārasuṃ 
  
      Sattarattandavaṃ buddho nisīdi pupphamaṇḍape 
 Bodhayanto bahu satte dhammacakkaṃ pavattayi 
  
      Dhammacakkaṃ pavatente   heṭṭhato pupphamaṇḍape 
 Culalāsitisahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu 
  
      Sattame divase pate padumuttaro mahāmuni 
 Chattacchāyāya māsino imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Anunakaṃ dānavaraṃ yo me pādāsi māṇavo 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
      Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅgini 
 Parivāressantimaṃ   niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ savikā sandamānikā 
 Upaṭṭhissantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni   bheriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Vajjayissanatimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Dhārentaṃ uparicchattaṃ machasaṃ   Sumahakaṃ machasaṃ sambhataṃ syā   
 Pavattento machasaṃ   Taṃ syā   Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Chaḷāsitisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Vicittavatthabharaṇā āvuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   
  
      Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 Parivāressantimaṃ niccaṃ sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
      Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Devaloke vasantassa puññakammasamaṅgino 
 Devalokapariyattaṃ ratanachattaṃ dhariyati   
  
      Icchissati yadā chāyaṃ   chadanaṃ dussapupphajaṃ 
 Imassa cittamaññāya nibaddhaṃ chādayissati 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamupena codito 
 Puññakamme na saṃyutto brahmabandhu bhavissati 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati 
  
      Piḷindivaccha   nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
 Devānaṃ asurānañca gandhabbānaṃ ca sakkato 
  
      Bhikkhunaṃ bhikkhunīyaṃ ca gihīnaṃ ca tatheva so 
 Piyo hutvāna sabbesaṃ viharissatanāsavo  
  
      Satasahasesa kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumutto saravegova kilese jhāpayī mama   
  
      Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ puññakkhette anuttare 
 Yattha kāraṃ karitvāna pattombhi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Anutakaṃ dānavaraṃ adāsi yo hi māṇavo 
 Ādi pubbaṅgamo āsi tassa dānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Chatte sugate datvāna   saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
                   
  
      Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ na jānāmi rajojallaṃ na limpati 
 Anupaddavo aniti ca homi apacitto sadā 
  
   Āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā machasaṃ   Dharissati machasaṃ   Yadāvāyaṃ syā   Gottena 
 machasaṃ   Piḷindavaccha machasaṃ   Jhāpayissati simu   Chatte ca sugate datvā 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Sukhumacchaviko homi visadaṃ hoti mānasaṃ 
 Chattasatasahassāni bhave saṃsarato mama 
  
      Sabbālaṅkārayuttāni tassa kammassa vāhasā 
 Imaṃ jātiṃ ṭhapetvāna matthake dhārayanti me 
  
      Kasmā   imāya rātiyā natthi me chattadhāraṇā 
 Mama sabbaṃ kataṃ kammaṃ vimuttichattapattiyaṃ 
  
      Dussāni sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavarutteme 
 Aṭṭānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo virajo sappabhāso patāpavā 
 Siniddhaṃ hoti me gattaṃ bhave saṃsarato mama 
  
      Dussasatasahassāni setā pitā ca lohitā 
 Dhārenti matthake mayhaṃ dussadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Koseyyakambaliyāni khomakappāsikāni ca 
 Sabbattha paṭilabhāmi tesaṃ nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Patte sugate datvāna saṅghe gaṇavarutatame 
 Dasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Suvaṇṇathāle maṇithāle rajate pi ca thālake 
 Lohitaṃkamaye thāle paribhuñajāmi sabbadā 
  
      Anupaddavo aniti ca homi apacito sadā 
 Lābhi antassa pānassa vatthassa sayanassa ca 
  
      Na vinassanti me bhogā ṭhitacitto bhavāmahaṃ 
 Dhammakāmo sadā homi appakleso anāsavo 
  
      Devaloke manussa vā anubandhā ime guṇā 
 Chāyā yathāpi rukkhassa sabbattha na jahanti maṃ 
  
      Cittabandhanasambaddhā sukatā vāsiyo bahu 
 Datvāna buddhaseṭṭassa saṅghassa ca tathevahaṃ 
 Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
                   
  
      Suro homavisāri ca vesārajjesu pārami 
 Dhiti viriyavā bhomi paggahītamano sadā 
  
      Kilesacchedanaṃ ñāṇaṃ sukhumaṃ atulaṃ suciṃ 
 Sabbattha paṭilabhāmi tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
   Tasmā syā 
  
                   
  
      Akakkase apharuse sudhote satthake bahu 
 Pasannacitto datvāna buddhe saṅghe tatheva ca 
  
      Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
 Kalyāṇacittaṃ viriyaṃ khattiñca mettasatthakaṃ 
  
      Taṇhāsallassa chinnattā paññāsatthaṃ anuttaraṃ 
 Vajirena samaṃ ñāṇaṃ tesaṃ nissandato labhe 
  
      Suciyo sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavarutteme 
 Pañcānisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Na saṃsayo kaṅkhacchedo abhirūpo ca bhogavā 
 Tikkhapañño sadā homi saṃsaranto bhavābhave 
  
      Gamhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ atthaṃ ñaṇena passayiṃ 
 Vajiraggasamaṃ ñāṇaṃ hoti me tamaghātanaṃ 
  
      Nakhacchedane sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Pañcanisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Dāsidāse gavasse bhatake ārakkhake bahu  
 Nhāpite bhattake sude sabbattheva labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Vidhupane sugate datvā tālavaṇṭe ca sobhane 
 Aṭṭhānisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ jānāmi pariḷāho na vijjati 
 Darathaṃ nābhijānāmi cittasantāpanaṃ mama 
  
      Rāgaggi dosamohaggi mānaggi diṭṭiaggi ca 
 Sabbaggi nibbutā mayhaṃ tassa nisasandato mama 
  
      Morahatthe cāmariyo datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Upasantakilesohaṃ virāmi anaṅgaṇo 
  
                   
  
      Parissāvane sugate datvā dhammakaruttama  
 Pañcanisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sabbesaṃ samatikkhamma dibbaṃ āyuṃ labhāmahaṃ 
 Appasayho sadā homi corapaccatthikehi ca 
  
   Nāṭake bahu machasaṃ   Datvā sukate dhammakuttare syā 
  
                   
  
      Satthena vā visena vā vihesampi na kubbate 
 Antarā maraṇaṃ natthi tesaṃ nissandato mama 
  
      Teladhare   sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sucārurūpo sugado   susamuggatamānaso 
 Acikkhittamano homi sabbārakkehi rakkhito 
  
      Sucighare sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Cetosukhaṃ kāyasukhaṃ iriyāpathajaṃ sukhaṃ 
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhāmi   tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Aṃsakhandhe   jite datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Cetoñāṇañca vindāmi sarāmi dutiyaṃ bhavaṃ 
 Sabbattha succhivi homi tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
      Kāyabandhe jine datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Chānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Samādhīsu na kampāmi vasī homi samādhisu 
 Abhejjapariso homi ādeyyavacano sadā 
  
      Upaṭṭitasati homi taso vayhaṃ na vijjati 
 Devaloke manusse vā anubandhā ime guṇe 
  
      Ādhārake jine datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcavaṇṇehi dāyādo   acalo homi kenaci 
  
                   
  
      Ye keci me sutā dhammā satiñāṇappabodhanā 
 Dhatā me na vinassanti bhavanti sucinicchitā 
  
      Bhājane paribhoge ca datvā buddhe gaṇuttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      So ṇṇamaye maṇimaye atho pi phalikāmaye 
 Lohitaṃkamaye ceva labhāmi bhājane ahaṃ 
  
   Teladhāre machasaṃ   Subhaddo machasaṃ   Paṭilabhe machasaṃ   Aṃsabaddhe 
 machasaṃ   Pañcavaṇṇe bhayābhāvo machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Bhariyā dāsadāsi ca hatthassarathapattikā 
 Itthi patibbatā ceva paribhogāni sabbadā 
  
      Vijjā mantapade ceva vividhe āgame bahu 
 Sabbaṃ sippaṃ nisāmemi paribhogāni sabbadā 
  
      Thālake sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Soṇṇamaye maṇimaye athopi phalikāmaye 
 Lohitaṅkamaye ceva labhāmi thālake ahaṃ 
  
      Assatthake   phalamaye atho pokkharapattake 
 Madhupānakasaṃkhe ca labhāmi thalake ahaṃ 
  
      Vatte guṇe paṭipatti ācārakiriyāsu ca 
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Bhesajjaṃ sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Dasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Āyuvā balavā viro vaṇṇavā yasavā sukhi 
 Anupaddavo aniti ca homi cāpacito   sadā 
 Na me piyaciyogatthi tassa nissandato mama 
  
      Upāhane jine datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ sivikā sandamānikā 
 Saṭṭhisatasahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Maṇimāyā kambalikā   soṇṇarajatapādukā 
 Nimbatatanti paduddhāre bhave saṃsarato mama 
  
                   
  
      Niyāmaṃ patidhāvanti āguācārasodhanaṃ  
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Pāduke sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Iddhāpādukamāruyha viharāmi yadicchakaṃ 
  
      Udapuñchanake coḷe   datvā buddhe gaṇuttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo virajo sappabhāso patāpavā 
 Siniddhaṃ hoti me gattaṃ rajojallaṃ na limpati 
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
   Asatthake machasaṃ assaṭṭhake syā   Apacito machasaṃ   Kambamayā machasaṃ   
 Niyamaṃ paṭidhāvanti ācāraguṇasodhanaṃ simu   Udakapuñachanacoḷe machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Katatradaṇḍe sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Chānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Puttā mayhaṃ bahu honti taso mayhaṃ na vijjati 
 Appasayho sadā homi sabbārakkhehi rakkhito 
 Khalitampi   na jānāmi abhattaṃ mānasaṃ mama 
  
      Osadhaṃ añajanaṃ datvā buddhe saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Aṭṭānisese anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Visālanayato homi setapito ca lohito  
 Anāvilapasannakkho sabbarogavivajjito 
  
      Labhāmi dibbanayanaṃ paññācakkhuṃ anuttaraṃ 
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
      Kuñcike sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Dhammadvāravicaraṇaṃ labhāmi ñāṇakuñcikaṃ 
  
      Kuñcikānaṃ ghare datvā buddhe saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Dvānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
 Appakodho anāyaso saṃsaranto bhave ahaṃ 
  
      Āyoge sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Samādhisu na kampāmi vasi homi samādhisu 
 Abhejjapariso homi ādeyyavacano sadā 
 Jāyati bhogasampatti bhāve saṃsarato mama 
  
      Dhumatette jine datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
                   
  
      Sati me ujukā hoti susambandhā nahāravo  
 Labhāmi dibbanayanaṃ   tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Dipaṭṭhāne   jāne datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Tiṇānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Jātimā aṅgasampanno paññavā buddhisammato   
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe tassa nissandato ahaṃ 
  
      Tumbake ca karaṇḍe ca datvā buddhe gaṇutatame 
 Dasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sadā gutto   sukhasamaṅgi mahāyasavā tathā gatī 
 Vipattivigato   sudhumālo sabbitiparivajjito 
  
   Khalitaṃ maṃ simu   Setapitasalohito simu   Nahāravo machasaṃ   Dibbasayanaṃ syā 
   Dipadhāre machasaṃ   Buddhasammato machasaṃ   Suputto machasaṃ   
 Vibhattigatto syā 
  
                   
  
      Vipule ca guṇe lābhi samāvacaraṇaṃ   mama 
 Sucivajjitaubbego tumbake ca karaṇḍake 
  
      Labhāmi caturo vaṇṇe hatthassaratanāni ca   
 Tāni me na vinassanti tumbadāne idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Añajalinnāḷiyo   datvā buddhe saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sabbalakkhaṇasampanno āyupaññāsamāhito 
 Sabbāyāsavinimmutto kāyo me hoti sabbadā 
  
      Tanudhāre sunisite saṅghe datvāna pipphile 
 Kilesakantanaṃ ñāṇaṃ labhāmi atulaṃ suciṃ 
  
      Saṇḍase sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Kileseluñcanaṃ   ñāṇaṃ labhāmi atulaṃ suciṃ 
  
      Natthuke sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Saddhaṃ sīlaṃ hiriñcāpi atho ottappiyaṃ guṇaṃ 
 Sutaṃ cāgañca khatti ca paññaṃ me aṭṭhamaṃ guṇaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Piṭhake sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Ucce kule pajāyāmi mahābhogo bhavāmahaṃ 
 Sabbe maṃ apacāyanti kitti abbhuggatā mama 
  
      Kappasatasahassāni pallaṅkā caturassakā 
 Paricārenti maṃ niccaṃ saṃvibhāgarato ahaṃ 
  
      Bhisiyo sugate datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Chānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Samagatto apacito   muduko cārudassano 
 Labhami ñāṇaparivāraṃ bhisidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tulikā vikatikāyo kaṭṭissā cittakā bahu 
 Varapotthake kambale ca labhāmi vividhe ahaṃ 
  
      Pāvāriko ca muduke mudukājānaveṇiyo 
 Labhāmi vividhatthare bhisidānassadaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Samāvacalanā machasaṃ   Hatthissaratanāni ca machasaṃ   Malaharaṇiyo machasaṃ 
 hatthalilaṅgake syā       Kilesahañajanaṃ machasaṃ   Samasugattopacito machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattosmi viññutaṃ 
 Atuccho jhānamañcomhi bhisidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Bimbohane jine datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Chānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Uṇṇike padumake ca atho lohitavandane 
 Bimbohane upadhemi   uttamaṅgaṃ sadā mama 
  
      Aṭṭaṅgike maggavare sāmaññe caturo phale 
 Tesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā   vihare sabbakālikaṃ 
  
      Dāne dame sañcame ca appamaññāsu rūpisu 
 Tesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā   vihare sabbakālikaṃ 
      Vatte guṇe paṭipatatiācārakiriyāsu ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ upadahitvāna vihare sabbadā ahaṃ 
  
      Caṅkame vā padhāne vā viriyebodhipakkhiye 
 Tesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā viharāmi yathicchakaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Sīlaṃ samādhi paññā ca vimutati ca anuttarā 
 Tesu ñāṇaṃ upanetvā viharāmi sukhaṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Phaḷapiṭhe   jāne datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Dvānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Soṇṇamaye maṇimaye dantasāramaye bahu 
 Pallaṅkaseṭṭhe vindāmi phalapiṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pādapiṭhe jāne datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Dvānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Labhāmi bahuke yāne pādapiṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
 Dāsidāsā ca bhariyā ye caññe anujivino 
 Smā paricarante maṃ pādapioṭassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Telānabbhañajane   datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcanisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Avyādhitā rūpavatā khippaṃ dhammanisantitā 
 Lābhitā annapānassa āyupañcamakaṃ mama 
      Sappitelañca datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
   Bimbohane upādhemi machasaṃ   Tesu ñāṇaṃ uppādetvā machasaṃ   Uppādetvā 
 machasaṃ   Palālapiṭhe sīmu   Telaabbhañajane machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Thamavā rūpasampanenā pahaṭṭhatanujo sadā 
 Avyādhi visado homi sappitelassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Mukhasodhanakaṃ datvā saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Pañcānisase anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Visuddhakaṇṭho madhurasaro kāsasāsavivajjito 
 Uppalagandho mukhato upavāyati me sadā 
  
      Dadhiṃ datvāna sampannaṃ buddhe saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Bhuñajāmi amataṃ cittaṃ   varaṃ kāyagatāsatiṃ 
  
      Vaṇṇagandhasopetaṃ madhuṃ datvā jine gaṇe 
 Anupamaṃ atuliyaṃ pive muttirasaṃ ahaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Yathābhūtaṃ rasaṃ datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Caturo phale anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Annaṃ pānañca datvā buddhe saṅghe gaṇuttame 
 Dasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Āyumā balavā dhīro maṇṇavā yasavā sukhi 
 Lābhi antassa pānassa suro paññāṇavā sadā 
 Ime guṇe paṭilabhe saṃsaranto bhave ahaṃ 
  
      Dhupaṃ datvā sugate saṅghe gaṇavaruttame 
 Dasānisaṃse anubhomi kammānucchavike mama 
  
      Sugandhadeho yasavā sighapañño ca kittimā 
 Tikkhapañño bhuripañño hāsagambhirapaññavā 
  
      Vepullajavanapañño saṃsaranto bhavābhave 
 Tasseva vāhasādāni patto santisukhaṃ sivaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piḷindivaccho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Piḷindivacchattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Bhattaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Selattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā vithisāmi ahosahaṃ 
 Mamaṃ   ñāti samānetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Buddho loke samuppanno puññakkhettamanuttaraṃ  
 Āsi so   sabbalokassa āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
  
      Khattiyā negamā ceva mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
                   
  
      Uggā ca rājaputtā ca cesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Āḷārikā kappakā ca   nhāpakā mālakārakā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Rajakā pesakārā ca cammakārā ca nhāpikā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Usukārā bhamakārā cammikā ceva   tacchakā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Kammārā soṇṇakārā ca tipulohakarā tathā 
 Pasannacittā sumanā pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Bhatakā ceṭakā ceva dāsakammakarā bahu 
 Yathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Udahāra kaṭṭhahārā kassakā tiṇahārakā 
 Yathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Pupphikā mālikā ceva paṇṇikā phalahārakā 
 Yathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Gaṇikā kumbhadāsī ca puvikā macchikāpi ca 
 Yathāsakena thāmena pugadhammaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Etha sabbe samāgantvā gaṇaṃ bandhama ekato 
 Adhikāraṃ karissāma puññakkhette anuttare 
  
   Mama machasaṃ   Puññakkhetto anuttaro machasaṃ   Āsisaso simu ādhāro       
 Āḷārakā ca suda syā   Cammakārā ca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Te me sutvāna vacanaṃ gaṇaṃ bandhiṃsu tāvade 
 Upaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ bhikkhusaṅghassa kārayuṃ 
  
      Niṭṭhāpetvāna taṃ sālaṃ udaggo tuṭṭhamānaso 
 Pareto tehi sabbehi sambuddheṃ upasaṅkamiṃ 
  
      Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ lokanāthaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Canditvā satthuno pāde idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Ime tīṇi satā vīra purisā ekato gaṇā 
 Upaṭṭhānasālaṃ sukataṃ niyyātenti   tavaṃ   muni 
  
      Bhikkhusaṅghassa purato sampaṭicchitva cakkhumā 
 Tiṇṇaṃ satānaṃ purato imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Tisataṃ pi ca jeṭṭho ca anuvattiṃsu ekato 
 Sampattiṃ hi   karitvāna sabbe anubhavissatha 
  
                   
  
      Pacchimabhave   sampatte sitibhāvamanuttaraṃ 
 Ajaraṃ amataṃ santaṃ nibbāṇaṃ phassayissatha  
  
      Evaṃ buddho viyākāsi sabbaññu samaṇuttaro 
 Buddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā somanassaṃ pavedayiṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ 
 Devādhipo pañcasataṃ devarajjamakārayiṃ 
  
      Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakakvati ahosabhaṃ 
 Devarajjaṃ karontassa mahādevā avandiṃsu 
  
      Idha mānuseka rajje   parisā honti bandhavā 
 Pacchimabhatva sampatte vāseṭṭho nāma brāhmaṇo 
  
      Asitikoṭinicayo tassa putto ahosahaṃ 
 Selo itimamaṃ nāmaṃ chaḷaṅge pāramiṅgato 
  
      Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ sasissehi purakkheto 
 Jaṭākhārikabharitaṃ keṇiyaṃ nāma tāpasaṃ 
  
      Paṭiyattāhutiṃ disvā idaṃ vacanamabuviṃ 
 Āvaho vā vicāho cā rājā vā te nimantito 
  
      Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ brāhmaṇe devasammate 
 Na nimantemi rājānaṃ āhuti me na vijjati 
  
   Niyyādenti machasaṃ   Tuvaṃ machasaṃ   Samāpatti hi syā   Pacchime bhave 
 machasaṃ   Rajjaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Na vatthi mayhaṃ āvaho vivābho me na vijjati 
 Sakyānaṃ nandijanano seṭṭho loke sadevake 
  
      Sabbalokahitatthāya sabbasattasukhāvaho 
 So me nimantito ajja tassetaṃ paṭiyādataṃ 
  
      Timbarūsakavaṇṇabho appameyyo anupamo 
 Rūpenāsadiso buddho svātanāya nimantito 
  
      Ukkāmukhapahaṭṭhova khadiraṅgārasannibho 
 Vijjupamo mahāvīro so me buddho nimantito 
  
      Pabbatagge yathā acci puṇṇamāyeva candimā 
 Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāso so me buddho nimantito 
  
      Asambhito bhayānito bhavantakaraṇo muni 
 Sihupamo vahāviro so me buddho nimantito 
  
                   
      Kusalo buddhadhammehi appasayho parehi so 
 Nāgupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Anantavaṇṇo amitayaso vicittasabbalakkhaṇo 
 Sakkupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Vasi gaṇi patāpi ca tejassi ca durāsado 
 Brahmupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Pattadhammo dasabalo balātibalapāragu 
 Dharaṇupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Silavicisamākiṇṇo dhammaviññāṇakhohito 
 Uddhupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Durāsado duppasaho acalo uggato brahā 
 Nerūpamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Anantañāṇo asamasamo atulo aggataṃ gato 
 Gaganupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
   Paṇṇarasamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Patiṭṭhā bhayabhitānaṃ tāṇo saraṇagāminaṃ 
 Assāsako mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Āsayo buddhimantānaṃ puññakkhettaṃ sukhesitaṃ 
 Ratanākaro mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Assāsako vedakaro sāmaññaphaladāyako 
 Meghupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Lokacakkhu mahātejo sabbatamavinodano 
 Suriyupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Ārammaṇavimuttīsu sabhāvadassano muni 
 Candupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Vuddho   samussito loke lakkhaṇehi alaṅkato 
 Appameyyo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Yassa ñāṇaṃ appameyyaṃ sīlaṃ yassa anupamaṃ 
 Vimutti asadisā yassa so me buddho nimattito 
  
      Yassa dhiti asadisā thamo yassa acintiyo 
 Yassa parakkamo jeṭṭho so me buddho nimattito 
  
      Rāgo doso ca moho ca visā sabbe samuhatā 
 Agadupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
                   
  
      Kilesavyādhi   bahudukkhasabbatamacinodano  
 Vejjupamo mahāvīro so me buddho tivantito 
  
      Buddhoti bho yaṃ vadesi ghosopeso sudullabho 
 Buddho buddhoti sutvāna piti me upapajjatha 
  
      Abbhantaramagaṇhanti piti me bahi nicchare 
 Sohaṃ pitimano santo idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
       Kahaṃ nu kho so bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Tattha gantvā namassassaṃ sāmaññaphaladāyakaṃ  
  
      Paggayha dakkhiṇaṃ bāhuṃ vedajāto katañajali 
 Ācikkhi me dhammarājaṃ sokapallavinodanaṃ 
  
   Buddho machasaṃ   Kelasavyādhi machasaṃ   Sabbatamacinodako simu 
  
                   
  
       Udentaṃva mahāmeghaṃ nīlaṃ añajanasannibhaṃ 
 Sāgaraṃ viya dissantaṃ passasetaṃ mahāvanaṃ 
  
      Ettha so vasate buddho adantadamako muni 
 Vinayanto ca veneyye bodhento bodhipakkhiye 
  
      Pipāsitova udakaṃ bhojanaṃva jighacchito 
 Gāmi yathā vacchagiddhā evāhaṃ viciniṃ jinaṃ 
  
      Ācāraupacāraññu dhammānucchavisaṃvaraṃ   
 Sikkhāpesiṃ sake sisse gacchante jinassantikaṃ 
  
      Durāsadā bhagavanto sihāva ekacārino 
 Pade padaṃ nikkipantā āgacechayyātha māṇavā 
  
      Āsiviso yathā ghoro migarājāva kesari 
 Mattocava kuñajaro danti evaṃ buddhā durāsadā 
  
      Ukkāsitañca khipitaṃ ajjhupekkhiya māṇavā 
 Pade padaṃ nikkhipantā upetha buddhasantikaṃ 
  
      Paṭisallānagarukā appasadā durāsadā 
 Durūpasaṅkamā buddhā garū honti sadevake 
  
      Yadāhaṃ pañhaṃ pucchāmi gaṭisammodayāmi vā 
 Appasaddā tadā hotha munibhūtāva tiṭṭhatha 
  
                   
  
      Yaṃ so deseti saddhammaṃ   khemaṃ nibbaṇapattiyā 
 Tamevatthaṃ nisāvetha saddhammasavaṇaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
      Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ sammodiṃ muninā ahaṃ 
 Taṃ kathaṃ vitasāretvā lakkhaṇe upadhārayiṃ 
      Lakkhaṇe dveva   kaṅkhāmi passāmi tiṃsalakkhaṇe 
 Kosobhitavatthaguyhaṃ iddhiyā dassayi muni 
  
      Jivhaṃ ninnāmayitvāna kaṇṇasote ca nāsike 
 Paṭimasi nalāṭantaṃ kevalaṃ chādayi jano
