   Dhammānucchavasaṃvareṃ simu   Sambuddho machasaṃ   Dve ca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tassāhaṃ lakkhaṇe disvā paripuṇṇe savyañajane 
 Buddhoti niṭṭhaṃ gantvāna saha sissehi pabbajiṃ 
  
      Satehi tihi sahito pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Addhamāse asampatte sabbe pattāmha nibbutiṃ 
  
      Ekato kammaṃ katvāna puññakkhette anuttare 
 Ekato saṃsaritvāna ekato vinivattayuṃ 
  
      Gopānasiyo davona pugadhamme vasī   ahaṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena aṭṭahetu labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Disāsu pujito homi bhogā ca amitā mama 
 Patiṭṭhā homi sabbesaṃ tāso mama na vijjati 
  
      Vyādhayo me na vijjanti dighāyuṃ pālayāmi ca 
 Sukhumacchaviko homi āvāse patthite   vase 
  
      Aṭṭha gopānasi datvā pugadhamme vasi ahaṃ 
 Paṭisambhidāehattañca etaṃ me aparaṭṭhamaṃ 
  
      Sabbavositavosāno katakicco anāsavo 
 Aṭṭhagopānasi nāma tava putto mahāmuni 
  
      Pañcathambhāni datvāna pugadhamme vasi ahaṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena pañcahetu labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Acalo homi mettāya anunaṅgo bhavāmahaṃ 
 Ādeyyavacano homi na dhaṃsemi yathā ahaṃ 
  
      Abhantaṃ hoti me cittaṃ acalo homi kassaci 
 Tena kammena sukatena vimalo homi sāsane 
  
                   
  
      Sagāravo sappatisso katakicco anāsavo 
 Sāvako te mahāvīra bhikkhu taṃ vandate muni 
  
      Katvā sukatapallaṅkaṃ sālāyaṃ paññapesahaṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena pañca hetu labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Ucce kule pajāyitvā mahābhogo bhavāmahaṃ 
 Sabbasampattiko homi maccheraṃ me na vijjati 
      Gamane patthite mayhaṃ pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati 
 Saha pallaṅkaseṭṭhena gacchāmi mama patthitaṃ 
  
   Casiṃ machasaṃ   Āvāse patte vase syā 
  
                   
  
      Tena pallaṅkadānena tamaṃ sabbaṃ vinodayiṃ 
 Sabbābhiññābalappatto thero candati taṃ muni 
  
      Parakiccattakiccāni sabbakiccāni sādhayiṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ 
  
      Pariniṭṭhitasālaṃ hi paribhogamadāsahaṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena seṭṭattaṃ ajjhupāgeto 
  
      Ye keci damakā loke hatthi asse damenti ye 
 Karitvā kāraṇā nānā dāruṇena dāmanti te 
  
      Nahevaṃ tvaṃ mahāvīra damesi naranāriyo 
 Adaṇḍena asatthena damesi uttame dame 
  
      Dānassa vaṇṇe kittento desanākusalo muni 
 Ekaṃ pañahaṃ   kathentova bodhesi tisate muni 
  
      Dantā mayaṃ sārathinā suvimuttā anāsavā 
 Sabbābhiññābalappattā nibbutā upadhikkhāye 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Atikkantā bhayā sabbe sālādānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā selo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Selattherassapadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Ekapañahaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Sabbakittikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Kaṇikāraṃva jotantaṃ   diparukkhaṃva ujjalaṃ  
 Osadhiṃva virovantaṃ vijjutaṃ gagane yathā 
  
      Asambhitaṃ anutrāsiṃ   migarājaṃva kesariṃ 
 Ñāṇālokaṃ pakāsentaṃ maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇo 
  
      Uddharantaṃ imaṃ lokaṃ chindantaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ 
 Gajjantaṃ   migarājaṃva addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Jaṭājinadhāro āsiṃ bahā uju patāpavā 
 Vākaviraṃ gahetvāna pādamule avatthariṃ 
  
      Kāḷānusāriyaṃ gayha anulimpiṃ tathāgataṃ 
 Sambuddhamanulimpetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ oghatiṇṇa  mahāmuni 
 Ñāṇālokena jotesi nāvaṭaṃ   ñāṇamuttamaṃ 
  
      Dhammacakkaṃ pavattesi maddase paratitthiye 
 Usabho jitasaṅgāmo sampakampesi medini 
  
      Mahāsamuddo ūmiyo velantambhi pabhijjare 
 Tatheva tava ñāṇamhi sabbadiṭṭhi pabhijjare 
  
      Sukhumacchikajālena sarambhi sampatānite 
 Antojālagatā pāṇā pilitā honti tāvade 
  
      Tatheva titthiyā loke puthupāsaṇḍanissitā 
 Antoñāṇavare tuyhaṃ parivattanti mārisa 
  
      Patiṭṭhā vuyhataṃ oghe tvaṃ hi nātho abandhunaṃ 
 Bhayaṭṭitānaṃ saraṇaṃ muttatthinaṃ   parāyaṇaṃ 
  
      Ekaviro asadiso karuṇāmettasañcayo  
 Susilo asamo   santo vasi tādi jitañajaso 
  
                   
  
      Dhīro vigatasammoho anojo akathaṅkathi 
 Vusito    vantadososi nimmalo payato    suci 
  
   Jalitaṃ machasaṃ   Jotitaṃ syā   Anuttāsiṃ machasaṃ   Asambhitaṃ syā   Oghatiṇṇo 
 syā   Pavaraṃ syā vajira       Muttatthinaṃ machasaṃ  Mettākaruṇā sañcayo 
 machasaṃ saññuto syā   Asamo susamo satto machasaṃ    Tusito machasaṃ    Saṃyato 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Saṅgātigo hatamādā   tevijjo tibhavattago 
 Simātigo dhammagaru katattho hitavappatho   
  
      Tārako tvaṃ yathā nāvā nidhivassāsakārako 
 Asambhito yathā siho gajarājāva dassito 
  
      Thometvā dasagāthāhi padumuttaraṃ mihāyasaṃ 
 Vanditvā satthuno pāde tuṇhi aṭṭhāsahaṃ tadā 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me silañca ñāṇañca dhammañcāpi pakittayi  
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Saṭṭhikappasahassāni devaloke ramissati aññe deve abhihotvā   issaraṃ kārayissati 
  
      So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati 
  
      Pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vicajjiya 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo   
  
      Yathāpi megho thanayaṃ tappeti mediniṃ imaṃ 
 Tatheva tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammena tapapayi mamaṃ 
  
      Sīlaṃ paññaca dhammañca thavitthā lokanāyakaṃ 
 Patombhi paramaṃ santiṃ nibbāṇaṃ padamaccutaṃ 
  
      Aho nūna sa bhagavā ciraṃ tiṭṭheyya cakkhumā 
 Aññatañca vijaneyyuṃ phuseyyuṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Ayaṃ me paccimā jāti bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ buddhamabhithomayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Gatamado syā   Gatatthohitavabbhuto machasaṃ   Saddhammañcāpi vaṇṇayi 
 machasaṃ   Aññe devebhibhavitvā machasaṃ   Nibbāyissatināsavo machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbakittiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sabbakittikattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Madhudāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sindhuyā nadiyā tīre sukato assamo mama 
 Tattha vācemahaṃ sisse itihāsaṃ salakkhaṇaṃ 
  
      Dhammakāmā vinitā te sotukāmā susāsanaṃ 
 Chaḷaṅge pāramippattā sindhukule vasatti te 
  
      Upapātagamane ceva lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā 
 Uttamatthaṃ gavesantā vasati pavane   tadā 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho loka uppajji tāvado 
 Ambhākaṃ anukampanto upagacchi vināyako 
  
      Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Tiṇasatthārakaṃ kavo lokajeṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Pavanāto   madhuṃ gayha buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
 Sambuddho pibhuñajitvā idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
       Yo taṃ adāsi madhuṃ me pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
 Tamahaṃ kittasissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Iminā dhudānena tiṇasatthārakena ca 
 Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahasasamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Vipine machasaṃ   Vipanāto machasaṃ   Gottena machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Devalokā idhāgantvā mātukucchiṃ upāgate 
 Madhuvassaṃ pavassittha chādayaṃ madhunā mahiṃ  
  
      Mayi nikkhantamattambhi kucchiyā ca suduttaraṃ 
 Tatrāpi madhuvassaṃ me vassate niccakālikaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Lābhi annassa pānasa madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sabbakāmasamiddhohaṃ bhavitvā devamānuse 
 Teneva madhudānena pattombhi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Vuṭṭhambhi deve caturaṅgule tiṇe 
 Sampupphite   dharaṇiruhe sañachanne  
 Suññe ghare maṇḍaparukkhamule  
 Vasāmi niccaṃ sukhito anāsavo 
  
      Majjhe mahante hine ca   bhave sabbe atikkamiṃ  
 Ajja me āsavā khiṇā nathidoni punabbhavo 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi madhudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā madhudāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Madhudāyakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Supupphite syā   Cappadese syā   Maṇḍaparukkhamulake machasaṃ   Majjhe 
 mayahaṃ bhavā assu syā       Ye bhave samatikkamiṃ syā     
  
                   
  
     Padumakuṭāgāriyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Piyadassi nāma bhagavā sayambhu lokāyako 
 Vivekakāmo sambuddho samādhikusalo muni 
  
      Vanasaṇḍaṃ samogayha piyadassi mahāmuni 
 Paṃsukulaṃ pattharitvā nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Migaluddo pure āsiṃ vipite   kānane ahaṃ 
 Pasadaṃ migamesante ābhiṇḍami ahaṃ tadā 
  
      Tatthadadasāsiṃ sambuddheṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
 Pupphitaṃ sālarājāṃva sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ 
  
      Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Jātassaraṃ samogayha padumaṃ āhariṃ tadā 
  
      Āharitvāna padumaṃ satapattaṃ manoramaṃ 
 Kuṭāgāraṃ karitvāna chādayiṃ padumenahaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko piyadassi mahāmuni 
 Sattarattindivaṃ buddho kuṭāgāre vasi jino 
  
      Purāṇaṃ chaḍḍhayitvāna navena chādayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna aṭṭhāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ 
  
      Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā piyadassi mahāmuni 
 Disā anucilokanto nisīdi lokanāyako 
  
      Tadā sudassano nāma upaṭṭhāko mahiddhiko 
 Cittamaññāya buddhassa piyadassassa satthuno 
  
      Asitāya sahassehi bhikkhuhi parivārito 
 Vanante sukhamāsinaṃ upesi lokenāyakaṃ 
  
      Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi adhivatthā ca devatā 
 Buddhassa cittamaññāya sabbe santipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Samāgatesu yakkhesu kumbhaṇḍe saha rakkhase 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe ca sampatte gāthāmā vyāhari   jiko 
  
       Yo maṃ sattāhaṃ pujeyi āvāsañca akāsi me 
 Tamahaṃ kintiyissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
   Araññe machasaṃ   Gāthā pabyāhari machasaṃ gāthā sabyāhari syā 
  
                   
  
      Sududadasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ gambhiraṃ suppakāsitaṃ 
 Ñāṇena kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Catuddasāni kappāni devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Kuṭāgāraṃ brahaṃ tassa   padumapupphehi   chāditaṃ 
 Ākāse dhārayissati pupphakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catubbise kappasate vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsarissati 
 Tattha pupphamayaṃ vyamahaṃ ākāse dhārayissati 
  
      Yathā padumapattambhi toyaṃ na upalimpati 
 Tathevimassa cañāṇamhi kilesā nopalimpare 
  
      Manasā vinivaṭṭhetvā pañcanivaraṇe ayaṃ 
 Cittaṃ janetvā nekkhamme agārā pabbajissati 
 Tato pupphamaye vyambhe dhārente nikkhamissati 
  
      Rukkhamule vasantassa nipakassa satimato 
 Tattha pupphamayaṃ vyamhaṃ   matthake dhārayissati 
  
      Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Datvāna bhikkhusaṅghassa nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Kūṭāgārena caratā   pabbajjaṃ abhinikkhamiṃ 
 Rukkhamule vasantamhi   kūṭāgāraṃ dhariyati 
  
                   
  
      Cīvare piṇḍapāte ca cetanā me na vijjati 
 Puññakammena saṃyutto labhāmi pariniṭṭhataṃ 
  
      Gaṇanāto asaṃkheyyā kappakoṭi bahu mama 
 Rittakā te atikkantā pamutatā lokanāyakā 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate piyadasasi vināyako 
 Tamahaṃ payirupāsitvā imaṃ yoniṃ upāgato 
  
      Idhaddasāsiṃ sambudadhaṃ   anomaṃ nāma cakkhumaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ upagantvāna pabbajaṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Dukkhassantakaro buddho maggaṃ me adesasi jino 
 Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pattomahi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Tosayitvāna sambudadhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anasāvo 
  
   Mahantassa machasaṃ   Padamapupphehi machasaṃ   Pupphamayaṃ vyambhaṃ 
 dhārentaṃ machasaṃ   Caraṇā simu     caete syā   Casantampi machasaṃ   Idha 
 passāmi machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ buddamabhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapujāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumakuṭāgāriyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Padumakuṭāgāriyattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
     Bakkulattherāpadānaṃ   
  
      Hivamantassa avidūre sobhito nāma pabbato 
 Assamo sukato mayhaṃ sakasissehi māpito 
  
      Maṇḍapā ca bahu tattha pupphitā sinduvārakā 
 Kapitthā ca bahu tattha pupphitā jivajivakā  
      Nigguṇḍiyo bahu tattha badarāmalakāni ca 
 Phārusakā alābu ca puṇḍarikā ca pupphitā 
  
      Ālakā   beluvā tattha kadali mātuluṅgakā 
 Mahānāmā bahu tattha ajjuṇā ca piyaṅgukā 
  
                   
  
      Kosambā salalā nipā nigrodhā ca kapitthanā 
 Ediso assamo mayhaṃ sasissohaṃ tahiṃ vasiṃ 
  
      Anomadassi bhagavā sayambhu lokanāyako 
 Gavesaṃ paṭisallānaṃ mamassamamupāgami 
  
      Upetamhi mahāvire anomadassimahāyase 
 Khaṇena lokanāthassa vātābādo samuṭṭhahi 
  
      Vicaratto araññamhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ cakkhumantaṃ mahāyasaṃ 
  
      Iriyañcāpi disvāna upalakkhesahaṃ tadā 
 Asaṃsayaṃ hi buddhassa vyādhi no upapajjatha   
  
   Campakā nāma ketakā syā   Āḷakā machasaṃ aḷakkā syā   Udapajjatha machasaṃ 
  bākulattherāpadāna machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Khippaṃ assamamāgacchiṃ mama sissāna santike 
 Bhesajjaṃ kattukāmohaṃ sisse āmantayiṃ tadā 
  
      Paṭissuṇitvā me vākyaṃ sissā sabbe sagāravā 
 Ekajjhaṃ sannipatiṃsu satthugāravatā mama 
  
      Kippaṃ pabbatamāruyha sabbosadhamahāsahaṃ 
 Pāniyayogaṃ katvāna   buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Paribhutte mahāvire sabbaññulokanāyake 
 Khippaṃ vāto vupasami sugatassasa mahesino 
  
      Passaddhaṃ darathaṃ disvā anomadassi mahāyaso 
 Sakāsane nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me pādāsi bhesajajaṃ vyādhiñca samayi mama 
 Tamahaṃ kittayisasāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Kappasatasahassani devaloke ramissati 
 Vādite turiye tattha modissati sadā ayaṃ 
  
      Manussalokamāgantvā sukkamūlena codito 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Pañcapaññāsakappamhi anomo nāma khattiyo 
 Caturanto vijitivi jambumaṇḍassa   issaro 
  
      Sattaratanampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
 Tāvatiṃsepi khebhetvā issaraṃ kārayissati 
  
                   
  
      Devabhuto manusso vā appabādho bhavissati 
 Pariggahaṃ vivajjetvā vyādhiṃ loke tarissati 
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena   satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
      Kilese jhāpayitvāna taṇhāsotaṃ tarissati 
 Bakakulo   nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Idaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati  
  
   Pāniyayoggaṃ katvā simu   Jambudipassa syā   Gottena machasaṃ   Bākulo 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Anomadassi bhagavā sayambhu lokanāyako 
 Vivekānuvilokanto mamassamamupāgami 
  
      Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sabbaññuṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Sabbosadhena tappesiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
      Tassa me sukataṃ sukhette bijasampadā 
 Khepetuṃ neva sakkomi tadā hi sukataṃ mama 
  
      Lābhā mama suladdhaṃ me yohaṃ adadakkhi nāyakaṃ 
 Tena kammāvasesena pattombhi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Sabbametaṃ abhiññāya gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bakakulo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bakakulattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Girimānandattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Bhariyā me kālakatā putto sivathikaṃ gato 
 Mātā pitā ca bhāta ca ekacitakamhi ḍayhare 
  
      Tena sokena santatto kiso paṇḍu ahosahaṃ 
 Cittakkhepo ca me āsi tena sokena aṭṭito 
  
                   
  
      Sokapallaparetohaṃ vanantamupasaṅkamiṃ 
 Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā rukkhamule vasāmahaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho dukkhassantakāro jino 
 Mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santike 
  
                   
  
      Padasaddaṃ suṇitvāna sumedhassa mahesino 
 Paggahetvānahaṃ sisiṃ ullokesiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
  
      Upagacchi mahāvīro   piti me upapajjatha 
 Tadāsi mekaggamano disvāna taṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Satiṃ paṭilabhitvāna paṇṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ 
 Nisīdi bhagavā tattha anukampāya cakkhumaṃ 
  
      Nisajja tattha bhagavā sumedho lokanāyako 
 Dhammaṃ me kathayi buddho sokasallavinodanaṃ 
  
       Anavahitā tato āguṃ ananuññātā ito gatā 
 Yathāgatā tathā gatā tattha kā paridevanā 
  
      Yathāpi pathikā sattā vassamānāya vuṭṭhiyā 
 Sabhaṇḍā upagacchanti vassassāpatanāya te 
  
      Vasse ca te oramite sampayanti yadicchakaṃ 
 Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ kattha kā paridevatā 
  
      Āgantukā pāhuṇakā caliteritakampitā 
 Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ tattha kā paridevatā 
  
      Yathāpi urago jiṇṇaṃ hitvā gacchati santacaṃ 
 Evaṃ mātā pitā tuyhaṃ santuṃ idha hīyare  
  
      Buddhassa giramaññāya sokalassaṃ vivajjayiṃ 
 Pāmojjaṃ janayitvāna buddhaseṭṭhamavandihaṃ  
  
      Vanditvāna mahānāgaṃ girimañajarimapujayiṃ  
 Dibbagandhena sampannaṃ   sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Pujayitvāna sambuddhaṃ sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Anussaraṃ guṇaggāni santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Nittiṇṇosi   mahāvīra sabbaññu lokanāyaka 
 Sabbe satte uddharasi ñāṇena tvaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Vimatiṃ dveḷahakaṃ cāpi sañachindasi mahāmuni 
 Paṭipadesi me maggaṃ tava ñāṇena cakkhuma 
      Arahā siddhipattā ca   chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā 
 Antalikkhacarā dhīrā parivārenti tāvade 
  
   Upāgate mahāvire machasaṃ   Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ machasaṃ   Pujayiṃ 
 girimañajariṃ machasaṃ   Dibbagandhaṃ sampavattaṃ machasaṃ   Tittaṇehāsi katthavi 
   Vasippantā ca machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Paṭipannā ca sekhā ca phalaṭṭhā santi sāvakā 
 Surodayeva padumā pupphanti tava sāvakā 
  
      Yathā samuddo akkhobho   atulo ca duruttaro  
 Evaṃ ñaṇena sampanno appameyyosi cakkhuma 
  
      Canditvāhaṃ lokajinaṃ cakkhamantaṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Puthu disā namassanto paṭikuṭiko agacachahaṃ 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna sampajāno patissato 
 Okkamiṃ mātuyā kucchiṃ sandhāvanto bhavābhave 
  
      Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Ātāpi nipako jhāyī paṭisallānagocaro 
  
      Padhānaṃ padahitvāna tosayitvā mahāmuniṃ 
 Candovabbhaghanā mutto vicarāmi ahaṃ tadā 
  
      Vivekamanuyuttombhi upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassambhi yaṃ buddhamabhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā girimānando thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Girimānandattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Mahāsamuddocakkhobho machasaṃ   Atulopi duruttaro machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
     Salalamaṇḍapiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute kakusandhambhi brāhmaṇambhi vusimati 
 Gahetvā salalaṃ mālaṃ maṇḍapaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Tāvatiṃsagato santo labhāmi vyambhamuttamaṃ 
 Aññe devetirocāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ caṅkamanto ṭhito cahaṃ 
 Channo salalapupphehi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Imasmiṃ yeva kappambhi yaṃ buddhamabhipujayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā salalamaṇḍapiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Salalamaṇḍapiyattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
     Sabbadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Mahāsamuddaṃ ogayha bhavanaṃ me sunimmitaṃ 
 Sunimmitā pokkharaṇi cakkavākupakujitā   
  
      Mandālakehi sañachannā padumuppalakehi ca 
 Nadi ca sandate tattha supatitthā manoramā 
  
      Macchakacchapasañachannā nānādijasamotthatā 
 Mayurakoñcābhirudā kokilādihi vagguhi 
  
      Pārevatā ravihaṃsā cakkavākā nadicarā 
 Dindibhā sāḷikā cettha pampakā   jivajivakā 
  
      Haṃsā koñcābhinaditā   kosiyā piṅgalā bahu 
 Sattaratanasampannā maṇimuttikavālukā 
  
      Sabbasoṇṇamayā rukkhā nānagandhasameritā 
 Ujjotenti divārattiṃ bhavanaṃ sabbakālikaṃ 
  
   Cakkavākapakujitā machasaṃ   Pammakā machasaṃ   Koñcāpi naditā machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni sāyaṃ pāto pavajjare 
 Soḷasitthisahassāni parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Abhinikkhamma bhavanā sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano vandayiṃ taṃ mahāyasaṃ 
  
      Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā sasaṅghaṃ taṃ nimantayiṃ 
 Adhivāsesi so dhīro sumedho lokanāyako 
  
      Mama dhammakathaṃ katvā uyyojesi mahāmuni 
 Sambuddhaṃ abhivadetvā bhavanaṃ me upāgamiṃ 
  
      Āmantayiṃ parijanaṃ sabbe sannipatātha vo 
 Pubbanhasamayaṃ buddho bhavanaṃ āgamissati 
  
      Lābhā amhaṃ suladdhaṃ no ye vasāma tavantike 
 Mayampi buddhaseṭṭhassa pujaṃ kassāma satthuno 
  
      Annaṃ pānaṃ paṭṭhapetvā kālamārocayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Vasisatasahassehi upesi lokanāyako 
  
      Pañcaṅgikehi turiyehi paccuggamanamakāsahaṃ 
 Sabbasovaṇṇamaye piṭhe nasidi purisuttamo 
  
      Uparicchadanaṃ āsi sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ tadā 
 Vijaniyo pavāyanti bhikkhusaṅghassa antare 
  
      Pahutenannapānena bhikkhusaṃghamatappayiṃ 
 Paccekadussayugale bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo maṃ   annena pātena sabbe ime ca tappayi  
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Upagacchati   yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sabbadā sabbasovaṇṇaṃ chadanaṃ dhārayissati 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Me machasaṃ   Tappayiṃ machasaṃ   Upapajjati machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyisasatanāsavo   
  
      Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sihanādaṃ nadissati 
 Citake chattaṃ dhārenti heṭṭhāchattambhi ḍayhatha 
  
      Sāmaññaṃ me anuppattaṃ kilesā jhāpitā mayā  
 Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā santāpo me na vijjati 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassambhi yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sabbadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā vihārāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaṭṭhessa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sabbadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
     Ajitattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ajjhogahetvā   himavantaṃ nisīdi lokanāyako 
  
      Nāhaṃ addakkhiṃ sambuddhaṃ napi saddaṃ suṇomahaṃ 
 Mama bhakkhaṃ gavesanto ābhiṇḍāmi vane tadā 
  
      Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ khattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ  
 Disvāna cittamāpajjaṃ   satto ko nāmayaṃ bhave 
  
      Lakkhaṇāni viloketvā mama vijjaṃ anussariṃ 
 Sutaṃ hi metaṃ vuddhānaṃ paṇḍitānaṃ subhāsitaṃ 
  
      Tesaṃ yathā taṃ vacanaṃ ayaṃ buddho bhavissati 
 Yannunāhaṃ sakkareyyaṃ gatiṃ me sodhayissati 
  
      Khippaṃ assamamāgantvā madhutelaṃ gahiṃ ahaṃ 
 Koḷambakaṃ gahetvāna upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ  
  
      Tidaṇḍake gahetvāna upagacchiṃ abbhokāse ṭhapesahaṃ 
 Padīpaṃ pajjaletvāna   aṭṭhakkhattuṃ avandahaṃ 
  
   Nibbāyissatināsavo machasaṃ   Mama simu   Ajjhogāhetvā machasaṃ   
 Davattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ machasaṃ   Cittināpajjiṃ machasaṃ   Vināyakaṃ machasaṃ   
 Pajjalitvāna machasaṃ 
  
                   
                   
  
      Sattarattindivaṃ buddho nisīdi purisuttamo 
 Tato ratyā vivasāne vuṭṭhāsi lokanāyako 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano sattarattindivaṃ ahaṃ 
 Dipaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
      Sabbe vanā gandhamayā pabbate gandhamādane 
 Buddhassa anubhāvena   upagacchuṃ tadā jinaṃ  
  
      Ye keci pupphagandhāse pupphitā dharaṇiruhā 
 Buddhassa anubhāvena sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Yāvatā himavantambhi nāgā ca garuḷā ubho 
 Dhammañca sotukāmā te āgacchuṃ buddhasantikaṃ 
  
      Devalo nāma samaṇo buddhassa aggasavako 
 Vasisatasahassehi buddhasantikupāgami 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Yo me dipaṃ padipesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
 Tamahaṃ nittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Saṭṭhakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhatuṃ rājā cacakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Paṭhaviyaṃ satatasataṃ vipulaṃ rajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāte asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Iminā dipadānena dibbacakkhu bhavissati 
 Samantato aṭṭhakosaṃ   passissati ayaṃ sadā 
  
      Devalokā cavantassa nibbattantassa jantuno 
 Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ padipaṃ dhārayissati 
  
      Jāyamānassa sattassa   puññakammasamaṅgino 
 Yāvatā nagaraṃ hoti tāvatā jotayissati 
  
      Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Asseva dipadānassa aṭṭhadipaphalena hi 
 Na jayissantimaṃ   jantu dipadānassadaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Ānubhāvena sabbattha   Āgacchuṃ buddhasantikaṃ machasaṃ   Aḍḍhakosaṃ simu   
 Āsi machasaṃ   Upaṭṭhissanti maṃ jantuṃ syā 
  
                   
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Ajito nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako 
  
      Saṭṭhikappasahassāni devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ 
 Tatrāpi me dipasataṃ jotate sabbakālikaṃ 
  
      Devaloke manusse vā niddhāvanti pabhā mama 
 Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna bhiyo hāsaṃ janesahaṃ 
      Tusitāhaṃ cavitvāna okkamiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ 
 Jāyamānassa sattassa āloko vipulo ahu 
  
      Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Bācariṃ upasaṅkamma sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ 
  
      Himavante vasanenāhaṃ assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ 
  
      Danto buddho dametāvi oghatiṇṇo nirūpadhi 
 Nibbāṇaṃ kathayi buddho sabbadukkhappamocanaṃ 
  
      Taṃ me āgamanaṃ sidadhaṃ tosito hi mahāmuni  
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe   yaṃ dipamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dipadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ajito thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ajitattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
   Tositohaṃ mahāmuniṃ machasaṃ tositohaṃ mahāmuni simu   Satasahassito kappe 
 machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Piḷindivaccho so ca sabbakitti madhundado 
 Kūṭāgāri khakkulo cagiri salalasavhayo 
                   
 Sabbado ajito ceva gāthāyo gaṇitā iha 
 Satāni pañca gāthānaṃ visati ca taduttari 
  
 Piḷindivacchavaggo cattāḷisatimo 
  
 Athavagguddānaṃ 
 Padumārakkhado ceva ummā   gandhodakena ca 
 Ekapadama saddasaññi mandāraṃ bodhi vandako 
 Avaṇḍañca piḷindi ca gāthāyo gaṇitā pi ca  
 Catusattati gāthāyo ekādasa satāni ca 
  
 Padumavaggadasakaṃ 
  
 Catutthaṃ satakaṃ samattaṃ   
   Umā machasaṃ   Iha machasaṃ   Catutthasatakaṃ samattaṃ machasaṃ

 Suttantapiṭake khuddakanikāye 
  
 Apadānapāḷi 
  
 Dutiyo bhāgo 
  
 Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa 
  
      Pabbhārakūṭaṃ nissaya sobhito nāma tāpaso 
 Pavattaphalaṃ bhuñjitvā vasani pabbatantare 
  
      Aggiṃ dāruṃ āharitvā ujjālesiṃ ahaṃ tadā 
 Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto brahmalokūpapattiyā 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mamuddharitukāmo so āgacchi mama santike 
  
       Kiṃ karosi mahāpuñña dehi me aggidārukaṃ 
 Ahamaggiṃ parivare tato me suddhi hehiti    
  
       Subhaddako tvaṃ manuje devate tvaṃ pajānasi 
 Tuvamaggiṃ  paricara handa te aggidārukaṃ   
  
      Tato kaṭṭhaṃ gahetvāna aggiṃ ujjālayī jino 
 Na tattha kaṭṭhaṃ pajjhāyi pāṭihīraṃ  mahesino 
       Na te aggi pajjalati āhutī te na vijjati 
 Niratthakaṃ vataṃ tuyhaṃ aggiṃ paricarassu me   
  
       Kīdiso so  mahāvīra aggi tava pavuccati 
 Mahampi kathayassetaṃ ubho parivarāmase   
  
   Metteyyattherāpadānaṃ sīmu 
   Bhohiti machasaṃ 
   Tuvaṃ aggiṃ machasaṃ   Pāṭibheraṃ machasaṃ 
   Te syā 
  
                 
  
       Hetudhamma nirodhāya kilesasamanāya ca 
 Issā macchariyaṃ hitvā tayo ete mamāhunī   
  
       Kīdiso tvaṃ mahāvīra kathaṃ gottosi mārisa 
 Ācārapaṭipatti te bāḷahaṃ kho mama ruccatī  
  
       Khattiyamhi                   kule jāto abhiññā pāramiṃ gato 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo   
       Yadi buddhosi sabbaññū pabhaṅkara tamonuda 
 Namassissāmi taṃ deva dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ  
  
      Pattharitvā jinacammaṃ nisīdana madāsahaṃ 
 Nisīda nātha sabbaññu upaṭṭhissamahaṃ tuvaṃ 
  
      Nisīdi bhagavā tattha ajinamhi suvitthate 
 Nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ pabbataṃ agamāsahaṃ 
  
      Khāribhārañca pūretvā tindukaphalamāhariṃ 
 Madhunā yojayitvāna phalaṃ buddhassa dāsahaṃ 
  
      Mama nijjhāyamānassa paribhuñji tadā jino 
 Tattha cittaṃ pasādesiṃ pekkhanto lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Mamassame nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo maṃ phalena tappesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Pañcavīsatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati 
  
      Tassa saṅkappamaññāya pubbakammasamaṅgino 
 Annaṃ pānañca vatthañca sayanañca anāmayo 
  
      Puññakammena saṃyuttā nibbattissanti tāvade 
 Sadā pamudito cāyaṃ bhavissati anāmayo 
  
      Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sabbattha sukhito hutvā manussattaṃ gamissati 
  
      Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragu 
 Sambuddhamupagantvāna arahā so bhavissati   
  
               
  
      Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattosmi viññutaṃ 
 Bhoge me ūnatā natthi phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Varadhammamanuppatto rāgadose samūhaniṃ 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tissametteyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Tissametteyyattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhama 
  
     Puṇṇakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Pabbhārakūṭaṃ                   nissāya sayambhu aparājito 
 Ābādhiko garu buddho  vasatī pabbatantare 
  
      Mama assamasāmantā panādo āsi tāvade 
 Buddhe nibbāyamānambhi āloko upapajjatha   
  
      Yāvatā vanasaṇḍasmiṃ acchakokataracchakā 
 Vyagghā  ca kesarī sabbe abhigajjiṃsu tāvade 
  
      Uppānaṃ tamahaṃ disvā pabbataṃ  agamāsahaṃ 
 Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Suphullaṃ sālarājaṃva sataraṃsiṃva uggataṃ 
 Vītaccikaṃva aṅgāraṃ nibbutaṃ aparājitaṃ 
  
      Tiṇaṃ kaṭṭhañca pūretvā citakaṃ tatthakāsahaṃ 
 Citakaṃ sukataṃ katvā sarīraṃ jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Sarīraṃ jhāpayitvāna gandhatoyaṃ samokiriṃ 
 Antalikkhe ṭhito yakkho nāmamaggahi tāvade 
  
      Yaṃ pūritaṃ  tayā kiccaṃ sayambhussa mahesino 
 Puṇṇako nāma nāmena sadā bhohi  tuvaṃ mune   
  
   Ābādhiko ca so buddho machasaṃ 
   Ādi tāvade syā udapajjatha machasaṃ 
   Vāḷā machasaṃ 
   Pabbhāraṃ machasaṃ 
   Taṃ puritaṃ syā 
   Yadā hosi syā 
   Muni sīmu 
  
               
  
      Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna devalokaṃ agacchahaṃ 
 Tattha dibbamayo gandho antalikkhe pavāyati  
  
      Tatrāpi nāmadheyyaṃ me puṇṇakoti ahū tadā 
 Devabhūto manusso vā saṅkappaṃ pūrayāmahaṃ 
  
      Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattatī  bhagavā 
 Idhāpi puṇṇako nāma nāmadheyyaṃ pakāsati 
  
      Tosayitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
      Ekanavute ito kappe  yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Sabbāsavā nābhijānāmi tanukiccassidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Puṇṇakattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
     Mettaguttherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa                   avidūre  asoko nāma pabbato 
 Tatthāsi assamo mayhaṃ vissakammena  māpito 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni 
 Nivāsayitvā pubbanhe piṇḍāya maṃ upāgami 
  
      Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Paggayha sugatappattaṃ  sappitelena pūrayiṃ  
  
      Datvānahaṃ buddhaseṭṭhe sumedhe lokanāyake 
 Añjalimpaggahetvāna bhīyo  hāsaṃ janesahaṃ 
  
       Iminā sappidānena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Devabhūto manusso vā labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ 
  
      Vinipātaṃ vivajjetvā saṃsarāmi bhavābhave 
 Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhitvā labhāmi acalaṃ padaṃ   
  
   Antalikkhā pavassati machasaṃ 
   Vattate machasaṃ 
   Ekanavutito kappe machasaṃ 
   Himavattassāvidure machasaṃ 
   Visukammena sīmu 
   Sugataṃ pattaṃ sīmu Subhakaṃ pattaṃ     
   Sappitelaṃ apūrayiṃ machasaṃ 
   Bhiyyo machasaṃ 
                 
  
       Lābhā tuyhaṃ suladdhaṃ te yaṃ maṃ addakkhi brāhmaṇaṃ   
 Mama dassanamāgamma arahā tvaṃ bhavissasi 
  
      Vissattho hohi mā bhiyi adhigantvā mahāyasaṃ 
 Mamaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna parimokkhasi jātiyā 
  
      Iminā sappidānena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Devabhūto manusso vā labhase vipulaṃ sukhaṃ 
  
      Iminā sappidānena mettacittavatāya ca 
 Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissasi 
  
      Aṭṭhatiṃsatikkhattuñca devarājā bhavissasi 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissasi 
 Cāturanto vijitāvī jambusaṇḍassa  issaro 
  
      Mahāsamuddovakkhobho duddharo paṭhavi yathā 
 Evameva ca te bhogā appameyyā bhavissare   
  
      Saṭṭhikoṭi bhiraññassa cajitvā  pabbajiṃ ahaṃ 
 Kiṃ kusalaṃ gavesanto bāvariṃ upasaṅkamiṃ 
  
      Tattha                   mante adhīyāmi chaḷaṅgaṃ nāma lakkhaṇaṃ 
 Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ uppajjitvaṃ mahāmuni 
  
      Tava dassanakāmohaṃ āgatomhi mahāmuni 
 Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi sappiṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ 
 Etthantare nābhijāne sappi viññāpitaṃ mayā  
  
      Mama saṅkappamaññāya uppajjati yadicchakaṃ 
 Cittamaññāya nibbattaṃ sabbe santappayāmahaṃ 
  
      Aho buddho aho dhammo  aho no satthusampadā 
 Thokaṃ hi sappiṃ datvāna appameyyaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
  
      Mahāsamudde udakaṃ yāvatā nerupassato 
 Mama sappiṃ upādāya kalabhāgaṃ na phassati  
  
   Brāhmaṇa machasaṃ 
   Jambumaṇḍassa machasaṃ 
   Catvā na sīmu datvāna syā 
   Sappiṃ viññāpitaṃ mayā machasaṃ 
   Aho buddhā aho dhammā machasaṃ 
   Na hessati machasaṃ Hissati syā 
  
                 
  
      Yāmatā cakkavāḷassa kariyantassa  rāsito 
 Mama nibbattavatvatthānaṃ okāso so na sammati 
  
      Pabbatarājā himavā pavaropi siluccayo 
 Mamānulittagandhassa upanidhiṃ  na hessati 
  
      Vatthaṃ gandhañca sappiñca aññañca diṭṭhadhammikaṃ 
 Asaṅkhatañca nibbānaṃ sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Satipaṭṭhānasayano samādhijhānagotaro 
 Bojjhaṅgabhojano ajja  sappidānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ ādhismā mettagutthero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Mettaguttherassa apadānaṃ katiyaṃ 
  
     Dhotakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
  
      Gaṅgā bhāgirathi nāma himavantā pabhāvitā 
 Haṃsavatiyā dvārena anusandati tāvade 
  
      Sobhito nāma ārāmo gaṅgākūle sumāpito 
 Tattha padumuttaro buddho vasate lokanāyako 
  
      Tidasehi                   yathā indo manujehi purakkhato 
 Nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhitova kesarī 
  
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā vasāmi  brāhmaṇo ahaṃ 
 Chaḷaṅgo nāma nāmena evannāmo mahāmuni 
  
      Aṭṭhārasasissasatā parivārenti maṃ tadā 
 Tehi sissehi samito gaṅgātīrā upāgamiṃ 
  
      Tatthaddasāsiṃ samaṇe nikkuhe dhotapāpake 
 Bhāgīrathiṃ tarantehaṃ  evaṃ cittesi tāvade 
  
   Kārayantassa syā Kayirantassa     
   Upanidhaṃ simu 
   Bojjhaṅgajanano syā 
   Ahosiṃ syā 
   Tarantohaṃ syā 
  
                 
  
       Sāyaṃ pātaṃ tarantāme buddhaputtā mahāyasā 
 Vihesayanti attānaṃ tesaṃ attā vihaññati 
  
      Sadevakassa lokassa buddho aggo pavuccati 
 Natthi me dakkhiṇe kāraṃ gatimaggavisodhanaṃ 
  
      Yannūna buddhaseṭṭhassa setuṃ gaṅgāya kāraye 
 Kārāpetvā imaṃ kammaṃ santarāmi imaṃ bhavaṃ   
  
      Satasahassaṃ datvāna setuṃ kārāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Saddahanto  kataṃ kārāṃ vipulaṃ me bhavissati   
      Kārāpetvāna taṃ setuṃ upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Sirasi añjaliṃ katvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
       Satasahassassa vayaṃ katvā  kārāpito mayā 
 Tavatthāya mahāsetu paṭigaṇha mahāmuni   
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me setuṃ akāresi pasanno sehi pāṇihi tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama 
 bhāsato 
  
      Darito pabbatāto vā rukkhāto  patitopayaṃ 
 Cutopi lacchati ṭhānaṃ setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Nāssa corā pasahanti nātimaññanti khattiyā 
 Sabbe tarissanāmitte setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Abbhokāsagataṃ                   santaṃ kaṭhinātapatāpitaṃ 
 Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ na bhavissanti cedanā 
  
      Devaloke manusse vā hatthiyānaṃ sunimmitaṃ 
 Tassasa saṅkappamaññāya nibbattissati tāvade 
  
      Sahassassā vātajavā sindhavā sīghavāhanā 
 Sāyaṃ pātaṃ upessanti setudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
      Āgantvāna manussattaṃ sukhitoyaṃ bhavissati 
 Ihāpi  manujasseva hatthiyānaṃ bhavissati 
  
   Datvā machasaṃ 
   Pabbatato machasaṃ 
   Rukkhato machasaṃ 
   Vehāsaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena  satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo   
  
      Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ jalajuttamanāmake 
 Tattha kāraṃ karitvāna pattohaṃ āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Padhānapahitattomhi upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhapi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhotako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Dhotakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ 
  
     Upasivattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre anomo nāma pabbato 
 Assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā 
  
      Nadī ca sandatī tattha supatthitthā manoramā 
 Anupatitthe jāyantī padumuppalakā bahu 
  
      Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā muñjarohitā 
 Macchakacchapasañchannā nadikā sandate sadā 
  
      Nimirā pupphinā tattha asokā khuddamālakā 
  Punnāgā giripunnāgā sampavanti mamassamaṃ 
  
   Gottena machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Kūṭajā                   pupphinā tattha tiṇasūlavanāni ca 
 Sālā ca salalā tattha campakā pupphitā bahū 
  
      Ajjunā atimuttā ca mahānāmā ca pupphitā 
 Asanā madhugandhī ca pupphitā te mamassame 
  
      Uddālakā pāṭalikā yūthikā ca piyaṅgukā 
 Bimbijālakasañchannā samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ 
  
      Mātaṅgavā  sattaliyo pāṭalī sinduvārakā 
 Aṅkolakā bahū tattha tālakūṭā ca  pupphitā 
  
      Seleyyakā bahū tattha pupphitā mama assame 
 Etesu pupphamānesu  sobhanti pādapā bahu 
 Samantā tena gandhena vāyate mama assamo 
  
      Harītakā āmalakā ambā jambu vihīṭakā   
 Kolā bhallātakā billā phārusakaphalāni ca 
      Tindukā ca piyālā ca madhukā kāsumāriyo   
 Labujā panasā tattha kadalī badarīphalā   
  
      Ambāṭakā bahu tattha vallikāraphalāni ca 
 Bījapūrasapāriyo  phalitā mama assame 
  
      Āḷakā isimuggā ca tato modaphalā bahū 
 Avaṭā pakkabharitā pilakakhudumbarāni ca 
  
      Pipphalī maricā tattha nigrodhā ca kapitthanā 
 Udumbarakā babhavo kaṇḍapakkā ca pāriyo   
  
      Ete vaññe ca babhavo phalitā assame mama 
 Puppharukkhāpi babhavo pupphitā mama assame 
  
      Āluvā ca kaḷambā ca bilāli takkalāni ca 
 Ālakā tālakā ceva vijjanti assame mama 
  
      Assamassāvīdure me mahājātassaro ahu 
 Acchodako sītajalo putatittho manoramo 
  
      Padumuppalā bahū tattha puṇḍarīkasamāyutā 
 Mandālakehi                   sañchannā nānāgandhasameritā 
  
   Mātaggarā machasaṃ Mātakarā syā Mātaṅgā vā     
   Tālakuṭṭhī ca machasaṃ 
   Pupphajātesu machasaṃ 
   Ambajambuvihītakā machasaṃ 
   Kāsumārayo machasaṃ 
   Candarīphalā syā     
   Cirasaṃrasapākā ca syā 
   Kaṇḍupaṇṇā ca bhariyo machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Gabbhaṃ gaṇyahanti padumā aññe pupphanti kesarī 
 Opupphapattā tiṭṭhanti padumakaṇṇikā  bahu 
  
      Madhu bhisambhā savati khīraṃ sappī mulāḷihi 
 Samantā tena gandhena nānā gandhasameritā 
  
      Kumudā ambagandhī ca nayitā dissare bahū 
 Jātassarassānukūlaṃ ketakā pupphitā bahū 
  
      Suphullā bandhujīvā ca setacārī sugandhikā 
 Kumbhilā suṃsumārā ca gahakā tattha jāyare 
  
      Uggāhakā ajagarā tattha jātassare bahu 
 Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā  muñjarohitā 
  
      Macchakacchapa sañchannā atho sampaṭakehi ca 
 Pārevatā ravihaṃsā kukutthā  ca nadīcarā 
  
      Dindibhā cakkavākā ca campakā jivajīvakā 
 Kalandakā ukkusā ca senakā uddharā bahu 
  
      Koṭṭhakā sukapotā ca kulīrā  camarā bahū 
 Kāreṇiyo  ca tilakā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ 
  
      Sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchakā 
 Vānarā kinnarā ceva dissanti mama assame 
  
      Tāni gandhāṇi ghāyanto bhakkhayanto phalānahaṃ 
 Gandhodakaṃ pinto ca vasāmi mama assame 
  
      Eṇimigā varāhā ca pasadā khuddarūpakā 
 Aggikā jotikā ceva vasanti mama assame 
  
      Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca sāḷikā pi ca kokilā 
 Mañjarikā bahū tattha kosikā poṭṭhasīsakā 
  
      Pisāvā dānavā ceva kumbhaṇḍā rakkhayā bahū 
 Garuḷā pannagā ceva vasanti mama assame 
  
   Padumākaṇṇikā machasaṃ   Balajā machasaṃ 
   Kukkutthā syā 
   Tuliyā machasaṃ 
   Kāseniyā syā 
  
 Piṭuva    
  
      Mahānubhāvā isayo santavittā samāhitā kamaṇḍaludharā                   
 sabbe ajinuttaravāsanā 
 Te jaṭābhārabharitā  vasanti mama assame 
  
      Yugamattañca pekkhantā nipakā santavuttino 
 Lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā vasanti mama assame 
  
      Vākacīraṃ dhunantā te phoṭentājinacammakaṃ 
 Sabalehi upatthaddhā gacchanti ambare sadā   
  
      Na te dakaṃ āharanti kaṭṭhaṃ vā aggidārukaṃ 
 Sayañca upasampannā pāṭihīrassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Lohadoṇiṃ gahetvāna vanamajjhe vasanti te 
 Kuñjarāva mahānāgā asambhītāva kesarī 
  
      Aññe gacchanti goyānaṃ aññe pubbavīdehakaṃ   
 Aññe ca uttarakuruṃ sakaṃ balamavassitā   
 Tato piṇḍaṃ āharitvā paribhuñjanti ekato 
  
      Sabbesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ uggatejāna tādinaṃ 
 Ajinavammasaddena vanaṃ saddāyate tadā 
  
      Edisā te mahāvīra sissā uggatapā mama 
 Parivuto ahaṃ tehi vasāmi mama assame 
  
      Tositā sakakammena vanītāpi samāgatā 
 Ārādhayiṃsu maṃ ete sakakammābhilāsino 
 Sīlavanto ca nipakā appamaññāsu kovidā 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Samayaṃ saṃviditvāna upagacchi vināyako 
  
      Upagantvāna sambuddho ātāpī nipako muni 
 Pattaṃ paggayha sambuddho bhikkhāya mamupāgami 
  
      Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ 
 Tiṇasantharaṃ paññapetvā  sālapupphehi okiriṃ 
  
      Nisīdetvāna  sambuddhaṃ haṭṭho saṃviggamānaso 
 Khippaṃ pabbatamāruyha agaruṃ aggahiṃ ahaṃ 
  
   Jaṭābhārabharitāva machasaṃ jaṭābhārabharitā ca syā 
   Tadā machasaṃ 
   Pubbavidehakaṃ syā     
   Pabamapassitā syā     
   Paññāpetvā machasaṃ 
   Nisādetvāna machasaṃ nisīditvāna syā 
  
                 
  
      Kumbhamattaṃ gahetvāna panasaṃ devagandhikaṃ 
 Khandhe āropayitvāna upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ 
  
      Phalaṃ                   buddhassa datvāna agaruṃ anulimpahaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ avandahaṃ   
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Isimajjhe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me phalañca agaruṃ āsanañca adāsi me 
 Tamahaṃ cittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Gāme vā yadi vāraññe pabbhāresu guhāsu vā 
 Imassa cittamaññāya nibbattissati bhojanaṃ 
  
      Devaloke manusse vā upapanno ayaṃ naro 
 Bhojanehi ca vatthehi parisaṃ tappayissati 
  
      Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Akkhobhabhogo hutvāna saṃsarissatayaṃ naro 
  
      Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca saṃsarissatayaṃ taro 
  
      Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Ekasattatikkhattuñca devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito   
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharissatanāsavo   
  
      Suladdhalābho laddho me yohaṃ addakkhiṃ nāyakaṃ 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Gāme vā yadi vāraññe pabbhāresu guhāsu vā 
 Mama saṅkappamaññāya bhojanaṃ hoti me sadā 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgoca bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷahiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upasīvo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Upasīvattherassa apadānaṃ pañcamaṃ 
  
   Avandihaṃ machasaṃ 
   Upasīvo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako syā 
  
                 
  
     Nandakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Migaluddo                   pure āsiṃ araññe kānate ahaṃ 
 Pasadaṃ migamesanto sayambhuṃ addasaṃ jinaṃ        Anuruddho nāma sambuddho 
 sayambhū aparājito 
 Vivekakāmo so dhīro vanamajjhogahī tadā 
  
      Catudaṇḍe gahetvāna catuṭṭhāne ṭhapesahaṃ 
 Maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā padamapupphehi chādayiṃ 
  
      Maṇḍapaṃ chādayitvāna sayambhuṃ abhivādayiṃ 
 Dhanuṃ tattheva nikkhippa pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Pabbajitassa aciraṃ  vyādhi me upapajjatha 
 Pubbakammaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
      Pubbakammena saṃyutto tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ 
 Tattha soṇṇamayaṃ vyamhaṃ nibbattati yadicchakaṃ 
  
      Sahassayuttahavāhiṃ dibbayānamadhiṭṭhito 
 Āruhitvāna taṃ yānaṃ gacchāmahaṃ yadicchakaṃ 
  
      Tato me nīyamānassa devabhūtassa me sato 
 Samantā yojanasataṃ maṇḍapo me dharīyati 
  
      Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭāmi accantaṃ  pupphasanthate 
 Antaḷikkhā ca padumā vassanti  niccakālikaṃ 
  
      Marīvike phandamāne tappamāne ca ātape 
 Na maṃ tāpeti ātāpo maṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Duggatiṃ samatikkanto apāyā pihitā mama 
 Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāpo me na vijjati 
      Mahīsaññaṃ adhiṭṭhāya loṇatoyaṃ tarāmahaṃ 
 Tassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Apathampi  pathaṃ katvā gacchāmi anilañjase 
 Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Pubbenivāsaṃ                   jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Āsavā me parikkhiṇā buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Jahitā purimā jāni buddhassa oraso ahaṃ 
 Dāyādomhi ca saddhamme buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Ahaṃ machasaṃ 
   Na ciraṃ pabbajitassa machasaṃ 
   Acchante machasaṃ 
   Vassante machasaṃ 
   Abbhamhi syā 
  
                 
  
      Ārādhitomhi sugataṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Dhammaddhajo dhammadāyādo buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Pāraṅgamaniyaṃ maggaṃ apucchiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Ajjhiṭṭho kathayī buddho gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ 
 Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ 
  
      Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ parimuttomhi jātiyā 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nandako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Nandakattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ 
  
     Hemakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Pabbhārakūṭaṃ nissāya anomo nāma tāpayo 
 Assamaṃ sukataṃ katvā paṇṇasāle vasī tadā 
  
      Siddhaṃ tassa tapokammaṃ siddhipatto sake bale 
 Sakasāmaññavikkanto ātāpī nipako muni 
  
      Visārado sasamaye paravāde ca kovido 
 Paṭṭho bhūmantalikkhambhi uppātambhi ca kovido 
  
      Vītasoko nirārambho appāhāro alolupo 
 Lābhālābhena santuṭṭho jhāyī jhānarato muni 
  
      Piyadassī nāma sambuddho aggo kāriṇiko muni 
 Satte tāretukāmo so karuṇāya pharī tadā 
  
      Bodhaneyyaṃ                   janaṃ disvā piyadassī mahāmuni 
 Cakkavāḷasahassampi gantvā ovadate muni 
  
      Mamuddharitukāmo so mamassamamupāgami 
 Na diṭṭho me jino pubbe na suto pi ca kassa ci 
  
                 
  
      Uppātā supinā mayhaṃ lakkhaṇā suppakāsitā 
 Paṭṭho bhūmantalikkhambhi nakkhattapadakovido 
  
      Sohaṃ buddhassa sutvāna tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Bhuñjanto  vā nisinno vā sarāmi niccakālikaṃ 
  
      Mayi evaṃ sarantambhi bhagavāpi anussari 
 Buddhaṃ anussarantassa pīti me hoti tāvade 
  
      Kālañca punarāgamma upesi maṃ mahāmuni 
 Sampattepi na jānāmi ayaṃ buddho mahāmuni 
  
      Anukampako kāruṇiko piyadassī mahāmuni 
 Sañjānāpesi attānaṃ ahaṃ buddho sadevake 
  
      Sañjānitvāna sambuddhaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvaṃ idaṃ pacanamabraviṃ 
  
       Aññe  pīṭhe ca pallaṅke āsandīsu nisīdare 
 Tuvampi sabbadassāvī nisīdi ratanāsane  
  
      Sabbaratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ nimminitvāna tāvade 
 Piyadassissa munino adāsiṃ iddhinimmitaṃ 
  
      Ratane ca nisinnassa pīṭhake iddhinimmite 
 Kumbhamattaṃ jambuphalaṃ adāsiṃ tāvade ahaṃ 
  
      Mama hāsaṃ janetvāna paribhuñji mahāmuni 
 Tadā cittaṃ pasādetvā satthārambhivādayiṃ 
  
      Piyadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Ratanāsanamāsīno imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me ratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ amataṃ ca phalaṃ adā 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Sattasattati kappāni devaloke ramissati 
 Pañcasattatikkhattuñca cakkavattī bhavissati 
  
      Dvattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Soṇṇamayaṃ                   rūpimayaṃ pallaṅkaṃ sukataṃ bahuṃ 
 Lohitaṅkamayaṃ  ceva lacchati ratanāmayaṃ 
  
   Tiṭṭhanto machasaṃ 
   Sabbe syā 
   Lohitaṅgamayaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Caṅkamantampi manujaṃ puññakammasamaṅginaṃ 
 Pallaṅkāni anekāni parivārissare tadā 
  
      Kūṭāgārā ca pāsādā sayanañca mahārahaṃ 
 Imassa cittamaññāya nibbattissanti tāvade 
  
      Saṭṭhināgasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
 Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā homakappanavāsasā  
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  
 Imaṃ paricarissanti ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
      Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
 Ājānīyāva jātiyā sindhavā sighavāhino 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi illiyāvāpadhārihi  
 Imaṃ paricarissanti ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ  
  
      Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā 
 Dīpā athopi veyyagghā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi 
 Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhidhenusahassāni dohaññā puṅgavūsabhe 
 Vacchake janayissanti ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Soḷasitthisahassāni dohaññā puṅgavūsabhe 
 Vacchake janayissanti ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ ratanapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate gotamo nāma cakkhumā 
 Namandhakāraṃ vidhametvā  buddho loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dassanamāgamma pabbajissatakiñcano  
 Tosayitvāna satthāraṃ sāsaneśiramissati 
      Tassa                   dhammaṃ suṇitvāna nilese ghātayissati 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Viriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ 
 Uttamatthaṃ patthayanto sāsane viharāmahaṃ 
  
      Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthi dāni punabbhavo 
  
   Hemakappanivāsanā sīmu Syā 
   Illiyācāpadhārīhi machasaṃ 
   Ratanapiṭhassidaṃ machasaṃ 
   Cāpahatthehi cammibhi sīmu 
   Vidhamitvā machasaṃ 
   Pabbajissati kiñcano machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgoca bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā hemako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Hemakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ 
  
 Sattaraghamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ 
  
     Todeyyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Rājāsi vijayo  nāma ketumatipuruttame 
 Sūro vikkamasampanno puramajjhāvasī tadā 
  
      Tassa rañño pamattassa aṭaviyo samuṭṭhahuṃ 
 Otārā  tuṇḍikā ceva raṭṭhaṃ viddhaṃsayuṃ tadā 
  
      Paccante kupite khippaṃ sannipātesarindamo 
 Bhaṭe ceva balatthe ca ariṃ niggāhayī tadā 
  
      Hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā sūrā ca cammayodhino 
 Dhanuggahā ca uggā ca sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Āḷārikā kappakā ca nahāpakā  mālakārakā 
 Sūrā vijitayaṅgāmā sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Khaggahatthā ca purisā vāpahatthā ca cammino 
 Luddā vijitasaṅgāmā sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Tidhā pabhinnā mātaṅgā kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā 
 Suvaṇṇakacchālaṅkārā sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Khamā sītassa uṇhassa ukkāraharaṇassa  ca 
 Yodhājīvā katakammā sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
   Rājā ajitañjayo machasaṃ Rājā vijitajayo syā 
   Uttarā syā ocarā     
   Nahāpakā machasaṃ 
   Ukkāruharaṇassa sīmu machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Saṃkhasaddaṃ                   bherisaddaṃ atho uddhama saddakaṃ 
 Etehi te hāsayanto sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Tisulakontamantehi kavacehi  tomarehi  ca 
 Koṭṭayantā  nipātentā sabbe sannipatuṃ tadā 
  
      Kimevātanisāmetvā  sa rājā ajitaṃ jino   
 Saṭṭhipāṇasahassāni sule uttāsayī tadā 
  
      Saddaṃ mānusakākaṃsu aho rājā adhammiko 
 Niraye paccamānassa kadā anto bhavissati 
  
      Sayanehaṃ tuvaṭṭento sayāmi niraye tadā 
 Na supāmi divārattiṃ sūlena tajjayanti maṃ 
  
      Kiṃ pamādena rajjena vāhanena balena ca 
 Na te pahonti dhāretuṃ tāsayanti  mamaṃ sadā 
  
      Kiṃ me puttehi dārehi rajjena sakalena ca 
 Yannūnā pabbajeyyāhaṃ gatimaggaṃ visodhaye 
  
      Saṭṭhināgasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsite 
 Suvaṇṇagacche mātaṅge hemakappanavāsase  
  
      Āruḷhe gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi 
 Saṅgāmāvacare dhāne  anapekkho vibhāyahaṃ 
 Sakakammena santatto nikkhamiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusite 
 Ājānīye ca jātiyā nindhave sīghavāhane 
  
      Ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi 
 Pahāyitvāna    te sabbe nikkhamiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsite 
 Dīpe athopi veyyagghe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje 
 Te sabbe parihāretvā   pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhidhenusahassāni                   sabbā kaṃsupadhāraṇā 
 Tāyopi   chaḍḍayitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
   Utuja machasaṃ uddhaṭa syā uddhava sīmu 
   Tisūlakontimattehi machasaṃ 
   Kaccatomarehi ca machasaṃ 
   Koṭṭettānaṃ sīmu 
   Kavacānivāsetvā syā 
   Ajitañjino syā Ajitañjayo machasaṃ 
   Tāpayanti machasaṃ 
   Hemakappanivāsate machasaṃ 
   hāne machasaṃ 
    Pahāretvāna machasaṃ 
    Parivajjetvā syā 
    Pāpiyo syā 
  
                 
  
      Saṭṭhiitthisahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
 Vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā 
  
      Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 Tā hitvā kandamānāyo pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso 
 Chaḍḍayitvāna taṃ rajjaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Nagarā nikkhamitvāna himavantamupāgamiṃ 
 Bhāgirathinadītīre assamaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna aggyagāraṃ akāsahaṃ 
 Āraddhaviriyo pahitatto vasāmi assame ahaṃ 
  
      Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā suññāgāre ca jhāyato 
 Na tu vijjati tāso me na passe bhayabheravaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma sumbuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni 
 Ñāṇālokena jotanto loke uppajji tāvade 
  
      Mama assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhiko 
 Buddhaseṭṭhamhi uppanne ārocesi mamaṃ tadā 
  
       Buddho loke samuppanno sumedho nāma cakkhumā 
 Tāreti janataṃ sabbaṃ tampi so tārayissati 
  
      Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvaṃ saṃviggo āsi tāvade 
 Buddho buddhoti cintento assamaṃ paṭisāmayiṃ 
  
      Aggidāruñca chaḍḍetvā saṃsāmetvāna santhataṃ 
 Assamaṃ abhivanditvā nikkhamiṃ vipinā ahaṃ 
  
      Tato vandanamādāya gāmā gāmaṃ purā purā 
 Devadevaṃ gavesanto upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ 
  
      Bhagavā tambhi samaye sumedho lokanāyako 
 Catusaccaṃ pakāsento bodheti janataṃ bahuṃ 
      Añjalimpaggahetvāna sīse katvāna vandanaṃ 
 Samubuddhaṃ abhivādetvā imā gāthā abhāsahaṃ 
  
       Vassike pupphamānambhi santike upavāyati 
 Tvaṃ vīra guṇagandhena disā sabbā pavāyasi 
  
      Campake nāgavanike atimuttakaketake 
 Sālesu pupphamānesu anuvātaṃ pavāyati 
  
                 
  
      Tava                   gandhaṃ suṇitvāna himavantā idhāgamiṃ 
 Pūjemi taṃ mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha mahāyasa 
  
      Varavandannonulimpiṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā tuṇhī aṭṭhāsī tāvade 
  
      Sumedho nāma bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo meguṇe pakittesi vandanañca apūjayī 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Ādeyyavākyavacano brahmā uju patāpavā 
 Pañcavīsatikappāni sappabhāso bhavissati 
  
      Chabbīsatikappasate devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Tato cutoyaṃ manujo manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Puññakammena saṃyutto brahmabandhu bhavissati 
  
      Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū 
 Tilakkhaṇena sampanno bāvarī nāma brāhmaṇo 
  
      Tassa sisso bhavitvāna hessati mantapāragū 
 Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
  
      Pucchitvā nipuṇe pañhe bhāvayitvāna añjasaṃ  
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo   
  
      Tividhaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassasa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā todeyyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Todeyyettherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ 
  
   Mānasaṃ syā 
  
                 
  
     Jatukaṇṇittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nagare haṃsavatiyā seṭṭhiputto ahosahaṃ 
 Samappito kāmaguṇe parivāremahaṃ tadā 
  
      Tayo                    pāsādamāruyha ubbiddhā gehalañchakā  
 Tattha taccehi gītehi parivāremahaṃ tadā 
  
      Turiyā āhatā mayhaṃ sammatālasamāhitā 
 Naccantā  itthiyo sabbā haranti yeva me mano 
  
      Velāpikā lāmaṇikā kuñjavāsī timajjhikā  
 Laṅghikā sokajjhāyī  ca parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Vetālino kumbhathūnī naṭā ca naccakā bahū 
 Naṭakā nāṭakā ceva parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Kappakā nahāpakā sudā mālākārā sumāpakā   
 Jallā mallāti sabbeva  parivārenti maṃ sadā 
  
      Etesu kīḷamānesu sikkhite katupāsane 
 Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi indeva tidasaṅgaṇe 
  
      Addhikā pathikā sabbe yācakā carakā bahū 
 Upagacchanti te niccaṃ bhikkhayantā mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Samaṇā brāhmaṇā ceva puññakkhettā anuttarā 
 Vaḍḍhayantā mamaṃ puññaṃ āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Paṭakā laṭakā  sabbe nigaṇṭhā pupphasāṭakā 
 Tedaṇḍikā ekasikhā āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Ājīvakā viluttāvī godhammā devadhammikā 
 Rajojalladharā ete āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Parivattakā siddhipattā  koṇḍapuggaṇikā   bahū 
 Tapassī vanacārī ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Oḍḍakā damiḷā ceva sākulā malayālakā 
 Sabarā   yonakā ceva āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Andhakā                   muṇḍakā sabbe kolakā sānuvindakā    
 Ārāvacīnaraṭṭhā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
   Tato machasaṃ 
   Mahābhoge valañjako machasaṃ   Rañjanti syā 
   Vāmanikā syā 
   Kuñjavā sīhivajjhitā syā 
   Supāsakā machasaṃ 
   Jallā mallā ca te sabbe machasaṃ   Paṭagā machasaṃ 
   Parittakā santipattā machasaṃ 
    Koṭapugganikā machasaṃ 
    Savarā machasaṃ 
    Hanuvindakā machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Alasandakā pallavakā babbarā bhaggakārusā   
 Rohitā  cetaputtā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Mādhurakā kosalakā kāsikā  hatthiporikā 
 Isiṇḍā makkalā ceva āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Celāvakā arammā ca okkalā  meghalā  bahū 
 Khuddakā suddakā ceva āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Rohaṇā sindhavā ceva citakā ekakaṇṇikā 
 Suraṭṭhā aparantā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Suppārakā kikumārā  malayā  soṇṇabhūmikā 
 Vajjī tārā  ca te sabbe āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Naḷakārā pesakārā cammakārā ca tacchakā 
 Kammārā kumbhakārā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Maṇikārā lohakārā soṇṇakārā ca dussikā 
 Tipukārā ca sabbe āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Usukārā bhamakārā pesakārā ca gandhīkā 
 Raja kā tunnavāyā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Telikā kaṭṭhahārā ca udahārā ca pessikā 
 Supikā suparakkhā ca āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
  
      Dovārikā                   aṇikaṭṭhā vandikā  pupphachaḍḍakā 
 Hatthāruhā hatthipālā āgacchanti mamaṃ gharaṃ 
      Ānandassa mahārañño   pamattassa   adāsahaṃ 
 Sattavaṇṇena ratanena ūnattaṃ   pūrayāmahaṃ 
  
      Ye mayā kittitā sabbe nānāvaṇṇā bahujjanā 
 Tesāhaṃ cittamaññāya tappayiṃ ratanenahaṃ 
  
      Vaggūsu bhāsamānāsu vajjamānāsu bherisu 
 Saṃkhesu dhamayantesu sakagehe ramāmahaṃ 
  
   Dhammarāniggamānusā machasaṃ 
   Gehikā machasaṃ 
   Kaliṅgā machasaṃ 
   Ārabbhā machasaṃ 
   Oghulā machasaṃ 
   Kumārā machasaṃ 
   Malla machasaṃ 
   Taṅgā machasaṃ 
   Bandhikā machasaṃ Ganthikā syā Sandikā     
    Ānandassa nāma rañño syā Arindamanāmarañño     
    Mamattassa machasaṃ samaggassa syā 
    Ūnatthaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Bhagavā tambhi samaye padumuttaranāyako 
 Vasīsatasahassehi parikkhīṇāsavehi so 
  
      Bhikkhūhi sahito vīthiṃ paṭipajjittha cakkhumā 
 Obhāsento disā sabbā dīparukkhova jotati 
  
      Vajjanti bheriyo sabbā gacchante lokanāyake 
 Pabhā niddhāvate tassa sataraṃsīva uggato 
  
      Kavāṭantarikāyāpi paviṭṭhena ca raṃsinā   
 Antoghare suvipulo āloko āsi tāvade 
  
      Pabhaṃ disvāna buddhassa pārisajje acocahaṃ 
 Nissaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho imaṃ vīthimupāgato 
  
      Khippaṃ oruyha pāsādā āgamiṃ antarāpaṇaṃ 
 Sambuddhambhivādetvā idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Anukampatu me sambuddhaṃ abhinesiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ 
 Tattha annena pānena santappesiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
  
      Nimantayitvā  sambuddhaṃ abhinesiṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ 
 Tattha antena pānena santappesiṃ mahāmuniṃ 
  
      Bhuttāviṃ kālamaññāya buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino 
 Sataṅgikena turiyena buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Antoghare nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo                   maṃ turiyehupaṭṭhāsī antapānañca dāsi me 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Pahūtahakkho hutvāna sabhirañño sabhojano 
 Catudīpe ekarajjaṃ kārayissata yaṃ naro 
  
      Pañcasīle samādāya dasakammapathe tato 
 Samādāya pavattento parisaṃ sikkhapessati  
      Turiyasatasahassāni nāriyo  samalaṅkatā 
 Vajjayissanti maṃ niccaṃ upaṭṭhānassasidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Tīṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
  
   Rasaminā machasaṃ 
   Nimantetvāna machasaṃ 
   Sikkhāpayissati machasaṃ 
   Bheriyo machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ   
 Anūnabhogo hutvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
  
      Ajjhāyako bhavitvāna tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragū 
 Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto carissati mahiṃ imaṃ 
      So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsanebhi ramissati 
  
      Ārādhayitvā  sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Kilese jhāpayitvāna arahāyaṃ bhavissati 
  
      Vipine vyaggharājāva migarājāva kesarī 
 Abhīto viharāmajja sakyaputtassa sāsane 
  
      Devaloke manusse vā daḷidde duggatimbhi vā 
 Nibbattiṃ me na passāmi upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Vivekamanuyuttombhi upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ gavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā jatukaṇṇithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Jatukaṇṇittherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ 
  
   Gottena machasaṃ 
   Ārādhayitvāna machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
     Udenattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa                   avidūre padumo nāma pabbato 
 Assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā 
  
      Nadiyo sandare supatitthā manoramā 
 Acchodakā sītajalā sundarā  nadiyo sadā 
  
      Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā muñjarohitā 
 Sobhentā nadiyo ete vasanti nadiyā sadā 
  
      Ambajambūhi sañchannā kareritilakā tathā 
 Uddālakā pāṭaliyo sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Aṅkolakā bimbijālā māyākārī ca pupphitā 
 Gandhena upavāyantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Atimuttā sattalikā nāgā sālā ca pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ  sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Kosambā salalā nīpā aṭṭhaṅgā ca supupphitā 
 Dabbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assama 
      Harītakā āmalakā ambajambu vibhīṭakā 
 Kolā bhallātakā billā phalāni bahu assame 
  
      Kalambā kandalī tattha pupphanti mama assame 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Asokapiṇḍī cavarī  nimbarukkhā ca pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Punnāgā giripunnāgā timirā tattha pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ smapavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Nigguṇḍī sirinigguṇḍī camparukkhettha pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Avidūre pokkharaṇī cakkavākūpakūjitā 
 Mandalakehi sañchannā padumuppalakehi ca 
  
   Sandare machasaṃ 
   Dibbagandhā sīmu 
   Asokapiṇḍicārī va machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Acchodakā                   sītajalā supatitthā manoramā 
 Acchā phalikasamānā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Padumā pupphare tattha puṇḍarīkā ca uppalā 
 Mandalakehi sañchannā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchāvalajā muñjarohitā 
 Vicarantā ca te tattha sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Kumbhīlā suṃsumārā ca kacchapā ca gahā bahū 
 Oguhā  ajagarā ca sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Pārevatā ravihaṃsā cakkavākā nadīcarā 
 Dindibhā sālikā cettha sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Nayitā ambagandhī ca ketakā tattha pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchakā 
 Anusañcarantā pavane sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Jaṭābhārena bharitā ajinuttaravāsanā 
 Anusañcarantā pavane sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Ajīnāni dharā ete nipakā santavuttino 
 Appahārā ca te sabbe sobhenti mama assamaṃ 
  
      Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna ajjhogayha vanaṃ tadā 
 Mūlaphalāni bhuñjantā vasanti assame sadā 
  
      Na te dāruṃ āharanti udakaṃ pādadhovanaṃ 
 Sabbesaṃ ānubhāvena sayamevāharīyati 
  
      Cullāsīti sahassāni isayettha samāgatā 
 Sabbeva jhāyino ete uttamatthagavesakā 
  
      Tapassīno brahmacārī codentā appaṇāvate 
 Ambarāvacarā sabbe vasanti assame tadā 
  
      Pañcāhaṃ sannīpatanti ekaggā santavuttino 
 Aññoññaṃ abhivādetvā pakkamanti disāmukhā 
  
   Ogahā machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragū 
 Tamandakāraṃ  vidhamaṃ uppajji tāvade jino 
  
      Mama                   assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhiko 
 So me saṃsittha sambuddhaṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ 
  
      Esa buddho samuppanno padumuttaro mahāmuni 
 Khippaṃ gantvāna sambuddhaṃ payirupāsaya  mārisa 
  
      Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā vippasannena cetasā 
 Assamaṃ saṃsāmetvāna nikkhamiṃ vipinā tadā 
  
      Ceḷeva ḍayhamānambhi nikkhamitvāna assamā 
 Ekarattiṃ nivasitvā  upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Catusaccaṃ pakāsonto desesi amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Supullaṃ padumaṃ gayha upagantvā mahesino 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
      Pūjayitvāna sambuddhaṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ 
 Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Yena ñāṇena sambuddho vasatīha anāsavo 
 Taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
      Saṃsārasotaṃ chinditvā tāresi sabbapāṇino 
 Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna taṇhāsotaṃ taranti te 
  
      Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ 
 Parāyaṇo patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dipaduttama   
  
      Yāvatā gaṇino loke satthavāhā pavuccare 
 Tuvaṃ aggosi sabbaññu tava antogadhāva te 
  
      Tava ñāṇena sabbaññu tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ 
 Tava dassanamāgamma dukkhassantaṃ karissare 
  
      Ye keci me gandhajātā loke vāyanti cakkhuma 
 Tava gandhasamo natthi puññakkhette mahāmune 
  
   Mahandhakāraṃ sīmu 
   Payirupāsa machasaṃ 
   Nivāsetvā machasaṃ 
   Dvīpaduttama machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Tiracchānayoniṃ nirayaṃ parimocesi  cakkhuma 
 Asaṃkhataṃ padaṃ santaṃ desesi tvaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo                   me ñāṇaṃ apūjesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   
  
      Suladdhalābhaṃ laddhombhi tosayitvāna subbataṃ 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā vibharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chalabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udeno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Udenattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ 
  
 Uddānaṃ 
  
 Metteyyo puṇṇako thero mettagū dhotakopi ca 
 Upasīvo ca nando ca hemako sattamo tahiṃ 
 Todeyyo jatukaṇṇī ca udeno ca mahāyaso 
 Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha asīti tīṇi cuttarīṃ 
  
 Metteyyavaggo ekacattāḷīsatimo   
  
   Parimocehi syā 
   Desehi syā 
   Ekacattāḷīsamo sīmu machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
     Bhaddālittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni 
 Vivekakāmo lokaggo himavantamupāgami 
  
      Ajjhogahetvā himavaṃ sumedho lokanāyako 
 Pallaṅkamābhujitvāna nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Samādhiṃ so samāpanto sumedho lokanāyako 
 Sattarattindivaṃ buddho nisīdi purisuttamo 
  
      Khārikājaṃ  gahetvāna vanamajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ 
 Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ 
  
      Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna sammajjitvāna assamaṃ 
 Catudaṇḍe thambhītvāna  akāsiṃ maṇḍapaṃ tadā 
  
      Sālapupphaṃ                   āharitvā maṇḍapaṃ jādayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano abhivandiṃ tathāgataṃ 
  
      Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Buddhassa giramañña sabbe devā samāgamuṃ 
 Asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho imā gāthā abhāsatha 
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Devasaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me sattāhaṃ maṇḍapaṃ dhārayī sālachāditaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Devabhūto manusso vā hemavaṇṇo bhavissati 
 Pahūtabhogo hutvāna kāmabhogī bhavissati 
  
      Saṭṭhināgasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā 
 Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅgusapāṇihi 
 Sāyaṃpāto  upaṭṭhānaṃ āgamissantimaṃ naraṃ 
 Tehi nāgehi parivuto ramissati ayaṃ naro 
  
   Bāribhāraṃ   machasaṃ 
   hapetvāna   machasaṃ 
   Sāyapāto       
                 
  
      Saṭṭhīassahasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā 
 Ājānīyā va jāniyā sindhavā sīghavāhino 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi illiyācāpadhārihi 
 Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhirathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā 
 Dīpā athopi veyyagghā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi 
 Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso 
 Pahūtadhanadhaññāni susamiddhāni sabbaso 
 Sadā pātubhavissanti buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Hatthi assā rasā patti senā ca caturaṅgini 
 Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Satānaṃ  pts page      tīṇikkhatatuñca devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharissatanāsavo 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassambhi addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Etthantaramupādāya gavesiṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Lābhā mayhaṃ suladdhaṃ me yamahaññāsi sāsanaṃ 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama 
 Tava ñāṇaṃ pakittetvā pattombhi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ yonuppajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sabbattha sukhito homi phalaṃ me ñāṇakittane 
  
                 
  
      Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattane bhavo 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vana me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddāli thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Bhaddālittherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ 
  
     Ekachattiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Candabhāgānadītīre assamo sukato mama 
 Susuddhapulinākiṇṇā paṇṇasālā sumāpitā 
  
      Uttānakūlā nadikā supatitthā manoramā 
 Macchakacchapasampannā susumāranisevitā 
  
      Acchā mayūrā dīpī ca karavīkā ca sālikā 
 Kūjanti sabbadā ete sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Kokilā mañjubhāṇī va haṃsā ca madhurassarā 
 Abhikujanti te tattha sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Sīhā vyagghā varāhā ca cakā  kokataracchakā 
 Giriduggambhi nādenti sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Eṇīmigā                   ca sarabhā bheraṇḍā sūkarā bahū 
 Giriduggambhi nādenti sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Uddālakā campakā ca pāṭalī sinduvārakā  
 Atimuttā asokā ca pupphanti mama assame 
  
      Aṅkolā yūthikā ceva sattalī bimbijālikā 
 Kaṇṇikā kaṇikārā ca pupphanti mama assame 
  
   Acchā   machasaṃ 
   Sinducārikā   sīmu 
  
                 
  
      Nāgā sālā ca saḷalā puṇḍarīkettha pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Ajjunā asanā cettha mahānāmā ca pupphitā 
 Sālā ca kaṅgupupphā ca sobhanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Ambā jambu ca tilakā nimbā ca sālakalyāṇi dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhayanti 
 mamassamaṃ 
  
      Asokā ca kapitthā ca bhaginimālettha  pupphitā 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Kadambā kadalī ceva isimuggā ca ropitā 
 Dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Harītakā āmalakā ambā jambu vibhītakā 
 Kolā bhallātakā billā phalino mama assame 
      Avidūre pokkharaṇī supatitthā manoramā 
 Mandālakehi sañjinnā padumuppalakehi ca 
  
      Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā aññe pupphanti kesarī 
 Opattakaṇaṇikā ceva pupphanti mama assame 
  
      Pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā  muñjarohitā 
 Acchodakambhi vicaraṃ sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Nayitā ambagandhi ca anukūle ca ketakā dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhayanti 
 mamassamaṃ 
  
      Madhū bhisambhā khirasappi mulāḷihi 
 Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantā sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Pulinā sobhanā tattha ākiṇṇā jalasevitā 
 Opupphā pupphitā senti sobhayantā mamassamaṃ 
  
      Jaṭābhārena bharitā ajinuttaravāsanā 
 Vākacīradharā sabbe sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Yugamattamapekkhantā                   nipakā santavuttino 
 Kāmabhoge anapekkhā vasanti mama assame 
  
   Hiricālettha machasaṃ 
   Khajā machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā paṅkadantā rajassirā 
 Rajojalladharā sabbe vasanti mama assame 
  
      Abhiññāpāramippattā antalikkhacarā ca te 
 Uggacchantā nabhaṃ ete sobhayanti mamassamaṃ 
  
      Tehi sissehi parivuto vasāmi vipine tadā 
 Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi sadā jhānasamappito 
  
      Bhagavā tambhi samaye atthadassi mahāmuni 
 Tamandhakāraṃ nāsento uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Atha aññataro sisso āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
 Mante ajjhetukāmo so chaḷaṅgaṃ nāmalakkhaṇaṃ 
  
      Buddho loke samuppanno atthadassī mahāmuni 
 Catusaccaṃ pakāsento deseti amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Tuṭṭhahaṭṭho pamudito dhammantaragatāsayo 
 Assamā abhinikkhamma imaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
       Buddho loke samuppanto battiṃsavaralakkhaṇo 
 Hatha sabbe gamissāma sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ   
  
      Ovādapaṭikarā te saddhamme pāramiṅgatā 
 Sādhūti sampaṭicchiṃsu uttamatthaṃ gavesakā 
  
      Jaṭābhārabharitā te ajinuttaravāsino 
 Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto  nikkhamiṃsu vanā tadā 
  
      Bhagavā tamhi samaye atthadassī mahāyaso 
 Catusaccaṃ pakāsento deseti amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Setacchattaṃ gahetvāna buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ 
 Ekāhaṃ dhārayitvāna buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ 
  
      Atthadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me chattamadhāresi pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Imassa jāyamānassa devatte atha mānuse 
 Dhāressati sadā chattaṃ chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Gavesantā machasaṃ 
  
                 
  
      Sattasattatikappāni                   devaloke ramissati 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca vakkavattī bhavissati 
  
      Sattasattatikkhattuñca devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Tamandhakāraṃ nāsento uppajjissati cakkhumā 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharissatanāsavo   
  
      Yato ahaṃ kammamakaṃ chattaṃ buddhassa dhārayaṃ 
 Etthantare na jānāmi setacchattaṃ adhāritaṃ 
  
      Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo 
 Chattadhāraṇamajjāpi vattate niccakālikaṃ 
  
      Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ atthadassissa tādino 
 Sabbāsavaparikkhiṇo natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā vatasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekachattiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
  
 Ekachattiyattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ 
  
     Tiṇasulakachadaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Jātijarañca maraṇaṃ paccavekkhiṃ ahaṃ tadā 
 Ekato abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Caramāno nupubbena gaṅgātīra mupāgamiṃ 
 Tatthaddasāsiṃ paṭhaviṃ gaṅgātīre samunnataṃ 
  
                 
  
      Asasmaṃ tattha māpetvā vasāmi assame ahaṃ 
 Sukato caṅkamo mayhaṃ nānādijagaṇāyuto 
  
      Mamupenti ca vissatthā kūjanti ca manoharaṃ 
 Ramamāno saha tehi vasāmi assame ahaṃ 
  
      Mama assamasāmantā migarājā catukkamo 
 Āsayā abhinikkhamma gajji so asanī viya
