     Catujjāttena gandhena nivayitvā   tamiṭṭhakaṃ 
 Muttā duggandhadosambhā sabbaṅgasusamāgatā 
  
     Sattapānisahassāni rataneheva sattihi 
 Kāretvā ghatapurāni vaṭṭiyo   ca sahassaso 
  
     Pakkhipitvā padipetvā ṭhapayi   sattapantiyo 
 Pujatthaṃ   lokanāthassa vippasannena cetasā 
  
     Tadāpi tamhi puññamhi bhāginihaṃ visesato 
 Puna kāsisu sañajāto sumitto iti vissuto 
  
     Tassāhaṃ bhariyā sukhitā sajjitā piyā 
 Tadāpi paccekamunino adāsi   ghanaceṭhanaṃ 
  
     Tassāpi bhāgini āsiṃ moditvā dānamuttamaṃ 
 Punāpi kāsiraṭṭhambhi jāto koliyajātiyā 
  
     Tadā koliyaputtānaṃ satehi saha pañcahi 
 Pañca paccekabuddhānaṃ satānisamupaṭṭhahi 
  
     Temāsaṃ tappayitvāna   adāsi ca ticivaraṃ   
 Jāyā tassatadā āsiṃ puññakammapathānugāta 
                   
     Tato cuto ahu rājā nando nāma mahāyaso 
 Tassāpi mahesi āsiṃ sabbakāmasamiddhini 
  
     Tadā ca so   bhavitvāna brahmadatto mahipati 
 Padumavatiputtānaṃ paccekamuninaṃ tadā 
  
     Satānipañcanunāni yāvajīvaṃ upaṭṭhahi 
 Rājuyyāne nivāsetvā nibbutāni ca pujayi 
  
     Cetiyāni ca kāretvā pabbajitvā ubho mayaṃ 
 Bhāvevo appamaññāyo brahmalokaṃ aggambhase 
  
     Tato cuto mahātitthe sujāto pipphalāyano 
 Mātā sumanadeviti kosiyagotto dijo pitā 
  
   Temayitvā   syā the a   Vaṭṭini   machasaṃ the a   hapayiṃ   machasaṃ   Pujanatthaṃ 
   machasaṃ   Adāsiṃ   machasaṃ   Vāsayitvāna   syā       Pattacivare   the a   Tadā 
 rājā   machasaṃ tato cuto   simu 
  
                   
     Ahaṃ maddajanapade sāgalāya puruttame 
 Kapilassa dijassāsiṃ dhītā mātā sucimati 
  
     Ghanakañcanabambena nimmiṇitvāna maṃ pitā 
 Adā kassapadhirassa kāmāsāvajjitassa   maṃ 
  
     Kadāci so kāruṇiko gantvā kammantapekkhanaṃ   
 Kākādikehi khajjante pāṇe disvāna saṃviji 
  
     Ghare cāhaṃ tile jāte disvānāpatāpane 
 Kimi kākehi khajjante saṃvegamalabhiṃ tadā 
  
     Tadā so pabbaji dhīro ahaṃ tamanupabbajiṃ 
 Pañca vassāni nivasiṃ paribbājavate   ahaṃ 
  
     Yadā pabbajitā āsi gotami jinaposikā 
 Tadāhaṃ tamupāgantvā buddhena anusāsitā 
  
     Na cireneva kālena arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Aho kalaṇāṇamittattaṃ kassapassa sirimato 
  
     Suto buddhassa dāyado kassapo susamāhito 
 Pubbanivasāṃ yo vedi saggāpāyañca passati 
                   
     Atho jātikkhayaṃ patto abhiññāvosito muni 
 Etāhi tihi vijjahi tevijjo hoti brāhmaṇo 
  
     Tatheva bhaddā kāpilāni tevijjā maccubhāyini 
 Dhāreti antimaṃ dehaṃ jetvā māraṃ savāhiniṃ 
  
     Disvā ādinavaṃ loke ubho pabbajitā mayaṃ 
 Tyambhā khiṇāsavā dantā sitibhūtāmha nibbutā 
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa   santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
     Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddākāpilāni bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bhaddākāpilāni theriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
   Kāmehi   vajjitassa   machasaṃ syā the a   Pekkhako   machasaṃ syā       
 Paribbājapathe   syā     
  
                   
    Yasodharāpadānaṃ 
     Ekasmiṃ samaye ramma iddhe rājagahe pure 
 Pabbhārambhi varekasmiṃ vasante naranāyake 
  
     Vasantiyā tamhi nagare ramme bhikkhunupassaye 
 Yasodharā bhikkhunīyā evaṃ āsi vitakkitaṃ  
  
      Nando rāhulabhaddo ca sāvakaggā tatheva ca 
 Suddhodano mahārājā gotami ca pajāpati 
  
     Abhiññātā ca mahātherā theriyo ca mahiddhikā 
 Sattiṃ gatāva āsuṃ te dipacciva nirāsavā 
  
     Lokanāthe dharanteva ahampi ca sivaṃ padaṃ 
 Gamissāmi ti cintetvā passanti āyumattano 
     Passitvā āyusaṅkhāraṃ tadaheva khayaṃ gataṃ 
 Pattacivaramādāya nikkhamitvā sakassamā 
     Purakkhatā bhikkhunīhi satehi sahassehi sā   
 Mahiddhikā mahāpaññā sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkami 
  
     Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā satthuno cakkalakkhino 
 Nisinnā ekamantamhi idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Aṭṭhasattativassāhaṃ pacchimo vattate vayo   
 Pabbhāraṃ hi   anupapattā ārocemi mahāmune 
  
     Paripakko vayo mayhaṃ pararittaṃ mama jīvitaṃ 
 Pahāya vo gamissāmi kataṃ me saraṇamatta 
  
     Vayaṃ hi   pacchime kāle maraṇaṃ uparundhati   
 Ajja rattiṃ mahāvīra pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ 
  
   Satehi saha pañcahi   simu       Masasāmahi   simu   Pacchimā vattati vayā   syā   
 Pabbhāramahi   machasaṃ   Vayamhi   machasaṃ   Uparuddhati   machasaṃ uparujjhati   
 pujā 
  
                   
     Natthi jāti jarā vyādhi maraṇañca yahiṃ mune   
 Tattha gacchāmahaṃ vīra gato yattha na dissati   
  
     Yāvatā parisā ettha   samupāsanti satthuno 
 Aparādhaṃ pajānanti   khamantaṃ sammukhā mune 
                   
     Saṃsaritvā ca saṃsāre khalitaṃ ce mamaṃ tayi 
 Ārocemi mahāvīra aparādhaṃ khamassu me 
  
     Sutvāna tassā vacanaṃ munindo idamabravi 
 Kimuttaraṃ te cakkhāmi nibbānāya vajantiyā 
  
     Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassehi mama sāsanakārike 
 Parisānañca sabbāsaṃ kaṅkhaṃ chindassu sāne 
  
     Sutvā taṃ munino vācaṃ bhikkhunī sā yasodharā 
 Vanditvā munirājaṃ taṃ idaṃ vacanamabravi 
  
      Yasodharā ahaṃ vīra agāre te pajāpati 
 Sākiyambhi kule jātā itthiyaṅge patiṭṭhitā 
  
     Thinaṃ satahasassānaṃ navutinaṃ chaḷuttari   
 Agāre te ahaṃ vīra pāmokkhā sabbaisasarā 
  
     Rūpācāraguṇupetā yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā 
 Sabbā maṃ apacāyanti devatā viya mānusā 
     Kaññāsahassappamuṇā sakyaputtanivesane 
 Samānasukhadukkhā tā devatā viya nandane 
  
     Kāmadhātumatikkantā  saṇṭhitā rūpadhātuyā 
 Rūpena sadisā natthi ṭhapetvā lokanāyakaṃ  
  
     Evamādini vatvāna uppatitvāna ambaraṃ 
 Iddhi anekā dasessi buddhānuññā yasodharā   
  
   Mahāmune   machasaṃ   Ajarāmaṃ santipuraṃ gamissāmi asaṅkhataṃ   simu 
 ajarāmaṃpuraṃ   machasaṃ   Nāma   simu machasaṃ   Sace metthi   simu 
 aparādhamajānanti   machasaṃ   Chaduttari   machasaṃ   Kāmādhātumatikkamma   
 machasaṃ   machasaṃ   phasā gāthā na disasate apica ayaṃ gāthā dissate  sambuddhaṃ 
 abhivādetvā iddhiṃ dasessi satthuno nekā nānāvidhākārā mahāiddhipi dassayi  
  
                   
     Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ sīsaṃ uttarato kuru 
 Ubho pakkhā duve dipā jambudipo   sarirato 
  
     Dakkhiṇañca saraṃ piñajaṃ nānāsākhā tu pattakā 
 Cando ca suriyo akkhi   merupabbatato sikhā   
  
     Cakkavāḷagiri   tuṇḍaṃ   jamburukkhaṃ samulakaṃ 
 Vijamānā upāgantvā vandate lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Hatthivaṇaṇaṃ tathevassaṃ pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā 
 Vandimaṃ suriyaṃ meruṃ   sakkavaṇaṇañca dassayi 
                   
      Yasodharā ahaṃ cira pāde vandāmi cakkhuma  
 Sahassaṃ lokadhātunaṃ phullapadmena   chādayi 
  
     Brahmavaṇaṇañca māpetvā dhammaṃ desesi suññataṃ 
  Yasodharā ahaṃ cira pade vandāmi cakkhuma 
  
     Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
     Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbesavā parikkhiṇā nanthidāni punabbhavo 
  
     Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mayhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
     Buddhānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ te   sudassitaṃ   
 Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
     Yaṃ mayhaṃ purimaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarase mune 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā 
  
     Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā vārayitvā anācaraṃ 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra sañcattaṃ jīvitaṃ mayā 
  
   Jamabudipā   sabbesuṃ   Vandañca suriyañcakkhi   machasaṃ si syā 
 candasuriyavisālakkhi   pujā   Sikhaṃ   machasaṃ pujā   Giriṃ   machasaṃ   Tuṇḍā   pujā 
   Vandasuriyamahaṃmeruṃ   pujā   Thullapādena   pujā   Saṅgamanetasu   sima   
 Nidassitā   machasaṃ 
  
                   
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhariyathoyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ   upakārāyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhojanatthāyadāsi maṃ 
 Na tattha vimanā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmuni 
  
     Nekakoṭisahassāni jīvitāni pariccachiṃ 
 Bhayamokkhaṃ karissaṃ ti cajāmi   mama jīvitaṃ 
  
     Aṅgagate alaṅkāre vatthe nānāvidhe bahu itthimaṇḍe na guhāmi tuyhattāya 
 mahāmuni 
                   
     Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ gāmāna nagamāni ca 
 Khetatā   puttā ca dhītā ca pariccattā mahumune 
  
     Hatthi assā gavā cāpi dāsiyo paricārikā 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra pariccattā asaṅkhiyā 
  
     Yaṃ mayhaṃ paṭimantesi   dānaṃ dassāmi yācake 
 Vimanaṃ me na passāmi dadato dānamuttamaṃ 
  
     Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsāre ca bahubbidhe 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyā 
  
     Sukhappattā na modāmi na ca dukkhesu dummanā 
 Sabbattha tulitā homi tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
     Anumaggena sambuddho yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinihari 
 Anubhutvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ patto bodhiṃ mahāmuni 
  
     Buhmadevañca sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamā te bahu mayā 
  
   Sahasasāni   machasaṃ pujā   Dadāmi   machasaṃ   Khettaṃ   machasaṃ   Patimattesi 
   simu 
  
                   
     Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
 Gavesato buddhadhamme ahaṃ te paricārikā 
                   
      Kappe satasahasse ca caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Paccantadesaviseye nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Tassa āgamana ṃmaggaṃ sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā 
  
      Tena kālena so āsi sumedho nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Maggañca paṭiyādesi āyato   sabbadassino 
  
      Tena kālenahaṃ āsiṃ kaññā brāhmaṇasambhavā 
 Sumittā nāma nāmena upagañachiṃ samāgamaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭha uppalahatthāni pujanatthāya satthuno 
 Ādāya janasammejjha   addasaṃ isimugagataṃ 
                   
      Cirānupari āsinaṃ   atikantaṃ manoharaṃ 
 Disvā tadā amaññissaṃ  saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama  
  
      Parakkamaṃ taṃ saphalaṃ addasaṃ isino tadā 
 Pubbakammena sambuddhe vittañcāpi pasidi me 
  
      Bhiyyo cittaṃ pasādesiṃ ise uggatamānase   
 Deyyaṃ aññaṃ na passāmi demi pupphāni te ise 
  
      Pañca hatthā tava hontu tayo hontu mamaṃ ise 
 Tena siddhi   samā hotu   bodhatthāya tavaṃ ise 
   Bhāṇavāraṃ catutthaṃ   
  
      Isi gahetvā pupphāni āgacchantaṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Pujesi janasammajjhe   bodhatthāya mahāisiṃ   
  
      Passitvā janasammajjhe dipaṅkaro mahāmuni 
 Viyākāsi mahāvīro isiṃ uggatamānasaṃ   
  
   Āyataṃ   simu   Janatāmajjhe   simu   Virānugataṃ dayitaṃ   machasaṃ syā   
 Isimahuggatamānase   simu   Saddhiṃ   machasaṃ syā   Hontu   machasaṃ   Janatāmajjhe 
   simu   Mahāisi   simu machasaṃ   imissānantaraṃ simu machasaṃ potthakesu ayaṃ 
 gāthā dissate na tu pujāvaliyaṃ  aparimeyye ito kappe dipaṅkaro mahāmuni mama 
 kammaṃ viyākāsi ujubhāvaṃ mahāmuni  
  
                   
      Samacittā samakammā samakāri bhavisasti 
 Piyā hessati kammenana tuyhatthāya mahāise   
  
      Sudassanā suppiyā   ca manāpā piyavādini 
 Tassa dhammesu dāyadā piyā hessati   itthikā 
  
      Yathāpi bhaṇḍasāmuggaṃ anurakkhanti   sāmino 
 Evaṃ kusaladhammānaṃ anurakkhissate ayaṃ 
  
      Tassa te   anukampanti purayissati pārami 
 Sihova pañajaraṃ hetvā   pāpuṇissati bodhiyaṃ 
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ maṃ buddho viyākari 
 Taṃ vācaṃ anumodanti evaṃkāri bhaviṃ ahaṃ 
                   
      Tassa kammassa sukatassa tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Devamānusakaṃ yoniṃ upapajja   asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ devesu mānusesu ca 
 Pacchime bhave sampatte ajāyiṃ sākiye kule 
  
      Rūpavati bhogavati yasasilavati tathā 
 Sabbaṅgasampadā homi kusalesu atisakkatā 
  
      Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakakāraṃ lokadhammasamāgamaṃ 
 Cittañca dukkhitaṃ natthi vasāmi akutobhayā 
  
      Nibbinditvāna saṃsāre pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Sahassaparivārena pabbajitvā akiñcanā 
  
      Agāraṃ vijahitvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Addhamāse asampatte catusaccaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahu teke sāgarasseva ūmiyo 
  
   Mahāisi   simu   Supiyā   machasaṃ   Viharissati   machasaṃ   Anurakkhati   machasaṃ 
   Maṃ   syā   Hitvā   si syā hetvā         Anubhotvā  simu machasaṃ 
  
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhā 
 Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampattā labhāmi sabbasampadā 
  
      Sā dadāti sakattānaṃ puññatthāya mahesino 
 Sahāyasampadā honti nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ 
  
      Parikkhiṇaṃ atitaṃ ca pacacuppannaṃ anāgataṃ 
 Sabbaṃ kammaṃ mamaṃ khiṇaṃ pāde vandāmi cakkhumaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sayodharātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
                   
      Dasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ 
      Kappe ca satasahasse caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dīpaṅkaro nāma jino uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro viyākāsi vināyako 
 Sumedhaṃ ca sumittaṃ ca samānasukhadukkhaṃ 
  
      Sadevakaṃ ca passantā civarantā sadevakaṃ 
 Tesaṃ pakittane amhe upagamma samāgamamaṃ   
  
      Amhaṃ sabbapati hohi   anāgatasamāgame 
 Sabbāva tuyahaṃ bhariyā manāpā piyavādikā 
  
      Dānasilamayaṃ sabbaṃ bhāvanā ca subhāvitā   
 Dīgharattaṃ ca no   sabbaṃ pariccatataṃ mahāmune 
  
   Sadevake   simu   Sabbā patibhonti         Bhāvanaṃ ca subhāvitaṃ         Mayaṃ 
       
  
                   
      Gandhaṃ vilepanaṃ mālaṃ dipaṃ ca ratanāmayaṃ 
 Yaṃ kiñci patthitaṃ sabbaṃ pariccattaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Aññaṃ cāpi kataṃ kammaṃ paribhogaṃ ca mānusaṃ 
 Dīgharattaṃ hi no sabbaṃ pariccattaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Anekajātisaṃsāraṃ bahuṃ puññaṃ hi no kataṃ 
 Issaramanubhotvāna saṃsaritvā bhavābhave 
  
      Pacchimahave sampatte sakyaputtanivesane 
 Nānākuluppanānāyo accharākāmavaṇaṇini 
  
      Lābhaggena yasaṃ pattā pujitā sabbasakkatā 
 Bābhiyo annapānānaṃ sadā sammānitā mayaṃ 
  
      Agāraṃ pajahitvāna pabbajitvāgāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte sabbā pattāmaha nibbutiṃ 
  
      Lābhiyo annapānānaṃ vatthasenāsanāni ca 
 Upenti paccayā sabbe sadā sakkatapujitā 
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni dasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā 
 gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dasahibhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
                   
        Aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ 
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni bhikkhunī sakyasambhavā 
 Yasodharāpamukhāti sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamuṃ 
  
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni sabbā honti mahiddhikā 
 Vandanti munino pāde ārocenti yathābalaṃ 
  
      Jāti khiṇā jarā vyādhi maranaṃ ca mahāmuni 
 Anāsavaṃ padaṃ santaṃ amataṃ yāma nāyaka 
  
      Khalitaṃ ce pure atthi sabbāsampi mahāmuni 
 Aparādhamajānanti   khama amhaṃ vināyaka 
  
       Iddhiṃ cāpi nidassetha mama sāsanakārikā 
 Parisānaṃ ca sabbāsaṃ kaṅkhaṃ chindatha yācatā  
  
      Yasodhari mahāvīra manāpā piyadassanā 
 Sabbā tuyhaṃ mahāvīra agārasmiṃ pajāpati 
  
      Thinaṃ satasahassānaṃ navutina chaḷuttari 
 Agāre te mayaṃ vīra pāmokkhā sabbaissarā 
  
      Rūpācāraguṇupetā yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā 
 Sabbāyo apacāyanti devatā viya mānusā 
  
      Aṭṭhārasasahassāni sabbā sākiyasambhavā 
 Yasodarā   sahassāni pāmokkhā issarā tadā 
                   
      Kāmadhātumatikkanattā saṇṭhitā rūpadhatuyā 
 Rūpena sadisā natthi sahassānaṃ 
      Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā iddhiṃ dassesu satthuno 
 Nekā   nānāvidhākārā mahāiddhipi dassayuṃ 
  
      Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ sisaṃ uttarato kuru 
 Ubho pakkhā duve dipā jambudipaṃ sarirato 
      Dakkhiṇaṃ ca saraṃ piñajaṃ nānāsākhā tu pattakā 
 Candasuravisālakkhā   merupabbatato sikhā 
  
   Aparādhaṃ pajānanti         Yasovati   si       Loke   simu   Candaṃ ca suriyaṃ 
 vakkhi   machasaṃ     
  
                   
      Cakkavāḷagirituṇḍā jamburukkhaṃ samulakaṃ 
 Vijamānā upagantvā vandanti lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Hatthivaṇṇaṃ tathevassaṃ pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā 
 Canda ca suriyaṃ meruṃ sakkavaṇṇaṃ ca dassayuṃ 
  
      Yasodharā mayaṃ vīra pāde candāma cakkhuma 
 Tava vīra pabhāvane nipphantā naranāyaka 
  
      Buddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetoparāyañāṇassa vasi homa mahāmune 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāma dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sababāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava sattike 
  
      Subbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ 
 Adhikārā bahu ambhaṃ tumhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Yaṃ amhaṃ purimaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarase mune 
 Tumhatthāya mahāvīra puññānupacitāni no 
  
      Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā vārayimaha anācaraṃ 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra cattāni jīvitāni no 
                   
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhariyatthāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ upakārāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthā mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassānaṃ bhojanatthāyadāsi no 
 Na tattha vimanā homa tuyhatthā mahāmune 
  
      Nekakoṭisahassāni jīvitāni vajimbha no 
 Bhayamokkhaṃ karissāma jīvitāni cajimha se 
  
      Aṅgagate alaṅkāre vatthe nānāvidhe bahu 
 Itthibhaṇḍe na guhāma tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
                   
      Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ gāmāni nigamāni ca 
 Khettā puttā ca dhītā ca pariccattā   mahāmune 
  
      Hatthi assā gavā cāpi   dāsiyo paricārikā 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra pariccatatā asaṅkhiyā   
  
      Yaṃ amhe paṭimantesi dānaṃ dassāma yācake 
 Vimanaṃ no na passāma dadato dānamuttamaṃ 
  
      Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ dukkhaṃ saṃsāre ca bahubadhe 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Sukhappattā na modāma   na ca dukkhesu dummanā 
 Sabbattha tulitā homa tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Anumaggena sambuddho yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinihari 
 Anubhutvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ patto bodhiṃ mahāmuni 
  
      Brahmadevaṃ ca sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamā tehi no bahu 
  
      Adhikārā bahu amhaṃ   tuyhatthā mahāmune 
 Gavesato buddhadhamme mayaṃ te paricārikā 
  
      Kappe ca sahatahasse caturo ca asaṅkhiye 
 Dipaṅkaro mahāvīro uppajji lokanāyako 
  
      Paccantadesavisaye nimantetvā tathāgataṃ 
 Tassa āgamanaṃ maggaṃ sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā 
  
      Tena kālena so āsi sumodho nāma brāhmaṇo 
 Maggeṃ ca paṭiyādesi āyataṃ   sabbadasisano 
                   
      Tena kālena āsimbha sabbā brāhmaṇasambhavā 
 Thaludajāni pupphāni āharimbha samāgamaṃ 
  
      Tasmiṃ so samaye buddho dipaṅkaro mahāyaso 
 Viyākāsi mahāvaro isimuggatamānasaṃ 
  
   Khettaṃ putataṃ ca dhitaṃ ca pariccattaṃ         Hatthiassaṃgavaṃ cāpi         
 Pariccattaṃ asaṃkhiyaṃ         Numodāma   machasaṃ   Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ ameha      
    Āyato   machasaṃ     
  
                   
      Calati racati paṭhavi saṅkampati sadevakaṃ 
 Tassa kammaṃ pakittente isinuggatamānaso   
  
      Devakaññā manussā ca mayaṃ cāpi sadevakā 
 Nānāpujaniyaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ pujayitvāna patthayuṃ 
  
      Tesaṃ buddho viyākāsi jotidipasanāmako 
  Ajja ye patthitā atthi te bhavissanti sammukhā  
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ no buddho viyākari 
 Taṃ vācamanumodanti evaṅkāri ahumha no 
  
      Tassa kammassa sukatassa tattha cittaṃ pasādiya   
 Devamānusakaṃ yoni anubhotvā asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
      Sukhadukkhenubhotvāna devesu mānusesu ca 
 Pacchimabhave sampatte jātāmbha sākiye kule 
  
      Rūpati bhogavati yasasilavati tato 
 Sabbaṅgasampadā homa kulesu atisakkatā 
  
      Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakkāraṃ lokadhammasamāgamaṃ 
 Cittaṃ ca dukkhitaṃ natthi vasāma akutobhayā 
  
      Vuttaṃ hetaṃ bhagavatā rañño antepare tadā 
 Khattiyānaṃ pure viro upakāraṃ ca niddasi 
  
      Upakārā ca yā nāri yā ca nāri sukhe dukhe 
 Atthakkhāyi ca yā nāri yā ca nārinukampikā 
                   
      Dhammaṃ care sucaritaṃ na naṃ duccaritaṃ care 
 Dhammacāri sukhaṃ seti asmiṃ loke parambhi ca 
  
      Agāraṃ vijahitvāna pabbajimbhanagāriyaṃ 
 Aḍḍhamāse asampatte catusaccaṃ phusimbha no 
  
      Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahuṃ ambhe sāgarasseva ūmiyo 
  
   Isimuggata mānasaṃ   machasaṃ       Pasādayuṃ   simu 
  
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ sampatti ca bahubbidhā 
 Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampannā labhāma sabbasampadā 
  
      Yā dadanti sakattānaṃ puññatthāya mahesino 
 Sahāyasampadā honti nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ 
  
      Parikkhiṇaṃ atitaṃ ca pacacuppannaṃ anāgataṃ 
 Sabbaṃ kammampi no khiṇaṃ pāde candāma cakkhuma 
  
      Nibbānāya vajantinaṃ kiṃ vo cakkhāma uttariṃ 
 Santasaṅkhatadosaṃ hi pappotha amataṃ padaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā 
 gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Yasodharāpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikukhunisahassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
 Kuṇḍalakesivaggo tatiyo 
  
 Tatthuddānaṃ 
 Kuṇḍalā gotami ceva dhammadinnā ca sakulā 
 Caranandā soṇā ca kāpilāni yasodharā 
 Dasasahassabhikkhunī aṭṭhārasasahassakā 
 Gāthāsatāni cattāri cha ca sattani meva ca 
                   
                   
       Yasavatipamukhabhikkhunīnaṃ apadānaṃ 
      Bhavā sabbe parikkhiṇā bhavasandhi vimocitā 
 Sabbāsavā ca no natthi ārocema mahāmune 
  
      Purimaṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ yaṃ kiñci sādhu patthitaṃ 
 Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Buddhapaccekabuddhānaṃ buddhānaṃ sāvakānana ca 
 Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ tuyahatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Uccanicamayaṃ kammaṃ bhikkhunaṃ sādhu patthitaṃ 
 Uccākulaparikamamaṃ katametaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Teneva sukkamūlena coditā kammasampadā 
 Mānusikamatikkantā jāyiṃsu khattiye kule 
  
      Uppatte ca kate kamme jātiyā cāpi ekato 
 Paccime ekato jātā khattiyā kulasambhavā 
  
      Rūpavati bhogavati lābhasakkārapujitā 
 Antepure māvira devānaṃ viya nandane 
  
      Nibbinditvā agārambhā pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ 
 Katipāhaṃ upādāya sababā pattāmha nibbuti 
  
      Civaraṃ paṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanenti bahu ambe sadā sakkatapujitā 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasavatipamukhāni aṭṭhāsakhattiyakaññā bhikkhunīssāni bhagavato 
 sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Yasavatipumukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahasāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
                   
                   
       Brahmaṇakaññābhikkhunīnaṃ apadānaṃ 
      Cullāsitisahassāni brahmaññakulasambhavā 
 Sukhumālahatthapādā pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune 
      Vessasuddakule jātā devā nāgā ca kintarā 
 Cātuddipā bahu kaññā pure tuyahaṃ mahāmune 
  
      Keci pabbajitā atthi saccadassāvino bahu 
 Devā ca kintarā nāgā khujjhissanti anāgate 
  
      Anubhotvā yasaṃ sabbaṃ satvāna sabbasampadā 
 Tvasi pasādaṃ paṭiladdhā bujjhissanti anāgate 
  
      Ambhe brāhmaṇadhitā tu brahmaññakulasambhavā 
 Pekkhato no mahāvīra pāde vandama cakkhuma 
  
      Upahatā bhavā sabbe mulataṇhā samuhatā 
 Samucchinnā anusayā puññasaṅkhārā dālitā 
  
      Samādhigocarā sabbā samāpattivasi tathā 
 Jhānena dhammaratiyā viharissāma no sadā 
  
      Bhavanetti avijjā ca saṅkhārāpi ca khepitā 
 Sududdasaṃ padaṃ gantuṃ anujānātha nāyaka 
  
      Upakārā mamaṃ tumbhe digharattaṃ katāvino 
 Bahuttaṃ saṃsayaṃ chetvā sabbā gacchantu   nibbutiṃ 
  
      Vanditvā munino pāde katvā iddhivikubbaṇaṃ 
 Kāci dassenti ālokaṃ andhakāramathāparā 
  
      Dassenti candasuriye sāgaraṃ ca samacchakaṃ 
 Sineruparibhaṇḍaṃ ca dassenti pārichattakaṃ 
  
   Gacchata       
  
                   
      Tāvatiṃsaṃ ca bhavanaṃ yāmaṃ dassenti iddhiyā 
 Tusitaṃ nimmite deve vasavatti mahissare 
      Buhmāno kāci dassenti caṅkamaṃ ca mahārahaṃ 
 Brahmavaṇṇaṃ ca māpetvā dhammaṃ desenti suññataṃ 
  
      Nānāvikubbaṇaṃ katvā iddhiṃ dasasiya patthuno 
 Dassāyiṃsu khalaṃ sabbā pade vandiṃsu satthuno 
                   
      Iddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homa mahāmune 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homa dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā nathidoni punabbhavo 
      Atthadhamamaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ ambhaṃ mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Pubbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ 
 Adhikārā bahu ambhaṃ tuyhatthāya mahāmune 
  
      Yaṃ ambhehi kataṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarataṃ mune 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra puññānupacitāni no 
  
      Yaṃ ambhehi kataṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarataṃ mune 
 Puraṃ haṃsavati nāma sambuddhassa kulāsayaṃ 
  
      Dvārena haṃsavatiyā gaṅgā sandati sababadā 
 Ubbāḷha nadiyā bhikkhu gamanaṃ na labhantite 
  
      Divasaṃ dve tayo ceva sattāhaṃ māsakaṃ tato 
 Catumāsampi sampuṇṇaṃ gamanaṃ na labhanti te 
  
      Tadā ahu sattasāro jaṭilo nāma jaṭṭhiko 
 Oruddhe bhikkhavo disvā setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayī 
  
      Tadā satasahassehi setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayi 
 Saṅghassa orime tīre vihāraṃ ca akārayi 
  
                   
      Itthiyo purisā ceva uccanicakulāni ca 
 Tassa secuvihāre ca   samabhāgaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
      Ambhe aññe ca manujā vippasanenna cetasā 
 Tassa kammesu dāyādā nagare janapadesu ca 
  
      Itthi purisā kumārā ca bahu ceva kumārikā 
 Setuno ca vihārassa vālukā ākiriṃsu te 
                   
      Vithisammajjanaṃ katvā kadali puṇaṇaghaṭe dhaje   
 Dhupaṃ cuṇaṇaṇaṃ ca   mālaṃ ca kāraṃ katvāna satthuno 
  
      Setuvihāre kāretvā nimantetvā vināyakaṃ 
 Mahādānaṃ daditvāna sambodhiṃ abhipatthayi 
  
      Padumuttaro mahāvīro tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ 
 Anumadeniyaṃkāsi jaṭilassa mahāmuni 
  
       Satahasasse atikkante kappo hessati bhaddako 
 Bhavābhavenubhotvāna pupāṇissati bodhiyaṃ 
  
      Ye keci hatthaparikammaṃ katāvi naranāriyo 
 Anāgatasmiṃ addhāne sabbā hessanti sammukhā 
  
      Tena kammavipākena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Upapannā devabhavanaṃ tuyhaṃ tā paricārikā 
  
      Dibbaṃ sukhaṃ asaṅkheyyaṃ mānusaṃ ca asaṅkhyayaṃ 
 Anubhonti ciraṃ kālaṃ saṃsarimbha bhavābhave 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ 
 Sukhumāli manussesu atho devapure vare 
  
      Rūpabhogayase ceva atho kittiṃ ca sakkataṃ 
 Labhāma satataṃ sabbaṃ sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ 
  
      Pacchime bhave sampatte jātāmha brāhmaṇe kule 
 Sudhumālahatthapādā sakyaputtanivesane 
  
   Tesu setuvihāresu   simu   Suṇaṇakuṭadadhajā       puṇaṇaghaṭā dhajā   machasaṃ 
   Dhumavuṇaṇañca       
  
                   
      Sabbakālampi paṭhaviṃ na pasasāmanalaṅkataṃ 
 Vikkhallabhumimasuciṃ na passāma mahāmune   
                   
      Agāraṃ vasante ambhe sakkāraṃ sabbakālikaṃ 
 Upanenati tadā sabbaṃ pubbakammabalena no 
  
      Agāraṃ pajahitvāna pabbajitvānagāriyaṃ 
 Saṃsārapathanittiṇaṇā vitarāgā bhavāmase 
  
      Civaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Upanetti sadā ambhe sahassāni tato tato 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ caturāsitibrāhmaṇakaññābhikkhunīssānisahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā 
 gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Caturāsitibhikkhunīsahasāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
       Uppaladāyikāpadānaṃ 
      Nagare aruṇavatiyā aruṇo nāma khattiyo 
 Tassa rañño ahaṃ bhariyā ekajjhaṃ cārayāmahaṃ 
  
      Rahogatā nisīditvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
 Ādāya gamaniyaṃ hi kusalaṃ natthi me kataṃ 
  
      Mahāsitāpa kaṭukaṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇaṃ 
 Nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi ettha me natthi saṃsayo 
  
      Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna pahaṃsatvona mānasaṃ 
 Rājānaṃ upagantvāna idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
                   
       Itthi nāma mayaṃ deva purisānugatā sadā 
 Ekaṃ me samaṇaṃ dehi bhojayissāmi khattiya  
  
      Adāsi me tadā rājā samaṇaṃ bhāvitinduyaṃ 
 Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna paramantena purayiṃ 
                   
      Puretvā paramaṃ annaṃ sahassagghanakenahaṃ   
 Mahācelena chādetvā adāsiṃ tuṭṭhamānasā 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
      Sahassaṃ devarājunaṃ   mahesittamakārayiṃ 
 Sahassaṃ cakkavattinaṃ mahesittamakārayiṃ 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
 Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ aññaṃ tassa kammaphalaṃ tato 
  
      Uppalasseva me vaṇeṇā abhirūpā sudassanā 
 Itthi sabbaṅgasampannā abhijātā jutindharā 
  
      Pacchimbhave sampatte ajāyiṃ sākiye kule 
 Nārisahassapāmokkhā suddhodanasutassahaṃ 
  
      Nibbanditvā agārehaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Sattamiṃ rattimappatvā catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātaṃ ca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Parimetuṃ na sakkomi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ mayhaṃ purimaṃ kammaṃ kusalaṃ sarase muti 
 Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra pariccattaṃ bahuṃ mayā 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Dve gatiyo pajānāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ucce kule pajāyāmi mahāsāle mahaddhane 
 Aññe kule na jānāmi piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ 
   Sahagandhalepanaṃ   simu   Sahasayadevarājunaṃ   simu 
  
                   
      Bhavābhave saṃsaritvā sukkamūlena coditā 
 Amanāpaṃ na passāmi somanassakataṃ phalaṃ   
                   
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ uppaladāyikā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Uppaladāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
     Sigālamātāpadānaṃ      Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammānapāragu 
 Ito satasahassamhi kappe upapajji nāyako 
  
      Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ jātāmaccakule ahaṃ 
 Nānāratanapajjote iddhe phīte maddhane 
  
      Pitunā saha gantvāna mahājanapurakkhatā 
 Dhammaṃ buddhassa sutvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ 
 Vaciduccaritaṃ hitvā ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ 
  
      Buddhe pasannā dhamme ca saṅghe ca tibbagāravā 
 Saddhammasavane yuttā buddhadassanalālasā 
  
      Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ assosiṃ bhikkhunīṃ tadā 
 Taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayitvāna tisso sikkhā apūrayiṃ 
 Tato maṃ sugato āha karuṇānugatāsayo 
  
   Somanassakatāphalaṃ   simu 
                   
                   
       Yassa saddhā tathāgate acalā suppatiṭṭhitā 
 Sīlaṃ ca yassa kalyāṇaṃ ariyakantaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ 
  
      Saṅghe pasāde yassatthi ujubhūtaṃ ca dassanaṃ 
 Adaḷiddoti taṃ āhu amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ 
  
      Tasmā saddhaṃ ca sīlaṃ ca pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ 
 Anuyuñejatha medhāvi saraṃ buddhānasāsanaṃ  
  
      Taṃ sutvāhaṃ pamuditā apucchiṃ paṇidhiṃ mama 
 Tadā anomo amito vyākarittha vināyako 
  
      Buddhe pasannā kalyāṇi lacchase taṃ supatthitaṃ 
 Satasahasse ito kappe okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā 
 Sigālakassa mātā ti hessati satthu sivikā 
  
      Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ 
 Mettacittā paricariṃ paṭipattihi nāyakaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni giribbajapuruttame 
 Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte mahāratanasañcaye 
  
      Putto sigāleko nāma mamāsi vipatho rato 
 Diṭṭhigahanapakkhanto   disāpujanatapparo 
  
      Nānādisā namassantaṃ piṇḍāya nagaraṃ vajaṃ 
 Taṃ disvā ovadi buddho magge ṭhatvā vināyako 
  
      Tassa desayato dhammaṃ ninādo   vimbhayo ahu 
 Devakoṭinaranārinaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu 
  
      Tadāhaṃ   parisaṃ gantvā sutvā sugatabhāsitaṃ 
 Sotāpattiphalaṃ pattā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
   Diṭṭhigahaṇapakkhanto   simu   Panādo   simu   Tadā taṃ       
                   
                   
      Na cireneva kālena buddhadassanalālasā 
 Anussatiṃ taṃ bhāvetvā arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Dassanatthāya buddhassa sabbadāva vajāmahaṃ 
 Atittāyeva passāmi rūpaṃ nayananandanaṃ 
  
      Sabbapāramisambhutaṃ lakkhinilayanaṃ varaṃ 
 Rūpaṃ sabbasubhākiṇaṇaṃ atittā viharāmahaṃ 
  
      Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  Sigālakassa yā mātā aggā saddhādhimuttikā  
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sigālamātā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sigālamātātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
     Sukakāpadānaṃ 
      Ekanavute ito kappe vipassī nāma nāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano   sabbadhammavipassako 
  
      Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ jātā aññatare kule 
 Dhammaṃ sutvāna munino pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Bahussutā dhammadharā paṭibhānavati tathā 
 Vicittakathikā cāpi jinasāsanakārikā 
  
   Cārudassayo   machasaṃ 
                   
                   
      Tadā dhammakathaṃ katvā janatāya hitaṃ bahuṃ 
 Tato cutāhaṃ tusitaṃ upapannā yasassiti 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe sikhi viya sikhi jino 
 Tapanto yasasā loke uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
      Tadāpi pabbajitvāna buddhasāsanakovidā 
 Jotetvā jinavākyāni tatopi tidivaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe vessabhu nāma nāyako 
 Uppajjitvā mahāñāṇi tadāpi ca tathevahaṃ 
  
      Pabbajitvā dhammadharā jotayiṃ jinasāsanaṃ 
 Gantvā marupuraṃ rammaṃ anubhosiṃ mahāsukhaṃ 
  
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe kakusandho jinuttamo 
 Uppajji narasaddulo   tadāpi ca tathevahaṃ 
  
      Pabbajitvā munimataṃ jotayitvā yathāyukaṃ 
 Tato cutāhaṃ tidivaṃ agaṃ sahavanaṃ yathā 
  
      Imasmiṃ yeva kappamhi koṇāgamana nāyako 
 Uppajji lokasaraṇo sabbasattanamuttamo 
  
      Tadāpi pabbajitvāna sāsane tassa tādino 
 Bahusasutā dhamamadharā jotayiṃ jinasāsanaṃ 
  
      Imasamiṃyeva kappamhi kassapo purisuttamo 
 Uppajji lokanayano araṇo maraṇanatagu   
  
      Tassāpi naravirassa pabbajitvāna sāsane 
 Pariyāputasaddhammā paripucchāvisāradā 
  
      Susilā lajjiti ceva tisu sikkhāsu kovidā 
 Bahuṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā yāvajīvaṃ hitāvahaṃ   
                   
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
   Varasaddulo         Araṇo amataṃgate   simu   Mahāmune   simu 
  
                   
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni giribbajapuruttame 
 Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte mahāratanasañcaye 
  
      Yadā bhikkhusahassena parito lokanāyako 
 Upāgami rājagahaṃ sahassakkhena vaṇaṇito 
  
       Danto dantehi saha purāṇajaṭilehi vippamutto 
 Siṅgitikkhasamaṇeṇā rajāgahaṃ pāvisi bhagavā  
  
      Disvā buddhānubhāvaṃ taṃ sutvā ca guṇasañcayaṃ 
 Buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā pujayiṃ taṃ yathābalaṃ 
  
      Aparena ca kālena dhammadinnāya santike 
 Agārā nikkhamitvāna sabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Kesesu chijjamānesu kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Uggahiṃ sāsanaṃ sabbaṃ pabbajitvā cirenahaṃ 
  
      Tato dhammamadesesiṃ mahājanasamāgame 
 Dhamme desiyamānambhi dhammābhisamayo ahu 
  
      Nekapāṇasahassānaṃ taṃ viditvāticimbhito 
 Abhippasanno me yakkho hamitvāna giribbajaṃ 
  
       Kiṃ me katā rājagahe manussā madhu pitāva acchare 
 Ye sukkaṃ na upāsanti desentiṃ amataṃ padaṃ 
  
      Tañca appaṭivāniyaṃ asevanakamojavaṃ 
 Pivanti maññe sappaññā valāhakamivaddhagu  
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
                   
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ sukkā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sukkātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
                   
     Rūpanandāpadānaṃ 
      Ekanavute ito kappe vipassi nāma nāyako 
 Uppajji cārunayano sabbadhammesu cakkhumā 
  
      Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ iddhe phīte mahākule 
 Jātā surūpā dayitā pujaniyā janassa ca 
  
      Upagantvā mahāvīraṃ vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
 Dhammaṃ suṇitvā saraṇaṃ upesiṃ naranāyakaṃ 
  
      Silesu saṃvutā hutvā nibbute ca naruttame 
 Dhātuthupassa upari soṇaṇacchattaṃ apūjayiṃ 
  
      Mutatacāgā silavati yāvajīvaṃ tato cutā 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsupagatā ahaṃ 
  
      Tadā dasahi ṭhānehi adhibhotvāna sesake 
 Rūpasaddehi gandhehi rasehi phusanehi ca 
  
      Āyunāpi ca vaṇṇena sukhena yasasāpi ca 
 Tathevādhipateyyena adhigayha virocahaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātāhaṃ kapilamhaye 
 hitā khemakasakkassa nandanāmātivissutā 
  
      Abhirūpaṃ upapadaṃ ahu me kattisuvakaṃ 
 Yadāhaṃ yobbanappattā rūpalāvaññabhusitā 
                   
      Tadā mamatthaṃ   sakānaṃ vivādo sumahā ahu 
 Pabbājesi tato mā sakyā vinassisuṃti   
  
      Pabbajitvā tathāgataṃ   rūpadessiṃ naruttamaṃ 
 Sutvāna nopagacchāmi mama rūpena gabbitā 
  
      Ovādampi na gacchāmi buddhadassanabhirukā 
 Tadā jino upāyena upanetvā sasantikaṃ 
  
      Tissotthiyo nidassesi iddhiyā maggakovido 
 Accharārūpasadisaṃ taruṇiṃ jaritaṃ mataṃ 
  
   Idaṃ mamatthe   machasaṃ       Vinassuṃ iti   machasaṃ       Tathā cāhaṃ      
  
                   
      Tāyo disvā susaṃviggā cirantā se kalebare 
 Aṭṭhāsiṃ bhavanibbintā tadā maṃ āha nāyako 
       Āturaṃ asuciṃ putiṃ passa nande samussayaṃ uggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ bālānaṃ 
 abhinanditaṃ 
  
      Asubhāya cintaṃ bhāvehi ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ 
 Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ 
  
      Evametaṃ avekkhanti rattindivamananditā 
 Tato sakāya paññāya abhinibbijja vacchasi  
  
      Tassā me appamatatāya viharantyādha yoniso 
 Yathābhūtaṃ ayaṃ kāyo diṭṭho santarabāhiro 
  
      Atha nibbindahaṃ kāyo ajjhattaṃ ca virajjahaṃ 
 Appamattā visaṃyuttā upasannāmbhi nibbutā 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ rūpanandā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Rūpanandātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
     Aḍḍhakāsi apadānaṃ 
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
                   
      Tadāhaṃ pabbajitvāna tassa buddhassa sāsane 
 Saṃvutā pātimokkhasmiṃ indriyesu ca pañcasu 
  
      Mattaññuni ca asane yuttā jāgariyepi ca 
 Vasanti yutayogāhaṃ bhikkhunīṃ vigatāsavaṃ 
  
      Akkosiṃ duṭṭhavittāhaṃ  gaṇike ti ca bhaṇiṃ tadā 
 Tena pāpena kammena nirayambhi apaccisaṃ 
  
      Teneva kammasesena ajāyiṃ gaṇikākule 
 Bahusova parādhinā pacchimāya ca jātiyaṃ 
  
      Kāsisu seṭṭhikulajā brahmacariyaphalenahaṃ 
 Accharā viya devesu ahosiṃ rūpasampadā 
  
      Disvāna dassaniyaṃ maṃ giribbajapuruttame 
 Gaṇikatte nivesesuṃ akkosanaphalena me 
  
      Sāhaṃ sutvāna saddhammaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa desitaṃ 
 Pubbavāsesampannā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Tatopasampadatthāya gacchanti jinasantikaṃ 
 Magge dhutte ṭhite sutvā labhiṃ dutopasampadaṃ 
                   
      Sabbaṃ kammaṃ parikkhiṇaṃ puññaṃ pāpaṃ tatheva ca 
 Sabbasaṃsāramuttiṇṇā gaṇikattaṃ ca khepitaṃ 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ aḍḍhakāsi bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Aḍḍhakāsitheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
                   
     Puṇṇāpadānaṃ 
      Vipassito bhagavato sikhino vessabhussa ca 
 Kakusandhassa munino koṇāgamanatādino 
  
      Kassapassa ca buddhassa pabbajitvāna sāsane 
 Bhikkhunī silasampannā nipakā saṃvutindriyā 
  
      Bahussutā dhammadharā dhammatthaparipucchikā 
 Uggahetā ca dhammānaṃ sotā payirupāsikā 
  
      Desenti janamajjhehaṃ ahosiṃ jinasāsane 
 Bāhusaccena tenāhaṃ pesalā atimaññisaṃ 
  
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni sāvatthiyaṃ puruttame 
 Anāthapiṇḍino gehe jātāhaṃ kumbhadāsiyā 
  
      Gatā udakahārikaṃ sotthiyaṃ dijamaddasaṃ 
 Sitaṭṭaṃ toyamajjhambhi taṃ disvā idamabraviṃ 
                   
      Udahāri ahaṃ site sadā udakamotariṃ 
 Ayyānaṃ daṇḍabhayabhitā vācādosabhayaṭṭitā 
  
      Kassa brāhmaṇa tvaṃ hito sadā udakamotari 
 Vedhamānahi gattehi sītaṃ vedayase bhusaṃ 
  
      Jānanti vata maṃ bhoti puṇṇike paripucchasi 
 Karontataṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ rundhantaṃ katapāpakaṃ 
  
      Yo vuḍḍho daharo vāpi pāpakammaṃ pakubbati 
 Dakāhisiñcanā bhoti pāpakammā pamuccati 
  
      Uttarantassa akkhāsiṃ dhammatthasaṃhitaṃ padaṃ 
 Taṃ ca ñatvā sa saṃviggo pabbajitvārahā ahu 
  
      Purenti ūnakasataṃ jātā dāsikule yato 
 Tato puṇṇāti nāmaṃ me bhujissaṃ maṃ akaṃsute 
  
      Seṭṭhiṃ tatonumodetvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Na cireneva kālena arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
                   
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra uppannaṃ tava santike 
  
      Bhāvanāya mahāpaññā sutena ca sutāvini 
 Mānena nicakulajā na hi kammaṃ vinassati 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ puṇṇā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Puṇṇātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
                   
     Ambapālī apadānaṃ 
      Yo raṃsiphusitāvelo phusso nāma mahāmuni 
 Tassāhaṃ bhagini āsiṃ ajāyiṃ khattiye kule 
  
      Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ vippasannena cetasā 
 Mahādānaṃ daditvāna patthayiṃ rūpasampadaṃ 
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe sikhi lokagganāyako 
 Uppajji lokapajoto tilokasaraṇo jito 
  
      Tadāruṇupare ramme brahmaññakulasambhavā 
 Vimuttacittaṃ kupitā bhikkhunīṃ abhisāpayiṃ 
  
       Cesikāva anācārā jinasāsanadusikā  
 Evaṃ akkosaṭitvāna tena pāpena kammunā 
  
      Dāruṇaṃ nirayaṃ gantvā mahādukkhasamapajitā 
 Tato cutā manussesu upapannā tapassini 
  
      Dasajātisahassāni gaṇikattamakārayiṃ 
 Tambhā pāpā na muccissaṃ bhutvā duṭṭhavisaṃ yathā 
  
                   
      Brahmacariyamasevissaṃ kassape jina sāsane 
 Tena kammavipākena ajāyiṃ tidase pure 
  
      Pacchimabhave sampatte ahosiṃ opapatikā 
 Ambasākhantare jātā ambapāliti tena haṃ 
  
      Parivutā pāṇakoṭihi pabbajiṃ jinasāsane 
 Pattāhaṃ acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ ṭhitā buddhassa orasā 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmuni 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā 
                   
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
  
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ ambapāli bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ambapālitheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
      Pesalāpadānaṃ 
      Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhumahāyaso 
 Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo 
  
      Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare upāsakakule ahaṃ 
 Pasutā taṃ jinavaraṃ disvā sutvā ca desanaṃ 
  
      Taṃ viraṃ saraṇaṃ gantvā silāni ca samādiyiṃ 
 Kadāci so mahāvīro mahājanasamāgame 
  
      Antano abhisambodhiṃ pakāsesi narāsabho 
  Ananussutesu dhammesu pubbe dukkhādikesu ca 
  
      Cakkhu ñāṇaṃ ca paññā ca vijjāloko ca āsi me  
 Taṃ sutvā uggahetvāna paripucchiṃ ca bhikkhavo 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
      Pacchime ca bhavedāni jātā seṭṭhimahākule 
 Upecca buddhaṃ saddhammaṃ sutvā saccupasaṃhitaṃ 
  
                   
      Pabbajitvā cireneva saccatthāni vicintayaṃ 
 Khepetvā āsave sabbe arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Iddhisu ca vasi homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā 
 Cetopariyañāṇassa vasi homi mahāmune 
  
      Pubbe nivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ 
 Sabbāsavā parikkhiṇā natthidāni punabbhavo 
  
      Atthadhammaniruttisu paṭibhāne tatheva ca 
 Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā 
  
      Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgiva bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavā 
                   
      Svāgataṃ vata me āsi mama buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ pesalā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pesalātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Khattiyāvaggo catuttho 
  
 Tatthuddānaṃ 
 Khattiyā brāhmaṇi ceva tathā uppaladāyikā 
 Sigālamātā sukkā ca abhirūpā aḍḍhakāsikā 
  
 Suṇṇā ca ambapāli ca pesalāti ca tā dasa 
 Gāthāyo dvisatānettha dvicattālisa cuttari 
  
 Atha vagguddānaṃ 
 Sumedhā ekuposathā kuṇḍalakesi khattiyā 
 Sahassaṃ tisatā gāthā sattatālisa piṇḍitā 
 Saha uddānagāthāhi gaṇitāyo vibhāvihi 
 Sahassaṃ tisatā gāthā sattapaññāsameva cāti 
  
 Theriapadānaṃ samattaṃ 
 Samattā apadānapāḷi
